O vos, tres chiers filz, je vos ai acomplit cest livre qui est li derriens de la science de medicine ensamble l’emplissement de lui, et ai fait la fin per ses expositions et par ses declarations.	Oh you, very cherished sons, I have completed this book which is the conclusion of the science of medicine, and filled it with its contents, and I have finished it by its explanations and by its declarations.
Et m’est venu en vision que je le vos acomplisse avec cest traitier, qui est partie de l’uevre de mains, c’est a savoir «cyrurgie».	And it came to me in a vision that I should complete it with this treatise, which is part of the work of hands, that is to say "surgery".
Et por ceu que l’uevre de mains est fortraite en nostre region et est etraingie dou tout en tout, si est perie li science et decopee, et n’est riens demorez de li fuers que les petites descriptions en livres des anciens que les mains ont muees.	And because the work of hands is fortified in our region and is extinguished from all to all, so it has perished the science and has been lost, and nothing remains but the small descriptions in books of the ancients that the hands have moved.
Et de ceu est venue li error et li vanitez, et sont closes les ententions et est aloignie li science.	And from this comes the error and the futility, and the minds are closed and the knowledge is distant.
Or me semble que je la vuel vivifier ensamble l’ordination de cest traitier selonc la voie d’exposition et de declaration et de l’abreviation;	It seems to me that I can revive it along with the order of this treatment according to the way of exposure and declaration and abbreviation;
et venrai ensamble les formes des ferremens de cautere, et des autres estrumens de l’uevre avec l’ajostement de la declaration et de preparation de li, sicom il est mestier.	and I will bring along the forms of the irons of cauterization, and other instruments of the work with the addition of declaration and preparation of it, as it is necessary.
Et por la raison de ceu que nuls boins maistres de mains n’est trovez en nostre tens, est li ars de medicine eslongié.	Because for the reason that no good master of hands is found in our time, the art of medicine is lengthened.
Et covient celui qui s’en entremet sormonter en la science d’anathomie, si com Galiens dit, tant qu’il saiche la juement des menbres, et les formes et les conjunctions et les separations d’aus, et aient connissance des osses et des nerf et des brais et le nombre d’ous, et le demenement et des voines movans et des reposans, et dou leu de lor issue.	And it is necessary for him who enters into this to surpass in the science of anatomy, as Galen says, until he knows the judgment of the limbs, and their forms and conjunctions and separations of them, and has knowledge of the bones and nerves and sinews and the number of joints, and the movement of the veins moving and resting, and the source of their issue.
Et por ceu dist Ypocras que li nons avec le non est mout, et avec l’uevre est poc;	And because, as Hippocrates says, we are not with the non-living, and with the work is little.
et meismement en l’art de main.	and even in the art of hand.
Nos vos disons en l’introite de cest livre que qui n’est conissans des choses devant dites, si se gart qu’il ne chiece en error et qu’il n’ocie les homes;	We tell you in the introduction of this book that those who are not familiar with the things mentioned before, so that they may not err and cause harm to men.
ensi que j’ai veut maintes fois plusors de ces qui s’entremettent de ceste science et si s’abandonent sen science et sens experiment.	such that I have wanted many times to test these who interfere with this science and if they abandon themselves to ignorance and lack of experience.
Car je vis un fol mire qui copa I apostume de scrophules ou col d’une femme, et copa les arteres dou col;	For I saw a foolish one who cut into an abscess of the neck or the breast of a woman, and cut the arteries of the breast;
por coi tant de sanc issit hors que li femme cheit morte entre ses mains.	which caused so much blood to issue out that the woman died in her hands.
Et vis I autre mire qui traït une piere d’un home d’eaige, et li piere estoit grans;	And I saw another foolish one who removed a stone from an old man's eye, and the stone was large;
si emporta avec li une piece de la vessie, et fut mors li hons dedens III jors.	and took with it a piece of the bladder, and died within three days.
Et je i avoie ja esteit apelez por lou traire, et vis la disposition dou malaide et la grandor de la piere, et soi bien s’on lou tailloit il en morroit.	And I had already been called for the extraction, and saw the position of the misalignment and the size of the stone, and it was clear that if they cut it, it would die.
Et vis I autre mire qui prist en cure I duc de nostre terre qui avoit la jambe brisie, et avec la briseure ot plaie;	And another mirror who took in care the duke of our land who had the leg broken, and with the breaker got the wound;
et li mires plains d’ignorance estraint la brisure sus la plaie as esteles par fort lieure, et ne lassa a la plaie point de xalain, et le lassa ensi I termine;	and the mirror pressed the break over the wound with great force, and did not leave any salve on the wound, and thus left it to the end;
et li comanda qu’il ne la desliast mie;	and he ordered that it not be moved little;
et demora ensi que li jambe fut toute enflee et li piez et vint a perdition.	and thus waited until the leg was completely rotten and the feet and came to destruction.
Je fuis apelez por venir a lui, et me hastai por venir deslier la jambe;	I was called to come to him, and I hurried to remove the leg;
et quant je l’oi desloie si fut em pais et ne sentit point de dolor.	and when I saw it removed so was in the field and did not feel any pain.
Mais toute voie li corruptions estoit ja confermee ou membre, et ne la poi saner;	But all ways of healing the corruption were already confirmed or the member, and it could not be healed.
et ne cessa li corrution d’aler par le membre tant que li membres fut dou tout perdus.	And the corruption did not cease to spread through the member until the member was completely lost.
Et vis I autre mire qui effondra I apostume enchancreit, et puis enflama per le malice de sa signorie.	And I saw another method that would crush the abscess and make it worse, and then it would inflame due to the evil of its lordship.
Car chancre, quant il est purs d’umor melancolique, ne covient mie qu’on i(l) touche de fer s’il n’est en teil leu c’on puisse toute oster ce que est corrumpus.	For an abscess, when it is free of melancholic humor, it only needs that one touch with iron if it is not in a place where one can completely remove everything that is corrupt.
Et por ceu, treschier filz, vos est besoig que vos sachiez que oevre de mains est devisee en II divisions:	Therefore, dear son, you must know that the work of hands is divided into two parts:
c’est asavoir, huevre ou il a peril en plusors dispositions;	That is to say, the first part where he has placed in many positions;
et je mostrerai en chescun leu de cest livre ou il a paour et peril.	and I will show in each chapter of this book where he has fear and danger.
Por coi il est besoig que vos vos en gardez, si que li fol mire ne puissent mal parler de vos.	Therefore, it is important that you keep this, so that the evil people cannot harm you.
Si prenez vos armes en cusenson, et entreprenez vos malaides legierement et fermement, et usez de la millor voie si que per la graice de Deu vos venez a salut et soiez loez;	If you take your arms in a firm and steady manner, and use the best way possible, then by the grace of God, you will come to safety and be healed.
et lassiez les maladies espoantables de grief saniteit;	And let the contagious diseases spread no further harm;
et ostez vos armes de ceu que vos fait douter, et aiez foit en vos si que vos puissiez venir de cestui monde a l’autre de gloire.	And take your arms away from what causes you doubt, and be in such a state that you can come from this world to the other of glory.
Galiens dist en aucuns de ses amonestemens:	Galenus says in some of his admonitions:
«Ne prenez mie en cure male maladie, que vos ne soiez apelez fol mire.	«Do not take up the care of a seriously ill patient unless you are called a foolish one.»
» J’ai deviseit cest traitier selonc III chapitres.	I have divided this treatment into three chapters.
Li premiers chapitres est des cauteres de feu et dé cauteres de medicine ague, et est li chapitres ordenez de lou chief jusques as piez;	The first chapters are about fire cauteries and medical cautery, and the chapters are ordered from the head to the feet.
et des formes des estrumens, et des ferremens de cautere, et de tout ceu qui est necessaire en l’ueuvre.	and the forms of instruments, and the cauterizing irons, and of all that is necessary in the work.
Li secons chapitres si est de taillier et de percier, et des ventouses et des plaies, et des estractions des saiettes, et des semblans choses;	The second chapters are about cutting and piercing, and wounds, and the extraction of arrows, and similar things.
et est li chapitres ordenez et les formes des estrumens.	and the chapters are ordered and the forms of instruments.
Li tiers chapitres est de restorer les dislocations et des torcions, et des semblans choses;	The third chapters are about restoring dislocations and twists, and similar things.
et est ordeneiz des lou chief jusc’as piez, et des formes des estrumens.	and is ordered by the high chief just as the feet, and the forms of instruments.
Ainsois que nos nos remembriens de l’uevre, il covient que je die la qualiteit de l’aide et dou nuisement de chescune complexion.	As we recall the work, it is necessary that I mention the quality of aid and the new harm from each condition.
Je dis que li qualiteis de l’aide, et dou nuisement, est li plus longe parole et subtilz science et li secrez reponus;	I say that the qualities of aid and harm are the longest spoken and most subtle science and the secrets kept;
et de ceu parlerent li plusors des saiges, et s’acorderent a ceu;	and many wise men have spoken of this, and agreed to it;
et me soffisent poc lor paroles, car je redous la longesce.	but I shorten the words little by little, because I reduce the length.
Je dis que cautere aide universement a toute complexion ou il a matiere, fuer que II complexions:	I say that fire cauterization helps universally in all matters where there is matter, whether the matter:
c’est a savoir complexion chaude sens matere, et complexion seche sens matere.	is to know whether the matter is hot without matter, and dry without matter.
En complexion chaude et seche ensamble matiere, deviserent aucun et dirent que cautere i est grans aide;	In hot and dry weather together with the matter, they devised any and said that fire cauterization is great help;
et li autre dirent le contraire:	and the others said the opposite:
que cautere ne vaut a maladie que vient de chalor et de sechour.	that fire cauterization is not good for disease that comes from heat and dryness.
Car li nature dou feu si est chaude, et ne doit mie estre cureiz de chaude maladie par chalor, ne per sechour;	For the nature of fire is hot, and should not be cured by heat or dryness;
et dist cil qui dist lou contraire que cautere fait grant aide a maladie chaude et seche que vient en cors des homes.	and those who said the opposite claimed that fire cauterization does great help to hot and dry disease that comes from people.
Car quant tu comperes le cors de l’ome et sa moistor a la complexion dou feu, tu trueves le cors froit.	For when you compare the body of the man and its moisture to the hot fire, you heat the body.
Et je m’acorde a ceste parole.	And I agree with this word.
Car je l’ai troveit aucune fois per experiment.	For I have found it once by experience.
Et toute voie, ne s’en entremette mie fuers que cil qui l’a esproveit, et qui conoit par lonc usaige le chapistre des cauteres, et la diversiteit des complexions des homes, et les dispositions et les causes de lor maladies, et les sorvenues et l’espaice dou tens;	And in all cases, one should not interfere except those who have experienced it, and who know by long use the chapter of cauterization, and the diversity of the complexions of people, and their dispositions and causes of their diseases, and the symptoms and the space of time;
des autres complexions n’avons nos mie paour, meismement em maladies froides et moistes.	We have no fear of other constitutions, even in diseases that are cold and moist.
Et tuit li mire s’asemblerent et s’acorderent au cautere.	And all the symptoms gathered and agreed to the cauterization.
Et sachiez, filz, que cautere ensamble feu si est des secrez des cures, et de plus grant bonteit que cautere de medicine ardant.	And know, sons, that cauterization with fire is one of the secrets of cures, and has greater goodness than cauterization with burning medicine.
Car li feus est simples, et ne vient mie fuers que au membre qui est cuis, et ne nuit a autre membre se poc nom.	For the fever is simple, and comes only to the member that is cooked, and does not harm other members unless it has a name.
Les medicines ardans vienent de membre a autre en aloignant, et font venir au membre maladies de grief sanation;	The burning remedies come from one member to another by separating them, and bring diseases of difficult healing to the affected member.
et par aventure ocit lou malaide.	And perhaps it finds the pain.
Li feus por sa hautece et por la bonteit de sa substance ne fait mie ceu, s’il n’i a superfluiteit.	The food for its height and for the goodness of its substance does not make it sick, if there is no excess.
Et ceu vos ai je troveit par experiment et par la longesce dou servise et de l’estude que j’ai mis en l’art, et esteit sus la verteit des choses;	And I have found this by experience and by the length of service and study that I have put into the art, and it is above the truth of things.
et por ceu je m’escuse de la longesce de la parole, car il ne me plait mie que je vos oste le secreit qui est reponus ou feu, et la qualiteit de l’uevre, coment il deboute les maladies des cors, si com li philosophe le dit en demostrant;	And because I excuse myself from the length of speech, for I only like to give you the secret that is hidden or by fire, and the quality of the work, how it drives away diseases of the body, as the philosopher says in demonstrating.
or le recevez en vos pensees.	receive in your thoughts.
Et sachiez, fil, que il s’acorderent en quel tens doient estre faites les cauteres, et eslirent prientens.	And know, my son, that they should be made in what degree the cautery should be done, and ask for permission.
Et je dis que cautere est covenable en tous tens, por ceu que li nuisemens sorvenans est desoz mis par l’aide dou cautere;	And I say that cauterization is beneficial in all cases, because the evils that come from it are removed by the help of cauterization;
et meismement se li cauteres est por dolors necessaires fors et hastans que ne puent atendre le tens que plus grans malice ne veigne au membre.	and indeed if it is for necessary pain, short and not able to wait until the greatest evil comes to the limb.
Et n’i pensez onques, chier fil, si com font li fol mire;	And do not think like a fool, child;
car a la maladie qui est sanee par cautere n’a point de revenue;	for the disease that is healed by cauterization has no return;
et il le dient ensi;	and it says so thus;
mais il n’est mie si com il cuident, por ce que cauteres nen est que medicine qui mue la complexion, et seche les humors que sont cause de la dolor, et vaut mues que medicine por le hastement de sa valor, et por la vertut de son oevre et de sa signorie.	but it is not as they think, because cauterization is only a medicine that moves the complexion, and dries the humors that are the cause of pain, and is more valuable than any other medicine for its swiftness of action, and by the power of its work and its authority.
Et possans chose est que li maladie viegne aucune fois selonc la complexion dou malaide et lou leu de la maladie et sa vertut;	And it is a matter of fact that the sickness comes at no certain time according to the nature of the body and the part of the disease and its power;
et sont assemblees en lui les superfluitez par l’aquisition des viandes et des semblans choses, se ce n’est cauteres administrez em leu ou il ait poc de superfluitez et de moistor, si com cauteres de dens por la dolor, et les semblans choses, et teil dolor ne revient mie;	and there are gathered in him the superfluities by the acquisition of meats and similar things, unless if cauteries are administered in the place where he has little superfluity and moisture, as cauteries of dense por la dolor, and similar things, and the pain does not return much;
mais ce avient poc.	but this happens little.
Et mout de gens n’entendent mie por coi cauteres est apelez li derriens de medecine, et c’est voir;	and many people do not understand why cauteries are called the back of medicine, and that is to see;
mais il ne croient mie que cauteres vaille aprés medicine, mais lor ententions est fause, et est cauteres li derriens de medicine por ceu que quant nos aministrons manieres de cures en aucune maladie et elles ne valent, adonc administrons nos le cautere, et il vaut.	but they do not believe that the fire cauteries are effective after medicine, but rather their intentions are false, and they use fire cauteries at the end of medicine because when we administer methods of healing in any disease and they do not work, then we administer the fire cauteries, and it is worth it.
Adonques apert bien que cauteres est li derriens de medicine, ne mie selonc l’entention des folz mires.	Therefore, it is necessary to carefully use cautery as a last resort in medicine, not according to the intention of those who are misguided.
Li ancien dirent que cauteres d’estrument d’or est muedres que de fer, et ne dirent ceu fuers que por la qualiteit de l’or et por la hautece de sa substance;	The ancients said that gold cauteries are more effective than iron ones, and they did not say why except for the quality of gold and its high value;
et dirent que li leus de cautere ne fait mie porriture, mais ceu n’est mie voir car je l’ai esprovei, et ai troveit que c’est voir en aucuns homes;	and they said that the points of the cauteries do not cause putrefaction, but it is not to see because I have experienced it, and I have found that it is so in some men;
et cauteres d’or vaut mues que de fer, si com il lou dirent.	And gold cautery is better than iron, as they say.
Et toutevoie quant tu chaufes estrument d’or, tu ne seis mie quant il est chaus par la color de l’or, et s’est tantost refroidiez;	And whenever you heat a gold instrument, do not hold it when it is hot because of the color of gold, and it has cooled slightly;
et s’on le chaufe trop;	and if it is heated too much.
si font au feu;	then they do at the fire.
et ensi i a assez d’empechement.	and thus there is enough prevention.
Et por ce usons nos de cautere de feir que nos l’avons mues apparilliet a nostre oevre.	And for this reason, we use fire cauterization that we have armed ourselves with for our work.
Or vos ai ordeneit cest chapitre des lou chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que li voie soit plus legiere a trover.	Or I would order this chapter on the shoulder joints from the feet, because it is easier to find there.
dou cautere olivaire	The fire cauterization
Cist cauteres vaut a moistor et a froidor sus lou cerveil, et en i a dous c’on fait par la cause d’une maladie qui est apelee «soda», et par la cause de maintes humors qui dessendent dou chief as eulz, et as oreilles, et por multitude de songes et dolor de dens et dolor de gorge, et meismement a toutes maladies qui vienent de froidor si com paralisie et sode et apoplexie et semblans maladies.	This fire cauterization is used for moisture and cold on the head, and it is done because of a disease called "soda", and because of many humors that descend from the joint to the eyes, and to the ears, and due to many dreams and tooth pain, and throat pain, and also for all diseases that come from cold, such as paralysis, soda, apoplexy, and similar diseases.
Li forme de cest cautere si est que li malaides soit espurgiez par medicine solutive mondifiant le chief III nuis ou IIII, selonc ceu que li vertus et li eaige et li acostumance dou malaide le puet soffrir;	The form of this cautery is that the hairs should be removed by solvent medicine changing the head III or IV times, depending on the virtues and age and custom of the hair that it can suffer;
et puis fai rere lou chief dou malaide.	and then make the head of the shoulder right again.
Et puis le fai seoir croisiet entre tes mains, et mettre ses mains sor som peis;	And then let him sit cross-legged between your hands, and put his hands on top of yours;
aprés met la racine de ta palme sus la racine de son neis entre ses II eulz;	after place the root of your palm above the root of his finger between his two fingers;
et lai ou venra tes dois moiens, si saigne d’enche puis eschaufe le cautere qui est apelé «olivare», de coi ci est li forme:	and let your middle fingers come out, if he bleeds from the wound then heat the cauterizing agent called "olive oil", of which this is the form:
Et le met sor le leu signiet d’encre, et fai en dessendant et en estraignant ta main poc et poc en trestornant;	And put it on the wound with a feather, and move your hand slowly and steadily in returning;
puis lieve ta main isnelement, et rewarde le leu se tu vois l’os I sol petit;	then lift your hand slowly, and reward the wound if you see the small bone of the forearm;
et se tu ne lou vois, si rencomence le cautere tant que tu voies l’os si com je lou t’ai dit;	and if you do not see it, restart the cauterization until you see the bone as I have told you.
aprés pren I poc de seil, et met en awe et molle coton dedens, et met sor le leu, et li laisse III jors;	then take some thread, and put it in warm water and soft cotton inside, and put it on the limb, and leave it for three hours.
aprés met sus cotun moilliet en burre;	then put on a soft bandage in butter.
et laisse sus tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	and leave it on until the burn is healed.
aprés cure la plaie de l’oignement qui est apelez «tetrafarmaçon», tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat the wound with the ointment called "tetra-farmaçon" until it is healed.
Et se dirent li ancien, que quant plus demoure overte li plaie, plus s’espurge;	And the old ones said that the longer the wound remains open, the more it purges.
et por ce si aide mues.	and therefore to help them.
Et dirent aucun de ces que on doit tant lassier le cautere que partie de l’os soit arse, et puis rese on ceu qui est ars de l’os, et soit curez.	And none of these said that one should burn the cauterizer so much that a part of the bone is burned away, and then remove what has been burned off from the bone, and treat it.
Et dient li autre c’on doit le cautere tant lassier sus, et bouter si fort c’on abaite de l’os ausi large comme I vertoil que les femmes mettent en lor fusez por ceu que les humors issent mues hors;	And they should apply the fire cauterizer as much more gently, and push it in as far as possible to break the bone as wide as a spoon that women put in their hair for the reason that the humors are pushed out moist.
et doit on lassier la plaie longement overte;	and one should leave the wound open long.
aprés le doit on curer et sodeir.	After that, one should cure and bandage it.
Et ces II manieres de cauteres ne me semblent mie estre bones dou tout en tout, fuers qu’en aucuns homes ou il ait voie de paor;	And these two methods of cauterization do not seem to be good for everyone at all times, unless in some men where there is a view of fear.
et mues me semble que je lou doie laissier;	And it seems to me that I should leave it.
car li chiés li est afoiblis par les solutions continuees de nature, si com nos le tesmoignons ens autres membres;	because the bones are weakened by continuous natural solutions, as we testify in other members;
et meisme quant li chiés dou malaide est foibles par nature, et li premiere semblance de cautere est plus salve et muedre por moi, et de celi use je oevre en donques emsamble salut.	and even when the affected bone is weak by nature, and the first appearance of cauterization is safer and less painful for me, and from this I work in consequence with a similar method to achieve health.
de l’anciainne dolor dou chief	of the ancient pain of the main
Quant en tout le chief vient dolor croniques, et dure longement, si doit user li malaides yeris et pilules qui sont apelees «cochie», et d’espurgement de chief et d’oiles et d’emplastres;	When the main cause of chronic pain and lasts for a long time, one should use the years and pills called "cochie", and head cleaning and eye and plasters;
et s’on li fait le cautere que nos avons devant dit, et il ne vaut.	and if one does the cauterization that we have previously mentioned, and it is not effective.
Pren warde se li chiés dou malade est de fort nature, et qu’il ne soit trop froit;	Take care when dealing with a patient who has a severe illness, and do not make them too cold.
adonques le cauterize desoz celui cautere un poc que nos avons dit desus.	Therefore, use the fire cautery to treat it as we have mentioned above.
Aprés fai cautere sus chescune corne dou chief jusc’a l’os, si com devant avons dit, et fai I cautere ou leu qui est apelez «vasselz»;	After applying the fire cautery to each horn of the skull to the bone, as we have mentioned before, and apply the "vasselz" cautery where it is needed.
et est I leus en coi on met ventouses;	and place suction cups there.
et alige ta main si que tu ne voises mie jusc’a l’os:	and keep your hand steady so you do not press too hard against the bone:
li malaides sent trop plus grant dolor en cest cautere que as autres, et je em parlerai aillors;	The hairs feel much greater pain in this cautery than in others, and I will speak of that later.
et covient que li cauteres des cornes soient plus subtis que cil dont on cautere la moieneteit dou chief, et c’est li forme:	and it is necessary that the cautery of the horns be more subtle than that which is used to cauterize the middle of the head, and this is the form:
dou cautere dou chief	For the fire cautery
Quant en une partie dou chief vient dolor sodaine, et est estendue li maladie jusc’a l’oil, et li chiés est espurgiez par medicines mondifians, et on a fait les autres cures que j’ai dit en la division des maladies, et tout ceu ne profite mie:	When in one part of the head there is sudden pain, and the illness has spread to the oil, and the patient is purged by medicines that are not effective, and the other treatments that I have mentioned in the division of diseases have been done, and all this does not help:
adonques li fai cauteres selonc II manieres, c’est a savoir de medicine ague et de feir.	therefore, the cautery is done in two ways, that is to say, by medicine and by fire.
Li cauteres de medicine ague si est que tu preignes une doce d’alz, et oste l’escorce et le recope I poc as II chiés, et puis fent la temple ou li dolor tient en teil maniere que tu puisses reponre la doce d’alz desoz le cuir;	The cautery by medicine is such that you hold a sharp instrument and remove the scab and the skin, and then make the temple or where the pain is located in some way so that you can replace the sharp instrument outside the skin;
et quant elle sera reponuee si le lie et l’estraint bien et le laisse ensi XII houres;	And when it is reset, if the joint and the constraint are well done, let it rest for twelve hours.
et puis le deslie et trait fuers la doce d’ail, et laisse la plaie ensi II jors ou III;	Then release and treat further with a poultice of garlic, and leave the wound thus for two or three days.
puis met sus cotun plongiet en burre tant que porreture en isse.	Then place a cast on it soaked in butter until it becomes firm.
Aprés le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	After the treatment of the wound, until it is healed.
et se tu vues si fai ceu d’aucunes medicines comburans que j’ai escrites ou dozime traitier des medicines comburans.	And if you see that some burning remedies that I have written or advised for treating burns, are causing harm.
Li cautere de fer si est selonc ceste meniere.	The fire cautery is done in this way.
Chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	Heat the fire cautery with this shape:
Et est apelez «clos» por ceu que li chief est fait a la forme d’un clo ou il ait I poc de corbeure, et em mileu a une petite apparance;	And it is called "closed" because the main part is made in the shape of a clot or it has a little beak, and in the middle has a small appearance.
et le met sor le leu dolorous, et tien ta main et trestorne le feir un poc legierement, tant que li moitiez de l’espés dou keur soit arse;	and place it on the painful joint, and hold your hand and gently press the bone slightly, until half of the bone's width is exposed.
et lieve ta main que li artere n’arde, que est defuers, et decorre habundance de sanc.	and gently press your hand so that the artery does not burn, which is below, and there is abundant blood flow.
Aprés met coton en awe de seil, et met sor le leu par III jors;	After placing gauze on a string, and place it on the joint for three days;
puis i met coton moilliet em burre, et puis cure le leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	then apply wet gauze, and then treat the joint with oil until it is healed;
et se tu vuelz cauterize ceste emigraine avec le cautere qui est apelez «cultellare», a tout la pointe, et te garde de coper l’artere en ceste emigraine qui n’est mie anciaine.	and if you want to cauterize this wound with the cauterizing iron called "cultellare", at all points, and be careful not to cover the artery in this wound which is not ancient.
de emigraine	of the wound
Quant tu cures emigraine si com nos avons devant dit en divisions des maladies, et ne profite mie, et vois que li cauteres devant dis de la medicine et dou fer ne li soffit mie, adonques covient il que tu eschaufes le cautere qui est apelez «cultellare» tant qu’il soit blans;	When you treat migraine as we have previously described in the divisions of diseases, and it does not improve, and you see that the fire before mentioned from medicine and iron does not suffice to alleviate the pain, then it is necessary that you extinguish the knife which is called "cultellare" until it is white.
et seigne ainsois sor le leu doillant une ligne de demi doi de lonc, et oste ta main une fois, et l’estrain que tu ne coper l’artere et que ne viegnes jusc’a l’os;	and let it rest on the painful limb for a line of half a finger's length, and take your hand once, and strain so that you do not cover the artery and that it does not come close to the bone;
et te warde de la mandibule que muet quant on menjut, et li ners n’ait regart que la muet et que spasmus ne veigne a malaide, et te warde de decorrement de sanc de l’artere quant elle sera copee, ou copement ait grant paour et meismement a celui que ne s’i conoit, et qui n’est estudians et esprovez;	and guard the jaw that moves when bent, and the nerves should only regard the moving part and that spasm should not cause pain, and guard against the escape of blood from the artery when it is cut, or cutting at a great risk and immediately to those who do not know, and which are not studied and experienced;
et laisse l’uevre em mi voie;	and leave the work in the middle way;
mais je vos dirai coment on restainche sanc quant li artere est copee, et je vos mostrerai a leu ou il afiert en cest livre.	but I will tell you how to stop the blood when the artery is cut, and I will show you where it appears in this book.
Et se tu vois que cist cauteres ne soffise mie a la maladie, et li malaides est soffrans, cauterize le enmi le chief ausi com nos avons dit, et cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit sanee;	And if you see that this cauterization does not suffice for the disease, and the wounds are painful, cauterize it with the head as we have said, and treat the wound until it is healed;
et se tu vues, aministre le cautere que nos avons dit ou chapistre de l’estraction de l’artere, avec le cautere qui ait II coutelz;	and if you see, administer the cauterization that we have said or chapter of the extraction of the artery, with the cauterizer that has two blades;
et est cist cauteres millors de celui et plus aidans.	and this fire cauterization is better than the other and more helpful.
de la dolor des oreilles de part froidor	of the pain in the ears from cold
Quant en l’oreille vient dolor de froit, et on i a ovreit de medicines solutives et des autres cures que nos avons dit en la division, et li dolors ne se muet, adonques eschaufe cest cautere qui est apelez «poins», de coi ci est li forme:	When pain in the ear comes from cold, and medicines have been administered and other treatments that we have said in the division, and the pain does not move, then heat this cautery which is called "poins", of which this is the form:
Aprés pointoie tout entor l’oreille malaide, ou entor les II se la dolor tient en ambedous, et t’esloigne un poc ensus de la racine de l’oreille puis que tu as signiet le leu d’enche;	After poking all around the ear pain, or both where the pain is felt, and push it slightly away from the root of the ear, then you have identified the joint.
et ait X poins entor chescune oreille;	and have ten points around each ear.
aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	after curing the joint until it is healed.
de la torture de la bouche	of the mouth torture
Torture qui doit estre curee par cautere nen est fuers que de celles que muevent de fleume, si com nos avons dit en divisions des maladie;	The torture that should be cured by cauterization is no more than those that move the stream, as we have said in the division of diseases.
et ne faire point de cautere as semblances que vienent de sechor et de spame de ners.	and do not use cauterization like those that come from blisters and sweat of the flesh.
Quant tu cures ceste semblance de torture qui muet de fleume d’ydres et d’espurgemens de chief et de gargarisme, et ceu ne vaut, adonc covient que tu cauterizes le malaide de III cauteres:	When you encounter this appearance of torture that moves from a stream of urine and spitting out of the mouth and choking, and it does not cease, then it is necessary to cauterize the pain with three cauteries.
l’une en la racine de l’oreille, et l’autre un poc defuers la temple, et le tier en l’ajostement des II levres;	One at the root of the ear, and the other slightly behind the temple, and the third in the junction of the two lips.
et met le cautere en la partie qui apert saine, et li fai cautere endroit le chief de l’oreille desus un poc desoz la corne dou chief, et un autre en la temple ausi longe com uns poce;	And place the cauteries in the part that opens healthily, and make the cauteries in the part above a little behind the ear, and another in the temple as long as a little finger.
et laisse le cautere tant sus que li moitiez dou keur soit arse;	and let the cauterization extend as far up as half of the wound is exposed;
et c’est li forme dou cautere:	and this is the shape of the cauterization:
Et est li semblance dou cutellaire que nos avons mise devant, mais il est un poc plus subtilz et covient que li coutelz soit un poc plus gros;	And it is the similar shape of the cauterizing knife that we have placed before, but it is a bit more delicate and it should be a bit bigger;
aprés cure lou leu si com j’ai devant dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	after curing the limb as I have previously said, until it is healed.
Quant apoplexie est ancieinne et tu la cures ensi com nos avons dit, et il ne profite mie, et li malaides n’ait fievre, adonques li fai IIII cauteres:	When apoplexy is old and you treat it as we have said, and it does not improve, and the pain does not have fever, then do four cauterizations:
II sus les II cornes dou chief, et I emmi le chief, et I ou leu qui est apelez «vasselz» si com nos avons devant dit, et lou derrien cautere sus la bouche de l’estomac;	II above the II horns of the head, and I press the head, and I place the one which is called «vasselz» as we have already said, and behind the fire cauterizes above the mouth of the stomach;
et soit curez si com nos avons dit devant.	and so treat it as we have said before.
de litargie	of laziness
A cest maladie covient doner au malaide yeres grans et pilules mondifians le cerveil;	For this disease, one should give the patient large and modified brain pills;
aprés reis lou chief dou malaide tout, et li met sus l’occipite l’emplaustre de sinapi qui est escrit ou traitier des emplastres;	after rubbing the entire head of the patient with the mustard plaster which is written or treated in plasters;
et c’est li maniere dou cautere:	and this is the way of the fire cauterization:
si lou fai si com j’ai dit.	if you do as I have said.
S’il est sanez ensi, boin est;	If he is thus healthy, good.
et s’il ne l’est, se li fai III cauteres des emmi le chief en dessendant jusc’a col, et ait d’espaice entre chescun cautere I doi de gros;	And if he is not, then make three cauterizations on the head by descending along the neck, and let there be space between each cautery of one large span;
et le cure si com les autres, et se tu i vues ajoster, et li malaides est soffrans, se li fai I cautere en mileu;	and treat him as with the others, and if you see that he is stiff, and the pains are severe, then make one cauterization in the middle;
et se mestiers est, II autres sus les II cornes, et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	and if he is a laborer, two more on the two horns, and treat him until he is healthy.
et soit li cauteres qui est apelez «olivare», si com j’ai devant dit.	And let the cauterizations be called "olivare", as I have previously mentioned.
de la froidor dou chief	of the cold from the head
Il covient que li chief soit mundifiez de yeres et de ceu que nos avons devant dit;	It is necessary that the head be cleaned of years and the flesh that we have previously mentioned.
aprés reis le chief dou malaide, puis li fai cautere emmi le chief et sus chescune corne, et I derrier et III sus l’espinee dou col;	After removing the bad flesh, then perform cauterization on the head and each horn, and at the back and three times above the spine of the neck.
et se tu en as plus mestier, et li cors est moiste et li malaides est soffrans, et li maladie est fors, se li fai IIII cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos;	If you have more skill, and the body is wet and the bad flesh is suffering, and the disease is far, then perform four cauterizations above the spine of the back.
et li laisse tant que li plus dou keur soit ars, et lieve ta main;	And let it rest until the most skilled is satisfied, and release your hand.
aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez, et soit li cauteres qui est apelez «olivare» que nos avons devant dit.	After the treatment until they are healed, and the cauterizations called "olivare" that we have previously mentioned.
de l’epilempsie	Of epilepsy
Li epilentiques ne doit useir de cautere fuers que cil qui est fleumatique, et covient premier mondifier le cerveil de yeres et d’autres cures que nos avons dites en la division quant li malaides est grans et soffrans de penre medicine.	The epileptics should not use cauterization except for those that are bleeding, and it is first necessary to modify the brain of years and other treatments that we have said in the division when the pain is great and suffering from lack of medicine.
Et se c’est uns enfes qui ne lou puisse soffrir, se li fai gargarisme et mastication mondifiant le cerveil sovent avec bones viandes;	And if it is a child who cannot bear the suffering, give them gargling and chewing, changing the brain often with good meat.
aprés li reis lou chief em mileu, et i fai I cautere selonc ce que nos avons dit devant, et I cautere sus lou vassel, et sus chescune corne;	After the head is removed in the middle, and the cautery is performed as we have said before, and the cautery on the neck, and on each horn.
et se li malaides est fors et soffrans, se li fai cauteres si com j’ai dit a celui qui ait paralisie et mollification de cors, sus l’espinee dou dos et dou col, et soit li cauteres olivier selonc la maniere que j’ai dit.	And if the pains are outside and severe, give them cautery as I have said to those who have paralysis and softening of the body, on the spine of the back and neck, and let the cauteries be made with olive oil according to the manner that I have said.
Se li malaides est enfes, se li fai I cautere subtil selonc ceste maniere:	If the pain is intense, apply the subtle cauterization in this manner:
Quant par la cause de melancolie sunt les superfluitez ou les moistors corrumpues et fleume grosse, adonques lou cauterize de teils cauteres com nos avons dit a celui qui ait paralisie.	When due to melancholy, the excess or corrupted moisture is great, then use the cautery of parts as we have said for those who are paralyzed.
Et se par la cause de melancolie est li superfluitez declinans a melancolie, et est li cors dou malaide moistes, adonc li done a boivre chose par coi li cervelz soit mundifiez, selonc ceu qu’il est devant en la division.	And if due to melancholy, the excess declining towards melancholy is wet, then give it to drink something by which the brain may be purified, according to what it is before in the division.
Aprés reis lou chief dou malaide;	After healing the main injury;
aprés fai I torteil de lin bien fait, ausi com I cercle, si le met emmi le chief;	After making a well-done tortilla, like a circle, and placing it on the head;
et li malaides sié croisiez, et soit bien tenus de toutes pars;	and if the wounds are crosswise, and held firmly from all sides;
aprés presente le linement, et vaut mues de burre de berbis ancien;	After applying the liniment, and it is good to use old birch bark butter;
et lou chaufe a feu tempreement, si que li dois s’on li boute le puisse soffrir;	and heat it with fire at a moderate temperature, so that the patient can bear it when drinking;
aprés vuide le cercle par dedens emmi le chief, et lou laisse refroidier;	After removing the circle from inside and placing it on the head, let it cool;
et fai ce a malaide chescune semaine une fois avec autre governement boin, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And do this to the wound every week with good management, until they are healed.
Ou se tu vues cauterize lou en faisant poins plusors a tot le cautere.	If you have seen cauterization done by making several pricks with the whole cautery.
Ceste maniere de cautere amoistit le cerveil igaument;	This method of cauterization moistens the brain excessively.
et puis met sus coton moilliet en burre et en graisse de geline.	Then place a wet cotton cloth on it and in goose grease.
de l’awe des eulz	of the eyes
Quant awe vient premierement as eulz par les signes que j’ai dit en la division, adonques encomence et done boivre au malaide chose mundifiant le chief, et le warde de toutes moistors, et lou fai suer ou bain plusors fois a jeun.	When the first sign comes to the eyes as I have indicated in the previous section, then begin and give the patient to drink a medicine mundifying the head, and keep it from all moisture, and make it sweat or bathe it several times a day on an empty stomach.
Aprés li comande a rere son chief, et li fai cautere emmi le chief, et li fai II cauteres sus les II temples se li dessendemens de l’awe est as II eulz ensamble, ou en I se li dessendemens est en I;	After that, command him to turn his head, and perform the cauterization on the back of his head, and make two cautery marks on both temples, above and below the ear, where one is missing.
et cope a tout le cautere toutes les voines et les arteres que sont desoz le keur, et soient li cautere lonc selon lou large de la temple;	And cover all the cauterization with veins and arteries that are outside the skull, and let the cauterization extend along the length of the temple.
et te warde de decorrement de sanc, et se tu vois trop de sanc issir, si li estainche de teil pooir com tu as.	And guard against bleeding from veins, and if you see too much blood coming out, stanch it with a piece of cloth that you have.
Et je t’enseignerai en l’estraction des arteres et a l’incision la cautele coment tu l’estencheras;	And I will teach you in the extraction of arteries and in the incision, how you would do it;
et aucune fois fait on cautere ou hatereil desoz les II os derrier.	and never cauterize or heat anything outside of the two lower bones.
dou cors des larmes	The path of tears
Quant les larmes des eulz sont ancienes et acostumees et sont sus les voines, ou delez les arteres que sont en l’aparance dou chief defors;	When the tears of the eyes are old and accustomed and are above the veins, or behind the arteries that are in the appearance of the main difference.
et on voit que c’est des superfluitez froides fleumatiques, adonques li fai le cautere que j’ai dit en l’encomencement de l’awe dessendant as eulz:	and we see that it is an excess of cold fluorescent, therefore the cauterize that I have said at the beginning of the work, descending to those.
I cautere emmi le chief, et II cauteres sus les II temples, et II cauteres ou haiterel desoz les II os;	The cauterize the main, and two cauterize above the two temples, and two cauterize outside of the two bones.
et s’il i a besoigne plus, si le cauterize saigement desus le sorcil a tout I petit cautere.	and if there is more, then the wise one should cauterize it thoroughly with a small firebrand.
dou cors des larmes par dedens les eulz	For the fire cautery, instruct the patient to let the hairs grow long and even; and if they prick at their base
Quant tu le medicines selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et il ne profite mie, adonques done a boivre a malaide III nuis cochies;	When you apply medicine according to what we have said in the division, and it does not help, then drink three drops of bad vinegar.
aprés li reis le chief, et li fai cautere ou mileu dou cautere olivaire;	After that, the king's oil, and the middle heat of the olive oil cauterization.
et fai II cauteres dou cautere qui est apelez «clavilis» sus les II sorcis, un poc desoz les chevous;	And make two cauterizations of the heat that is called "clavilis" on the two firebrands, a little away from the hooves.
et te warde de l’artere que tu ne la coper.	and guard the artery so you do not cover it.
Et c’est li forme dou cautere qui est apelez «clavilis»:	And this is the form of the cauterization called "clavilis":
Quant li papiere de l’oil est mollifie de maladie et de moistor, adonques la cautarize de cest cautere qui est apelez «olivare».	When the paper of oil is softened by disease and moisture, then the cauterization of this cauterization which is called "olivare".
de coi ci est li forme:	For what purpose this form is used.
Et se tu vues si fai II cauteres sus les II sorcis ausi lons com li sorcilz sont;	And if you see that you make two cauterizations on the two firebrands as long as the firebrands are.
et n’i lassiez mie la main fors que tant que li tierce partie de la papiere soit arse, selonc la maniere que j’ai dit.	and do not leave off the hand until the third part of the paper is burned, according to the manner that I have said.
dou poil qui point l’oil	the hair that does not hold the oil
Aucune fois avient que li poil des oilz sont convertit au pardedens, et poignent l’oil, et i fait on cauteres selonc II manieres:	Never is it the case that the hairs of the eyes are converted to parched, and they prick the eye, and if cauterization is done in two ways:
c’est a savoir de feu, ou de medicine ardant.	which is to say, by fire, or by burning medicine.
Ou cautere de feu comande au malaide qu’il laisse les poilz tant qu’il soient lons et igals;	For the fire cautery, instruct the patient to let the hairs grow long and even;
et s’il le poignent a lor nassance, se li estraint les eulz qu’il ne se muevent tant qu’il naissent.	and if they prick at their base, hold the eyes steady so they do not move until they grow.
Quant il naissent et i sont igalz, adonques met le malaide en ton sain;	When they grow and are even, then place the hairs on your skin.
aprés seigne sus la papiere des eulz une figure que soit ausi com li fuelle dou mirte, et soit li comencemens dou signe delez les poilz;	After drawing a figure above the eyes that is as similar to the mirror as possible, and starting from the beginning of the sign below the hairs.
puis i met coton moilliet en glaire d’uef et muscillaige de persillion sus l’oil, puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	Then place moistened cotton in glare of egg and musk of lavender on the oil, then heat the cauterizing iron to this shape.
Aprés cauterize sus la figure que tu as signiet poc et poc mout de fois, que li keurs soit ars lai endroit;	After cauterizing slowly and gently a few times, until the patient's skin is no longer sensitive in that place.
et li signes de la santeit de l’uevre est que tu voies la papiere retraite, et les poilz levez a la pointure de l’oil;	And the signs of health in this work are that you see the eyes retreat, and the hairs stand up at the height of the oil.
adonques lieve ta main, et laisse ensi III jors, puis i met coton moilliet en burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	Then gently place your hand, and leave it thus for three days, then put cotton wool on the burn until the burn is healed.
aprés le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	After the treatment of ointment until it is healed.
Et se aprés ceu vienent li poilz, et li papiere est mollifie adonques rencomence le cautere sus cel leu meisme, si com tu as fait premiers;	And if after this the hairs come back, and the skin is softened, then begin the cauterization again on the same limb, as you did before.
et se li poil sont defuer, si le cauterize tant que li papiere soit levee a son leu natureil, et soit igals, et ne poignent mie li poil l’oil.	And if the hairs are not enough, then cauterize until the skin is at its natural level and even, and do not prick the hairs with it.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il laisse les poilz tant qu’il soient grans et igalz, puis fai de parchemin la forme de la foille de mirte;	The fiery cautery is that you command the patient to let the hairs grow long and even, then make a piece of parchment in the shape of the leaf of myrtle.
puis pren de savon fransois et de vive chalz, de chescun une .З., et broie ensamble bien;	Then take French soap and live charcoal, of each one. Z., and grind them together well.
et le fai hastanment, si qu’il ne refroide, puis en espant sus la forme que tu es fait sicom la foille dou mirte, et met sus la papiere des eulz;	And make it into a paste, so that it does not cool, then spread it on the shape you have made like the leaf of the mint, and put it on the paper of the eyes.
et se li maladie tient en I oil soulement, si doit on ovrer en I, et se en ambedous ausi;	And if the disease holds only in one eye, then you must cover it with a cloth, and also do so in the other.
et met desoz l’oil coton moilliet en abin d’uef;	And put some woolen cotton moistened in front of it.
et li chiés dou malaide soit en ton sain et met ton doi mostrant sus la medicine, et presse I poc et lou muef toutes les fois que li malaide sent mordication de la medicine, car il sent mordication ausi com de feu.	And the patient with the pain should be in a healthy position and put your other hand above the medicine, and press the poison and the mouth every time the pain feels the sting of the medicine, because it feels stinging also like fire.
Quant tu as ceu fait longement, si oste la medicine a ton doit.	When you have done this for a long time, then you will have the knowledge of the remedy to your task.
Et quant li mordication sera passee, si leve le leu d’awe, et rewarde se tu vois la papiere levee ausi com s’ele estoit levee par constraignement de feu ou par incision;	And when the cauterization has been passed, lift the limb from the fire, and reward yourself if you see the paper raised as it was raised by constraint of fire or by incision;
et s’il est ensi, si est bien.	and if so, it is good.
Se ceu non, si remet encor de la medicine sus lou leu ou li medicine n’ait ovreit, tant que tes ovraiges soit igalz, et tes eulz mis a point;	If not, still put the medicine on the limb or the medicine has not worked until your work is equal and your eyes are fixed;
puis met sus coton moilliet en burre tant que li keurs ars soit cheus, aprés cure le leu de l’oignement qui est apelez «dyafenis» et d’autre, tant qu’il soit sanez.	then put cotton moistened in burre on the limb until the wounds are cleansed, then cure the limb of the burn which is called "diaphnesis" and others, until they are healed.
Et se t’est mestier que tu te warde bien a ton ovraige par grant warde qu’il ne chiece point de la medicine as eulz.	And if you have the task to stay within your work, be careful not to cut into the medicine with those.
Et se li papiere devient mole aprés, et li poil poignent en l’oil, si recomence la medicine sus celui leu qui est mollifiez de la papiere proprement, ensi com tu as fait devant;	And if the paper becomes soft after, and the hairs are pricked in the oil, then the treatment begins again on the joint that is softened properly by the paper, as you have done before.
aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	after the cure until it is healed.
et c’est li forme de la fuelle dou mirte:	and this is the form of the fuller's thistle:
Et saichés que li eul des homes sont divers en grandor et en petitece, et selonc ceu soit tes constraignemens;	And it is known that the eyes of men are different in size and shape, and according to what your constraints are.
et ne soit mie reponue li droite voie a celui cui est li estude de cest art.	and do not reply the wrong way to him who has studied this art.
de la cure de fistule par cautere	Of the treatment of fistulas by cauterization
Quant tu cures fistule si com nos avons dit en divisions des maladies, et tes cures ne profitent mie, adonques covient il que tu li fais cautere selonc ceste maniere.	When you treat fistulas as we have described in the division of diseases, and your treatments do not work, then it is necessary to cauterize them in this way.
Comande au malaide qu’il mette son chief en ton sain;	Command the patient to put his head in your hand.
et teigne li menistres son chief entre tes mains en teil maniere qu’il ne se mueve, ne ne demoinne son chief;	and tie the assistant's head between your hands in such a way that it does not move, nor remove its head.
aprés met coton moilliet en abin d’uef ou en jus de persillion sus l’oil;	after put wool felt under or in the juice of parsley on the oil;
aprés chaufe le cautere qui est teilz:	after heat the cauterizing iron that is there:
et est chevez au chief si com li forme d’une penne de vouteul, ensamble la queil soit li cautere;	and is shaped like a pen of vulture, together with the quill so that it be the cauterizing iron;
se tu vues, si soit apointé des l’un chief dusc’a l’autre, et se tu vues, si soit ausi com une tente;	if you see, if it is pointed at the head from one to the other, and if you see, if it is also like a tent;
mais toutevoie, cist qui est chevez vaut mues por ton ovraige.	but anyway, this which is shaped is worth more for your work.
Aprés presse la fistule s’ele est overte, et en trai la porriture, et la seche;	After pressing the fistula, it is opened, and through it, the pus is drained, and dried.
et s’ele est close, si la oevre, et trai fuers la bowe;	And if it is closed, then open the wound, and drain the poisonous fluid out of it.
aprés met sus le cautere chaut forment, et tien ta main au cautere a la partie dou neif ensus de l’oil, que ta mains ne faice folie;	After applying the cauterizing agent generously, hold your hand on the cautery at the part below the navel, so that your hand does not do harm.
et met le cautere en la graisse de l’oil, et la corromp.	And apply the cauterizing agent to the fat of the oil, and corrupt it.
Se tu viens au comencement dou cautere jusc’a l’os, si serait bien.	If you come to the beginning of the cautery just at the bone, that would be good.
Se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere encor une fois, et autre se tu en as mestier, et le laisse III jors;	If not, then begin the cauterizing agent again once more, and if you have the skill, leave it for three days.
aprés i met sus coton moilliet en burre, et lou cure de l’oignement desiccatif tant qu’il soit sanez, et se XL jors passent qu’il ne soit sanez, si met sus medicine ague corrosive tant que li os soit descovers;	After placing moist cotton on the wound, and applying a drying ointment until it is healed, if after 40 days it is not healed, then apply a corrosive medicine until the bone is exposed.
et lou reis selonc ceu que il venrait en son chapistre.	And the treatment according to what it would come in its chapter.
Et i a une maniere de cautere de fistule que aucun des anciens dirent.	And there is a way of cauterizing a fistula that no ancient people mentioned.
Entens a fistule, et fens le leu;	For fistula, and fasten the limb;
aprés met en la fendure I camahan subtil de coi ci est li forme:	After placing in the wound, the subtle instrument of which this is the form:
et i font a la quantiteit d’une .З. de plonc;	And they make with the quantity of one ounce of lead;
et tien ta main ou camahan fermement, et ne se mueve li malaides nes point, que li plons fondus ne corre a son oil;	And hold the instrument firmly in your hand, and do not move the hairs until the lead melts and corrodes its oil;
et covient c’on mette sus l’oil a malaide coton moilliet en abin d’uefz ou en awe:	and it is necessary to put on top of the wound, cotton oil moistened with urine in front of the inflammation or behind.
li plonc si art lou leu de fistule, et lou saine per mervillouse saniteit.	the plug if the hole of the limb of a fistula, and the healthy one by miraculous healing.
Et se li fistule est sanee per le cautere que nos avons dit, c’est boin.	And if the fistula is healed by the cauterization that we have said, it is good.
Se ce non, si covient aministrer pertus au neif, et ramener la fistule au cors dou neif selonc ceu qu’il covient en som propre leu.	If not, then you must administer poultices to the wound, and bring the fistula back to the core of the wound according to what is proper for that limb.
des crevaices en levres	of cracks in the lips
Mout de fois avienent crevaices en levres que sont apelees «poil», et meismement en levres des enfans.	Many times there are cracks in the lips that are called "hair", and also in the lips of children.
Quant tu cures ces crevaices de ceu que nos avons dit en divisions, et li cure ne profite, adonques eschaufe I petit cautere cultellaire selonc ceste forme:	When you treat these cracks as we have said in the previous section, and the treatment does not help, then heat a small cauterizing needle according to this form:
Et le met hastanment en celles crevaices tant qu’il viegne jusc’a font;	And put it firmly in those cavities until it comes just before it sets.
aprés cure le leu de cerote tant qu’il soit sanez.	After healing the limb of plaster until it is healed.
de l’aposteme de la goule	of the abscess of the groin
Quant apostume vient en la racine de la goule ou en l’uve, ou ou palais, ou as racines des dens, aprés fait porriture et ront et est enveillis et devient fistule;	When an abscess comes at the root of the tongue or in the eye, or in the palate, or at the roots of the teeth, after it is pierced and drained and swells and becomes a fistula.
et tu le cures si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie:	and you treat it as we have said in the sections, and it does not improve:
adonques covient il que tu aies I cautere selonc la quantiteit de la fistule;	then it is necessary that you apply the fire cauterization according to the size of the fistula;
aprés le bote ou pertus de la fistule, et tien ta main tant que li fer chaus viegne au font de li, et ou derrien leu;	after the boil or rupture of the fistula, and hold your hand until the iron comes to the bottom of the wound and behind the bone;
et fai ensi une fois ou II, aprés le cure de ce que nos avons dit en cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	and do this once or twice, after treating as we have said in the cures, until it is healed.
et s’il est curez ensi, c’est boin;	and if it is treated thus, it is good.
et se ceu non, si covient descovrir le leu et oster l’os corrumput, selonc ceu que vos le troverez en son chapistre.	and if not, then you must reveal the bone and remove the corrupted bone, according to what you find in its chapter.
dou movement des dens	movement of the teeth
Quant les gencives sont mollifies par moistor et les dens muevent, et tu le cures per medicines et ceu ne vaut, adonc met le chief dou malaide en ton sain;	When the teeth are softened by moisture and the joints move, and you treat them with medicines but it does not help, then put the head of the painful part in your mouth.
aprés eschaufe le cautere dont li forme venra ci aprés en teil maniere que tu mettes une cainne sor le dent;	After heating the cauterizer of its shape will come out after in some way that you put a cane on the tooth.
et met dedens le cautere chaut hastanment, et tien tant ta main que li malaides sente la chalor venant a la racine dou dent;	And put the cauterizer deeply and hold your hand so that the pain feels the heat coming to the root of the tooth.
aprés lieve ta main et rencomence le cautere selonc ta volenteit;	After releasing your hand and start the cauterizer according to your will.
aprés emplisse li malaides sa bouche d’awe salee, et la teigne une houre et raiche fuers.	After filling the pain with salt water, and the tissue for an hour and let it dry out.
Et en teil maniere li dens qui estoit movans si est confermez, et li gencive mollifie restrainte, et li moistors corrumpue sechie.	And in a similar manner, the tooth that was moving is now fixed, and the gum is softened by being held, and the moisture is corrupted and dried.
de la dolor des dens	of the pain of the teeth
Quant dolor de dens vient por froidor, ou il i a froidor ou veir, et les cures de medicine ne valent, adonc i ait mestier de cautere selonc II manieres:	When pain from the tooth comes from cold, or there is cold or wind, and medical treatments do not work, then it is necessary to use cauterization in two ways:
et cautere de burre et cautere de feu.	and cauterization with butter and cauterization with fire.
Cautere de burre si est telz que tu preignes burre de vaiche, et le bout en une cuillier de fer ou d’arain;	Cauterization with butter is such that you take butter from a fresh cheese, and the end in an iron or silver spoon;
aprés pren coton et envolope sus la pointe d’une tente, et la moille en burre bulit, et met sus le dent dolant hastanment et tien tant qu’il soit refroidiez;	then take cotton and wrap it around the tip of a tent, and dip it in melted butter, and put it on the painful tooth quickly and hold it until it is cooled;
et ensi fai sovent tant que sa vertus viegne a la racine de la dent, et se tu vues si moille laine et coton en burre froit, et met sus le dent doillant, et met sus I fer chaut tant que li feus viegne au chevement dou dent.	and thus do often until its virtue reaches the root of the tooth, and if you see that dipping linen and cotton in melted butter does not work, then put the hot iron on the painful tooth until the heat reaches the movement of the tooth.
Li cauteres ensamble feu si est telz que tu preignes uns cainne de fer ou d’arain, et soit grosse si que li feus ne viegne a la bouche dou malaide;	The cauteries are such that you grasp a needle of iron or brass, and it should be large enough that the heat does not reach the mouth of the wound.
aprés chaufe le cautere, de coi li forme venra ci aprés, et le met sus le dent et tien ta main tant que li cauteres soit refroidiez;	After heating the cautery, from which the form will come after, and place it on the tooth and hold your hand until the cauteries are cooled.
fai ceu sovent, car li dolor sera ostee celui jor meisme ou l’endemain.	Do this often, for the pain will be as strong the same day or the following day.
Et covient que li malaides emplisse sa bouche de boin burre en l’empressement de cel cautere, et puis le raiche fuer;	And it is necessary that the wounds fill their mouth with good butter in the urgency of this cauteries, and then the rich one.
et c’est li forme dou cautere:	et c’est li forme dou cautere: This is the form of the fire cauterization.
Et fai cautere dou queil chief que tu voudras, et selonc ceu que tu as pooir;	And make the fire cauterization as you wish, and according to what you have at hand;
et c’est li forme de la caine:	This is the form of the knife.
des scrophules	of tumors
Quant les scrophules sont de fleume et de moistors froides, et ne sont obeissans a digestion par medicines, adonques eschaufe le cautere cheveit de coi ci aprés vient li forme, et ait II aovertures por les fumees a issir au cautere de l’autre partie;	When the scrofula are cold and humid, and do not obey digestion by medicines, then heat the fire cauterization of hair from this after, and have two openings for the fumes to escape to the other side of the cautery.
et met le cautere chaut sus l’apostume une fois, ou II se mestier est, tant qu’il viegne au font de l’apostume;	And put the fire cauterization on top of the abscess once, or as often as necessary, until it reaches the base of the abscess.
et se li apostume est petis si met cautere selonc la quantiteit de l’apostume, et le laisse ensi III jors;	And if it is an abscess, apply cauterization according to the size of the abscess, and leave it like this for three days.
et met sus coton moilliet em burre tant que li arsure soit ostee;	Then place a piece of soft cloth soaked in butter until the burn is healed.
aprés cure le leu d’oignemens et de tentes tant qu’il soit sanez.	After care for wounds and dressings until they are healed.
Li forme de la cainne:	The form of the uterus:
Quant les moistors vainquent sus les chenals dou pormon, et meismement quant ce vient de froide complexion, adonc covient que li malaides soit voidiez premiers par medicines solutives;	When the moisture is strong in the pores of the skin, and especially when it comes from a cold constitution, then it is necessary to first remove the pains by means of solutions.
aprés li fai cautere a la racine de la gorge, et te garde que tu ne venir mie jusc’a la gorge, et n’ardre dou keur mais c’un poc.	Then apply cauterization to the root of the throat, and be careful not to come too close to the throat, and do not burn it with a strong heat but with a small amount.
Aprés li fai I autre cautere a la jointure dou col au chief de l’espinee, et soit li cauteres qui est apelez «clavile» de coi nos avons la forme devant;	After the other cautery at the joint of the neck to the head of the spine, and it is the cauteries that are called "claviere" by which we have the shape in front.
et cure le leu si com nos avons devant dit tant qu’il soit sanez.	and heal the limb as we have said above until it is healthy.
de la toust	of the whole
Quant tous et maladie de pormon sont de moistors froides, et li malaides nen ait fievre ne sechor, et est li maladie anciaine, se li fai .II cauteres sus la forcele en leus vuis;	When all and the disease of pormon are from cold moisture, and the pains do not have fever or sweat, and the disease is ancient, then he should make two cautery above the forehead in his eyes.
et I autre cautere emmi le pis entre II mameles;	and the other cautery between the breasts.
et soit li cauteres qui est apelez «clavile» selonc la forme qui est devant dite.	and it is the cauteries that are called "claviere" according to the shape that is said in front.
Et se tu vues, fai cautere en poignant a tot le cautere qui est apelez «poins» de coi li forme est ci devant en la maladie des oreilles;	And if you see, perform the fire cauterization by holding the entire cautery that is called "points" because of its form in the disease of the ears.
et soient li poins jusc’a XXX, ou enqui entor.	and let the points be just to 30, or within.
Aprés cure le leu selonc ceu qui est devant dit, et soit li cauteres a III rains selonc ceste forme:	After treatment, the patient according to what has been said before, and let it be that the cauteries are applied at three intervals according to this form:
Et por ceu sont li cautere plus legier, por ceu que tu en fais III a cop.	And because the cauteries are lighter, because you make three of them in a cup.
de la dislocation de l’ajutoire	of the dislocation of the shoulder
Quant li chiés de l’ajutoire est desaloiez par cause de moistor, et on le remet a leu, et il n’i puet demorer ains revient adés et desalue par petit movement qui avient, si com nos avons esproveit, adonques covient il que tu ramoinnes la dislocation premierement.	When the head of the shoulder is dislocated due to moisture, and it is reset but cannot stay in place, repeatedly dislocating with slight movement as we have experienced, then you must first reset the dislocation.
Aprés soit sovinez li malaides sus son dos et sus son costeit;	After, let the hairs be shaved on his back and on his ribs;
aprés lieve le keur qui est dedens le titillite as dois de ta main senestre;	After, relieve the part that is within the ticklishness of two fingers of your right hand.
et se li jointure est desaluee dedens, si eschaufe le cautere qui a II ners douqueil ci est li forme:	And if its joint is dislocated within, then heat the cautery that has two needles at the end in this form:
et cauterize lou keur tant qu’il le perce jusc’a costeit, et venrait li fugure dou cautere ensamble IIII cauteres;	and cauterize the part until it pierces to the ribs, and bring the figure of the cautery together with four cauteries.
et por ceu est faite cautere avec le cautere qui a III ners, por coi li figure de cauterization sunt sis cauteres;	and because of this, the fire cautery is made with the cautery that has three prongs, for the reason that the shape of cauterization is these three cautery.
et sont li nerf selonc la subtiliteit d’une tente et c’est li forme dou cautere qui a III ners:	and the nerves are according to the thinness of a tent, and this is the shape of the cautery that has three prongs.
Et aucune fois est ajostez sus ce I nerf por coi il i a VIII cauteres.	And never are they placed on this one nerve because it has eight cautery.
Aprés met sus le cautere porrelz broiez avec seil;	After putting the cautery on top, press with silk;
aprés fai reposer le malaide, et ne soit meus li membres par lonc tens tant qu’il soit bien confortez.	After allowing the wound to rest, and not making the limbs too long by stretching them until they are well comforted.
Et s’il est desaloiez desus, liquelz chose avient poc, adonques fait cautere sus l’epaisse dou cautere clavile, ou mout de cauteres en poignant.	And if it is dislocated above, this thing happens quickly, then make a cauterization above the thick part of the cauterizing knife, or with many cauterizations in pricking.
Car li jointure est refermee, et est ostee li moistor et est sanez li malaides.	For the joint is closed, and it is covered by moisture and is healthy of the pain.
Quant en l’estomac vienent froidures et mout de moistors tant qu’il l’estraient a sa complexion, et sont multipliet li catharre a lui, et es manieres de cures acostumees et il ne profite mie, adonc covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus son dos, et estende ses jambes et ses mains.	When in the stomach come cold and much moisture until it is at its condition, and are multiplied by vomiting to him, and are customary ways of cures and he does not improve, then it is necessary that the pain be soothed above his back, and extends his legs and his hands.
De ceu en aprés li fai III cauteres I desoz la cuillier dou pis per la quantiteit d’un doi, a tout le cautere clavile, et II cauteres defuers les II costez tant que li figure des cauteres soit a III angles, et ait teil espaice entre l’une et l’autre qu’elles ne soient jointes ensamble quant elles giteront porriture;	Because of this, after making three cautery with the fork from the least amount of one dog, to all the cautery clavicle, and two cautery before the two ribs until the shape of the cautery is at three angles, and has equal space between them so that they are not joined together when they are moving;
et soient li cautere si parfont qu’il porpreignent les II pars dou keur, et soit li figure des cauteres selonc ceste forme sens ajostement:	and let the fire cauteries be so sharp that they pierce both parts of the wound, and let the shape of the cauteries be according to this form without jostling:
Et se tu vues cauterize d’un grant cautere enmi l’estomac selonc ceste forme;	and if you see that a great cauterization is being done in the stomach according to this form;
et celui qui avra paour de cest cautere, cauterize en poignant et seigne sus l’estomac i. point selonc la quantiteit que tu vues d’enche;	and the one who has fear of this cauterization, cauterize by pricking and holding above the stomach i.e., not according to the quantity that you see of it;
puis le cauterize a tot le cautere qui est apelez «poins».	then cauterize with the whole cauterization called "point".
Aprés le cure de la cure que nos avons eut devant, tant qu’il soit sanez.	After the care of the cure that we have had before, as long as they are healthy.
Quant au foie vient dolor de froit et de moistor et de grosse ventositeit, tant qu’il est fuer mis de sa complexion natureil per les superfluitez;	When the liver comes from pain and moisture and great swelling, as long as it is forced out of its natural condition by excesses;
et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne li profite mie, si covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus son haitereil;	and the pain is treated with what we have said in the sections, and it does not help him much, so it is necessary that the pain be removed from its base.
et signe d’enche III cauteres selonc ceste forme et ceste figure et ceste quantiteit sus lou foie, defuer les ypocondres, lai ou li coutes de l’ome vient;	and the sign of three cauteries according to this form and this figure and this quantity on the liver, under the hypochondres, where the neck of the swan comes;
et ait d’espaice entre chaicun cautere la groissece d’un doi;	and there should be space between each cauterization the thickness of a finger;
et soient li cautere dou lonc dou cors, et ne presser mie mout ta main a tot le cautere;	and let the cauterization be long along the body, and do not press much with your hand on the cauterization;
et soit arse tant soulement li moitiez dou keur, et soit li malaides drois sus ses piez;	and let it be arched as much as only half of the curve, and let the hairs be straight up on their feet;
et s’il ne peut, si soit gisans, et estende ses jambes, et lieve ses brais;	and if he cannot, then let him lie on his side, extend his legs, and loosen his breeches.
et c’est li forme:	and this is the form:
Et se ta volentez est, si cauterize ces cauteres dou cutellaire, se tu es subtilz et saiges en l’art, et te warde que tu n’ardes mie tout le keur, car tu feroies sechier tout le cors;	And if you wish to, then cauterize these cauteries with a surgical knife, if you are skilled and wise in the art, and guard that you do not burn all at once, for you would make the whole body harder;
et qu’il ne viegne jusc’a boueil, car li keurs est mout subtilz lai endroit, et lou saiches por voir.	and that it does not come to boiling, for the wounds are very delicate in that place, and the hard parts to see.
Quant il a apostume au foie, et tu vues savoir s’il est en la char dou foie ou en la toile:	When he has an abscess in the liver, and you know whether it is in the flesh of the liver or in the membrane:
s’il est en la char, se sent li malaides dolor ne mie trop fort;	If he is in the carriage, he does not feel the pain much.
et s’il est en la toile, si sent dolor forsenee.	And if he is on the bed, he feels the pain greatly.
Et lors quant ceste cure desoit les mires, si covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus sa teste;	And when this cure lies down, it is necessary that the pain be above his head;
et puis seigne d’enche le leu ou li apostumes est, et puis chaufe le cautere qui est semblans au rais, de coi ci est li forme:	and then the lord of the limb where the abscess is, and then heat the cauterizing agent which is similar to rice, from which this form is made:
Et cauterize I cautere tant que li keurs soit ars, et viegne jusc’a syphac, tant que li porreture soit toute fuers;	And cauterize the cauterizing agent until the wound is sealed, and it comes just to the surface, until the suppuration is completely gone;
aprés la cure selonc la cure des essues tant qu’il soit sanez;	After the cure according to the cure of bandages until they are healed;
et ne covient mie que de cest cautere use nuls fuers que cil qui ait estudieit longement en l’art de medicine, et par cui mains cestes maladies ont corrut aucune fois.	and it is only appropriate for this cauterization to be used by none other than those who have long studied the art of medicine, and by whose hands these diseases have never corrupted.
Adonques puet il hardiement ovrer, et toutevoies il me semble que mues vaut li laissier.	Therefore, it can be bravely overcome, and in all ways, it seems to me that it is worth leaving it alone.
dou cautere de pleuresin	The cautery of the chest
Li ancien dirent que on doit faire a pleuresin cauteres de racines d’aristologe, et en teil maniere:	The ancients said that one should apply a cautery of aristolochia roots in this manner:
pren une racine d’aristologe longe, la plus grant que tu poras troveir, et soit seche, et soit ausi grosse et ausi longe comme tes dois;	Take a long aristolochia root, the longest you can find, and let it dry, and let it be as thick and long as your fingers;
et la moille en oile, et l’emprens au feu, et cauterize I cautere entre la forcele et lou col, et II petis cauteres un poc en dessendant en la partie qui est desoz la barbe;	and grind it in oil, and put it in the fire, and apply the cauterization between the nape and the neck, and use two small cautery irons to burn on the part that is outside the beard.
et II cauteres entre la quinte coste et la sisime, en declinant derrier un poc;	And the second fire cautery between the fifth rib and the sixth, in declining behind a little.
et I cautere emmi le pis, et I autre sus l’estomac, et I entre II espaules, et II as II costez dou pis defuers le cautere qui est entre II espaules;	And the first fire cautery at the worst place, and the second above the stomach, and the third between the shoulders, and the fourth on both sides before the fire cautery that is between the shoulders;
et ne presser mie ta main, ains fai apertement ausi com en odorant.	And do not press too hard with your hand, but make it open as if smelling.
