Et dirent aucun ancien que aucun home usent de cautere de feir semblant a I raseur, et l’eschaufent et le mettent entre les costes, tant qu’il vient a cel aposteme;	And they said no ancient one that any man uses a fire cautery like the razor, and they clean it and put it between the ribs, until it comes to the abscess.
et saut fuers li dolor, si com nos avons dit en l’aposteme dou foie.	and it jumped out of its place, as we have said in the abscess of the liver.
Mais en cestui ovraige est paour ou li malaides muert maintenant, ou fistule i vient qui ne puet estre sanee.	But in this work, there is fear or the wounds are fatal now, or a fistula comes that cannot be healed.
de la mice	of the mouse
Quant tu cures la maladie de la mice de ceu que nos avons dit as divisions des cures, et il ne profite mie, adonques i afierent III manieres de cautere que tuit sont boin.	When you treat the mouse disease that we have said about divisions of treatment, and it does not improve, then they resort to three methods of fire cauterization that are all good.
Desquelz li une maniere si est que tu faices III cauteres, ou IIII, en lignant selonc la longor de la mice, selonc la figure dou cautere dou foie que nos avons dit devant;	When one method is such that you make three or four cauterizations, along the length of the mouse, according to the shape of the cautery of the liver that we have said before.
et n’apresser mie ta main a tout le cautere, et soit li malaides sovins sor son dos;	and do not press your hand too much on the entire cautery, and let the hairs be above its back.
et une autre maniere de cautere si est que tu eschaufe le cautere qui a II ners, si com nos l’avons mostreit en la dislocation de l’espaule;	And another method of cauterization is that you heat the cautery with two needles, as we have shown in the dislocation of the shoulder.
et lieve le keur qui est endroit la mice, ou li coutes dou malaide vient devers senestre, et soit li elevations dont tu lieves le keur selonc la keur, selonc la longesce dou cors, et li cautere soient selonc la largesce dou cors.	and relieve the curvature that is near the mouse, where the pain of the hair comes from the side, and let the elevations that you relieve the curvature along the curve, according to the length of the body, and the cautery should be according to the width of the body.
Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII.	After applying the second cup, let the flames reach as far as the other side, and then remove the cautery, and thus you will have four.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	And if you see that it has been cauterized with the entire cautery at three cups.
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	After the treatment when it has grown worse due to prolonged tension, and this is appropriate that the other cures before mentioned should be done.
de ydropisie	of hydrocephalus
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	Caustic is not good for hydropsy, except in the manner which is called "asclepiades".
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis;	If your treatment according to the methods we have mentioned in divisions does not help, then it is necessary that you make four cauteries around the belly, and one above the stomach, and one above the liver, and one above the spleen, and two behind the back on the spine, and one in the worst place.
et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	and let the cauteries be close to the edge of the wound.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere;	After leaving the cauterization open for a while to prevent scarring, and do not neglect the care of the wound after the cauterization;
et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	and healing will proceed quickly, and together with God's help, the two intentions will be achieved.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit;	The shape of the cauterization for the belly is as shown in the figure we have before us;
et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	and the one for the back is olive-shaped, according to what is shown there.
de l’enfleure des piez	of the swelling of the feet
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire;	When the feet are swollen to one who is hydroptic, and are plain of a yellowish hue, you must cauterize above the back between the auricular and annular;
et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	And lightly touch the wound with the fire cauterizer, heading towards the opening.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not enter too deeply into the flesh, thus avoiding the yellowish part, and let the cauteries be done in this form:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire;	After making two incisions on each leg at the tip of the knife;
et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe;	And either cauterize the longer one behind the knee in front and the other in front of the leg inside;
et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse;	and leave the cauterizations overlong to cure, as it is better to do so.
aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	After the other treatments that we have said.
de la menoison	of the menstruation
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures;	When the solution of the belly comes from cold and moisture, as long as the retentive and digestive virtues which are in the stomach and in the intestines are affected, and cannot be cured by other methods of treatment.
et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule;	and you see the patient suffering greatly and of great virtue, then apply a large cauterization on the stomach according to what he has spoken of before or cauterization of the stomach, the cauterization circulates.
et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	and IV cauterizations around the neck delicately to all cauterization of the cross, and II cauterizations on the hips.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et I cautere sus chaicun yle, et II petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	If you see abundant moisture and the pain is intense, then perform fire cauterization on the base of the nail, and I cauterize each one, and II small cauterizations above the stomach below the large one, for the cure is beneficial when it has good help.
de la cure des emorroydes	of the treatment of wart
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres:	When the emorrhoids are at their foundation, or one or more, and are ancient and are large humors cold and moist corrupted, and are cured as we have said in divisions, and it does not improve, then apply cauterizations:
III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois;	III above the spine of the back, which is completely undisturbed and gradually triangular, and I cauterize II below the ribs.
et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile;	et if you think that his stomach is cooled, and the meat does not cook, and one sees the face swells, then the face is cauterized above the stomach as previously mentioned, and the other above the liver, and the other at all the cauterizing knife;
et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	and let the cauterizing knife remain long and tense.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After healing, the limb as long as it is healthy.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	of the cartilage that is called "thelul
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit;	when you cut the skin, if the cauterizing knife seems like a razor, and then put it all ablaze on the skin that is being cut;
et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort;	et let your hand approach as the fire cauterizes the vein at its birth, of which there is no pain.
fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit;	Do this once or twice, and if there is much bleeding, cauterize as we have said.
aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez;	After applying ointments until they are healed.
et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	And if you cauterize with a large firebrand, it will have greater help.
de plaie mal curee	of an improperly treated wound
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the wound cannot be suffered by a lancer or opened, as we will tell you in its place, if it is an illness that cannot be healed except by cauterization.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When any comes with fistula, and is awake and given porridge and corrupted moisture, then you must apply a thin tent to all of it, and guard that you wash the tent as much as it has of purity.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing;	After heating the cautery to the sharpness of a razor, and inserting it into the fistula according to the amount that enters, and then reapply the cautery as long as the corrosion and decomposition are sufficient, once, or twice, or three times, depending on the amount needed.
et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	and guard against the veins that are within, and great veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans;	if the fistula goes to the center of the bladder and intestine, then guard against these paths, and do not make any other movements except in the belly, and think that it is not healed.
aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement;	after curing the limb as long as it is healthy, and if the wounds are closed, and the matters are removed along with time, then cure that the wounds are completely healed.
et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font;	and if the matters are not removed, close the wound and corrupt the bone at the source.
et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	And thus, as one of those that we will say in its place.
de la maladie des reins	of the disease of the kidneys
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit;	When pain from cold comes to rain, and great moisture, and does not take the form of a woman, then it is necessary that you make a fire cauterization on both sides of the rain with the clavile cautery that we have already mentioned.
et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	And if we cauterize it in the middle, it will have three cauterizations in a row, and they will be greater help.
de la vessie	of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce;	When the bladder is weak and thin from cold and moisture, and the hairs retain the urine, then make a fire cauterization in the part before the bladder, where the beginning of the hair begins, and on the right and left, and let each cauterization be as long as a pin.
et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing;	and the first fire cauterization after the back, or II if you have a strong desire for it.
et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	and let the fire cauterizer be applied according to the form previously mentioned.
de la marris	of the marsh
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde;	When the wound is cold and moist, and does not leave any trace to be conceived, and the flowers are corrupted and their termination is late;
et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor:	and when they come, if they feel great pain:
adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos;	therefore it is necessary to apply the third fire cauterization around the wound, as we have said or the fire cauterizer of the bladder, and two fire cauterizations after the back.
et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	and let the fire cauterizer be applied as we have said.
de la hainche	of the belly
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble;	When moisture descends to the bottom of the back, and for this reason it moves out of its place, and the signs are that the thigh is longer than the other when measured together;
et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle;	and it is found in the lower parts of the back, then you should cauterize the pain above the bottom of the back with a cautery similar to a circle, and sign it in front of the joint around the back so that it returns, so that the back is within the circle;
et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	and if the cautery is such as those used to cauterize the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs;	And if this cautery is not present, then make three cauteries of large olives, and the cautery should be applied as usual to all the careers;
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and the cure as long as they are healthy.
de la dolor de la hainche	of the pain in the back
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene:	When pain comes in the side of the belly, and it is from cold and moisture, and the pains are treated as we have said in the division and the cure does not work, and the disease is ancient:
adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	then it is necessary that you purge the pain of large humors with bad-smelling pills, or other good-smelling pills similar.
Aprés li fai cautere;	After you do the cauterization;
et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres:	and the manner of the cauterization is according to the two methods:
c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	that is to say together with burning medicines and fire cauterization.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz:	1. The fire cautery is performed in many ways, such as:
que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire;	2. you cauterize the sac of the hip III triangular cauteries in this form, and it makes good depth and great, and has between each cauterization a space of the size of an egg, and let the cauterizing oil.
aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	3. one never cauterizes in the middle of the hip joint, because it is there with four in this form:
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche;	4. and if you see, if it cauterizes with the cauterizing circle that we have previously mentioned in the hip dislocation;
mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	but do it in such a way that the circle contains all the waist, and all the spines are straightened.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	And this is the way it is done in lithotomy, when the pain is in the groin and does not reach up to the thigh or the leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc;	And if it comes to the thigh and leg, then make two cautery marks where the hairs are, and one above the ankle four times, on the right side a little.
et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur;	and let the cautery marks be even, and straighten the spine.
et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	and if the hairs feel that the pain extends to two fingers or near the bone, then cauterize where it feels the pain three or four times at the cautery called "points".
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus;	And if the profession requires it, do more of it.
et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	And if the pain is located from the groin to the thigh, perform cauterization with a point or circular cautery, and be careful in all your cauterizations that you do not burn the nerves and large arteries, and that you do not cause greater harm and contraction.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	And I have also seen many who have done cauterization above the ankle of the foot, and left it for so long that the leg was completely numb, and the feet as well, and all the feet were rotten and corrupted.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After a bout of vomiting that resulted in death.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pain is on both sides together, perform cauterization on one and the other, in this manner.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce;	And the wise say in the cauterization of the loins, regarding this method, take such a needle and make it as large as a navillon of a finger, or slightly smaller, and make it with interstices and make one interstice join to the other at the distance of the quantity of a new penny.
et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait;	And let there be pliers over two parts, and also like a nose, and there should be one well-made iron tongs;
et c’est li forme:	And this is the form:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit;	And let it be heated until it is completely red and gives off a scent, and then place it on the back of the bad shoulder, and turn it over to the healthy side;
et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors;	and the cautery once the heater has cooled and leave for three days;
et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens;	and then apply a poultice of butter, and leave the wound open for a long time;
aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	after the treatment of ointment until it is healed.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent;	Albucasis says that we use this cauterization little due to its fearsome appearance, and few see those who use it.
et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	And therefore, this is a bad cauterization, which can suffer, and where it is applied.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi;	The cauterizing instruments of medicine are such that you make an instrument for piercing through the edge of the door, and either of brass or iron at one end, and in the top has II us, and between each the quantity of the size of a doe;
et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	and they should be overturned and above, and they join together according to this form:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche;	After placing the board of the back lying on its side, and quickly place your hand high on the board of the back.
aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	After pouring between the two circles of the hot water which is heated by the fire into a pot, and let it stand for an hour with low heat, and suffer the patient with the heat and burn of the.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu;	For it also has the effect of biting as if by fire.
et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit;	And when the biting has passed, loosen your hand with the instrument and lift the back of the hot water gently, and let it stand for three hours, and put on butter until the black part of the burn is removed.
et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait;	and let it remain three days to ripen;
et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	and this would be the last aid after the treatment of wounds until they are healed.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument;	And if the pain has spread to the thigh or leg, use the same instrument that you have used in the buttocks, increased.
et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	and this is the method of hot water, and I wrote it to treat the correction of medicine.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take chalk and live charcoal, as much of one as the other, and grind them together, and put them in a new jar.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir;	or if there is a small puncture other than the tip of a razor can be inserted;
et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main;	and put the other one can be well soaked in salt and alkali and soft water above, until there is the second above the powders that you have well soaked in your hand;
et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	and let it remain so long as it descends like awake and cuts or could break down, then take all of it, and pour it over the charcoal and over the alkali as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres.	And if it is very hot, it should be administered in the form of work of other medical works and cauteries of other members.
Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	For it does harm like fire, and if there are other medicines that are well cauterized in the abdomen like this, and honey, and charcoal with soap, all these things mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	And Galen tells us of a cure that some people were cured of the pain of the back and sciatica, and it was very effective, and he said that no other cure was made, and that they were well after one time when this cure was made, and he bathed himself as he teaches afterwards.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie;	And in this way you should apply a fresh and dry green fig, and grind it very well with a little fat, and put on the abdomen and thigh and leg where the pain is, and bandage it.
et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	and he leaves it for three hours, during which time the pain is not felt anymore.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	Then make the patient enter a hot bath until the heart is slightly warm, and then make them lie down, and the pain will go away completely and they will be healed.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And let it be known that no one should use such medicines with cauterization, unless after the evacuation of blood.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout;	And Dioscorides says that when the vein of the throat is cauterized with the wool of a goat, it helps a lot.
et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	and it should be done in this way.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take linen and pour old oil into it, and place it on the groove that is between the thumb and the other one called the foreshaft.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains;	After taking dry goat's wool and putting it in the fire until it becomes charcoal, and placing it on the linen, and leaving it until it is soaked.
et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee;	and do again in the same way, and do not stop doing so until you think that it is approaching the back, and that the pain has ceased.
et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	and these methods of cauterization are called "goat's beard cauterization".
de la dolor dou dos	of great pain to two joints
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, whether from falling or by impact or from too great evacuation, or from similar matters spread out cold, none of these is as effective as cauterizing with hot matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir;	It is recommended that the hairs are removed with fetid powders or similar substances, which are applied on top of the wound, where the pain is, three lines deep, and in each line V cauteries or more according to the virtue and quantity that the hairs can bear;
et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»;	and the cauteries are made according to the cauterization called "puncture".
et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	and if you see, make III cauteries or IV at the average cauterization called "clavière" in this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor;	Many times this disease comes to small children, and the signs of its beginning are that they have narrow backs when they stand, and fear.
et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	and you push in the lower spinous process of the back and see what appearance comes above the others.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this and you want to cure it, if you cauterize with the fire cautery according to this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	If the fire cautery grasps every part of the spinous process.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you see, then cauterize around the spinous process with the fire cautery touching the second or third line, and they are close to each other.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	After treatment, the limb should be kept as we have said, and you must not administer cauterization in a way that causes damage to the nerve.
de la dolor des jointes	The pain of the joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere:	When the pain of joints is from moisture that is spread to each limb of the body, and when the pain comes in the feet, which is properly called "gout", and when it is caused by cold and medicines cannot cure it, then it is cured by cauterization in this way:
fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	Make much of the cauteries around the joint of the foot, and let the cauteries be done in this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if there is a time when you must hold the face down, then perform the entire cauterization as claimed by the term "point".
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire;	And if the pains come from the groin and other joints, and often occur, then cauterize above each groin with three or four cautery irons of each part, using the oil cauterizer.
et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if you have more skill, then do more, but do not hold your hand too far from the patient until the spirit of cure is present.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pain descends to the jaw and the back, then administer the cauterization that we have mentioned in its chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes;	And if the pains are in the hands, then cauterize around the knuckles two lines deep.
et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main;	And if there is no pain after that, then cauterize above each joint and above the hair of the hand.
et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	If the pains come from the back or shoulders, cauterize each part, and apply good care and many medicines.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	For if you give good management and purge the humor, it will be healed with the help of God.
de la routure dou syfac	of the toothache
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor;	When fracture comes in angles, and the bowels descend to the groin, and this is not new, then when you see it to cure, that it does not move more that day.
et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre;	and that he uses things that lower the belly, so that the bowels descend from his belly;
aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors;	After, make him sit on his back between your hands, and command him to comb his hair until the bowels are returned, and tie them at your feet, and sign with your finger from above the broken bone of the thumb, and to all a sign that is similar to half a circle above the chest.
puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	then heat the cautery of this kind, which is in the form:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	so long as it is white and sweats scents.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu;	then reset the dislocations at their joints.
et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier;	and the assistants wipe their hands above that they do not return backwards.
et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains;	and work well the thighs at the hairs, and put a cloth and a bandage above them on the thighs, and the other below where he wipes his hands.
puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os;	then place the cautery above the sign of your hand, and hold it straight and hold it until you reach the bone, and if you do not reach it the first time, then continue with another until you come just to the bone.
et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere;	and guard subtly so the pus does not escape when you perform the cauterization;
que tu ne le brulasses;	so you do not burn it.
et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	and that by this means the hairs do not die, or other harm.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And when you do not see the bone at the fire cauterization, your works are worthless.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure;	And it is necessary that the cauterizations for children be subtle according to their age, and for large people also large according to their size;
aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	after three days care for the wound of the cauterization with butter until the scab is hardened;
aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee;	after the care of other remedies until it is healed, and grind the hairs 40 days on their back until the wound is well healed;
et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	And it is necessary that his bowel movements be loosened long before he enters the chamber.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors;	And after forty days, when he wishes to rise, apply a well-made bandage for forty more days.
et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire;	And he should have good rest, work little and avoid too much overeating and drinking, and too much loud noise.
et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	And when he does this instruction, he is completely healed.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will say what to do after the treatment of cutting into his chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	of the rupture of the belly
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur;	When wounds come in other bellies and are known, and you see that they do not grow any more, apply the fire cautery according to its quantity, and let it be third-degree heat.
aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit;	After the cure as we have said;
et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	And none of the ancients have said that it should be cauterized with the fire cautery at three angles according to this form:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	but the first sign is the swelling of the limb and make a line across the width above the tear, and another below, and hold your hand on all the cauterizing iron.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	But the first cauteries are lighter and more painful.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	of ancient pain in any limb
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain comes to any limb, or to fall or to be injured, and this pain lasts long, and the medical cure does not help, then it is necessary to cauterize with the cauterizing iron called «poins», and the cauteries should follow the length of the limb and its smallness and its weakness and its strength and its location of twists and its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien;	If it is healthy and the first cautery is applied well, then it is good;
se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	If not, then begin another cautery above the first one, for it is usually customary that it should be allowed to die in the member that is closest, which is why you must make the cauteries until the hairs are healed.
de meselerie	of medical instruments
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	Medical instruments are often not helped by cauterization due to great harm, and at the same time, the disease that comes from the putrefaction of fluids and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief:	If you see that the cautery has not taken effect, then take care if the disease is at the beginning, and if it has been cured according to what we have said in the division, and does not remain or disappear, and you doubt that the corruption will not spread throughout the wound, then make five cauteries above the chief:
I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous;	I embrace the head with both hands, and the other towards the forehead at the end of the jaw.
et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel;	and II above the two horns, and I behind on the hauterel.
et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir;	and let the hand be as far as the cautery comes to the bone, and as long as the scars come out so that the vapors of the large humors can escape.
et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	and cauterize on the small one according to what it is in front.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse;	And if the wound is scattered everywhere;
et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules;	and it is evident that you should cauterize with these cautery we have said or at the head, and the cautery in the nose, and two cautery on the spine of the neck, and six cautery on the spine of the back, and one great one on the croup and one other below, and two on the shoulders;
et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains;	and II above the ears, and II above the tendons of the little finger, and I above each joint of the hands and feet, and above the wrists;
et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler;	and guard against the nerves that are above the lower back, so as not to burn them;
et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	and never perform a fire cauterization above the bone of the thumb, and I above the bone of the stomach, and I above the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite;	And know that the more you perform a fire cauterization, the less you should give aid, and move it less;
et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	And know that the hairs do not feel pain as much as healthy people do, because the body is already corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	It is necessary that the cauterization be large and small according to the members and the joints, as you will find in the methods of irons.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After curing the wound with flour several times with honey and other treatments until it is healed.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre;	When a swelling comes to any member and is treated with medicines, oils, and plasters, and it is not healed, then you must cauterize over the member according to its size and smallness.
et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur;	and let the cauterization go a little into the healthy flesh;
puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat the wound until it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure;	And never cauterize with the hand and at the back and at the elbow, at the end of the nerve that moves the member, and thus if it is calcified the swelling;
et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	and in no way intervene unless they are known about the members and the outlets of the nerves moving the body.
de albaras	For the barbarians
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color;	When the disease called "albaras" is awakened, and medical treatment does not help, then cauterize with a cautery a little in front, according to the amount of the spirits' strength, until the whiteness is stopped, and it is moved its color;
puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie;	then the cure of flour and lentils with rose oil and plantain leaves, and blood of a pigeon and blood of a dove, of each one a part;
et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	and let it be mixed altogether, and let it be tied with a cloth, and let it be applied to the limb as long as it is healed.
li cure de chancre par cautere	the treatment of chancres by cauterization
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When a chancres appears at the beginning, and you see it stop spreading, then cauterize it with a cautery that seems like a circle, all around the circumference of the chancres.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre;	And all the wise people said that one should make a fire cauterization as in the middle of the chancre;
et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois;	and this does not seem good to me, because I believe that it should not be ulcerated and corrupted, and I have never seen it happen;
et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	and the better thing is that it should be cauterized around, with the fire that is called "circle", as we have said in many cauterizations.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	of the swelling that cannot die
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens;	When someone has a disease called "adubelati", and it is slow to die out or due to the excess that it causes or due to the age of the malady when they are decrepit (that is, too old) and they have little blood, or due to the tension;
et tu la vues haster de meurer:	and you see it hurrying to die:
adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant;	then cauterize around the wound with many small cauteries by holding them;
aprés le laisse ensi.	then leave it thus.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	For it will hasten to die.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see it pierced by the entire cauterization, then warm up the cauterization from where this is the form:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And place your hand in the middle of this disease called "adubelati" until the cauteries have pierced the skin, and be such cauteries that the pain felt before is in a similar manner to the course of the porridge is alleviated.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	After the treatment until he is completely healed.
li cure dou feu par fer	The treatment of fire by iron
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another way of disease is called "corrodens", and it is nothing other than a piece of member, for it twists the members as if the dry reeds would.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est;	If you see this disease in the limb that can suffer cauteries and fire together, then heat the small, sharp cauteries greatly according to what is needed for the limb or the disease.
aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	then cauterize all parts until you reach all the corruption, and nothing remains of it, so that all that is corrupted is removed.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	And then leave it for three days, and apply a poultice with oil over the wounds until the burnt flesh is removed and all the corruption.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	After the treatment of boils, they generate carbuncles.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin;	And if you see after three days that healthy pus does not appear, it is good;
et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	And if not, then restart the fire cautery on the part that has remained undamaged.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu;	And this method has never been treated with medicine in place of fire cauterization.
mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division:	But all fire cauterization is of greater help, and I have already given the cure of medicine in the division:
pren la quant tu en as mestier.	Take it when you have the opportunity.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	of the peas that come to the feet
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	Many times it comes to the feet by defect, and a disease arises which is called "clubfoot" according to our understanding, and it is a great disfigurement that makes the foot ugly.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the cauteries of this disease are according to two methods.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	That is to say, fire cauterization, and water cauterization with hot iron.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges;	Fire cauterization is such that it heats the cautery hair as if it were a pen feather, and it should be made of good iron at the measure that it can pierce the nail of all parts, and that it has thin edges.
aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou;	After you put everything on top of the nail, and turn your hand all around the nail until it reaches the head of the nail.
et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture;	and let it stay there for three days until it begins to rot.
puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	Then make a poultice of wild savage crushed herbs with linen, and leave the poultice on all night, and the nail will fall off and be removed from its roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then cure the joint with poultice applying hot char until it is healed.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude;	And if they are converted by the previous wound, and often in the hands and feet, then it is necessary to apply fire cauterization with very hot fire.
et est en teil maniere:	and in a similar manner:
pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues;	Take a needle of iron or steel, or a quill pen, and place it above the nail and the althelul, that is to say, the verucas.
et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine;	And place the needle above it so that it pierces all around, then put a little hot wax, and hold your hand firmly, and press your hand back and forth so that the edge of the needle reaches the root of the nail, and find the hot wax penetrating to the root.
et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre;	And suffer the pain a little from the burning of the hot wax for an hour.
puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	Then leave it thus, and it will fall off at all its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	After doing another one like this, remove all those who are in the chest, then treat the boils that cause char.
li cure dou trembler	the cure for trembling
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee;	When some tremble from cold or fever quartan or other, it is necessary that you make four burns or four on the spine of the back, one cautery between each spine.
et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire;	and one on the belly, and one above the stomach at the cautery of the olive.
si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	It will let the trembling go, and it will hurry the health from the cold disease.
des pustules puans	of pus-filled boils
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	No times have appeared previously when the chest was bathed with pus and pustules that come from large corrupt matter.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule:	If it is necessary at the first when they appear that one makes burns above each head of the pustule:
un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	a fine cauteries of willow bark, of which the point is grasped in the fire, or of the root of aristolochia long, or at the lens cauteries.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez;	And often the cauterization is done at the beginning when they appear, according to this method, and it cannot grow into new ones, but breaks down the excess that comes from it, and are healed.
mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	but it must be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	when the artery is cut
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses;	Many times there are great flows of blood from the artery that is cut at the wound that comes from the perforators, or in the incision of the abscess, or in the cauterization of the limb, and similar things;
et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	and it is a very painful thing to stop.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus;	And in any case when it has to do with anyone, you must quickly place your finger on the wound of the vein, and hold it tight until the bleeding stops completely and no more comes out.
puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge;	Then, apply fire cauteries of olive oil, many small and large ones, until they are all red.
puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	Then, apply I, or large or small depending on the wound and the location where the artery is, and place the cautery above that vein or where you hold your hand, and keep the cautery until the blood does not flow out.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement I autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if you have to lift your elbow quickly when lifting the vein, and the cautery is extinguished, then take the other cautery that is at the fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez;	And do not stop doing this one after another until the blood is stopped.
et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide;	And be careful that you do not burn the nerve that is nearby, and that other harm does not come to the wound.
et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit:	And be aware that when the vein is not cut, it cannot be stopped immediately when the artery is large, unless by one of the four methods that we have mentioned.
ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc;	or by cauterization, or by extraction when it is not yet treated, or by strong ties of thread, or by medicines placed above that have the power to stop bleeding;
et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	and either tied and restrained in this way.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Whoever administers tight binding with cloths or other things burning above, or similar things, does not benefit if not done carefully.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne;	And if this happens to anyone and they do not have any remedy present, then they should put their finger index above the wound of the vein as we have said, and well compress it until it is stopped above the wound and above the vein;
et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez;	and they should not move it, but they should apply cold compresses often until it is very cold and the blood is congealed and stopped.
et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	and make inquiries about the matter of cauteries and medicines.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	Here begins the second book of remedies for wounds
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres;	We have told you in the first chapter all about the diseases for which it is necessary to use fire cauterization or burning medicines, and their questions and causes and instruments and forms of cauteries.
et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	and I have put that chapter of the neck down to the feet, and I will go to this chapter by the same way because it is easier to find what we want.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And therefore when I begin this chapter, it is necessary, dear child, that you learn that in this chapter there is more danger and fear than in the first of the cauteries, and for this reason it is necessary to take greater precaution.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses;	For in the work of this chapter, there is often the evacuation of blood when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and in the treatment of wounds, and in the extraction of arrows, and in cutting into stones, and similar things;
ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	where there is doubt and fear, and many die.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	And I warn you that you should not undertake foolishness.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	For many methods of people come for cure.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice;	if they come from such people who have become so with their illness that they die quickly because of the treatment they receive for their disease, and from the greatness of its evil.
et de ces doit on avoir paor.	and one must fear these.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit:	And there are those who give you their sense, and say:
«atendez, je sui garis»;	wait, I am ready";
et li maladie est despitouse.	and the disease is spiteful.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los;	You should not grant permission to those who come to you with this manner, but put more caution in your honor than in your desire, and do not open foolishly but wisely of what you are certain and what you have taken and lost.
et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie;	and use prognosis and indication in the treatment of your ailments so that health may be converted.
et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	and this will help you to gain good reputation, and glory, and memory for the long time.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Very dear son, Our Lords grant you good understanding and rightness, and if you wish to breathe from the holy inspiration of His hand, amen.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	Or I have ordered you this chapter by dividing it into sections, according to what is before or after the chapter on cauteries, that I have divided from the beginning to the end, because you will find it more easily what you will have to do.
dou chief plein d’aigue	The beginning full of sharp
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant;	It is known that this disease often affects infants at birth, and when the neck of the child is held too tightly;
et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	and sometimes it comes from a cause that has not been remedied.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors;	And I have never seen this disease except in children, and all those that I have seen have died;
et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	and therefore it seems to me that I should avoid this work in these treatments.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir;	And I saw a child who was suffering from severe pain, and the head was swelling each day until it could no longer bear it.
et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os;	and I thought that the swelling was so great that he died, and this swelling is assembled outside the bone above the shoulder, between the neck and the bone.
et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large;	and the work is such that if the swelling is between the neck and the bone, and the abscesses are small, then you must make a wide incision into the head.
et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre;	and it should be as long as we, until the swelling flows out.
et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	and here is the form of the space:
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai II fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If the moisture is more abundant, and the abscess is larger, then make two incisions in the form of a cross, according to this shape:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut:	And if the moisture is outside the bone, and you see the signs that you see the commissures of the head opened on each part, and the sharp pain that you feel when you press it with your hand inside, and it does not return to you:
si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	then it is necessary that you cut into the head three incisions in this manner:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	And after the incision, drain all the moisture out.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor;	After you strain the incisions with bandages and powders, and put in wine and oil, and leave it so for five hours;
puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	then you release it, and treat the wound with bandages and blisters, and leave the head strapped again, and give the patient to eat dry meat without moisture until the member is comfortable and healthy.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue;	And another way of incising is that you look for the size of the abscess and the sharpness of the needle;
car aucune fois est elle devant;	for it is never in front;
aucune fois derrier;	for it is never behind;
aucune fois en destre;	for it is never on the right;
et aucune fois en senestre.	and it is never on the left.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir;	Then cut where the abscess is open, and fill the needle with, and make the incision according to what you have the power to do;
et warde que tu ne coper l’artere;	and be careful not to cover the artery.
et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	and if blood comes out, so that the hairs die from the detachment of blood and the evacuation of moisture.
de reume	of return
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les II arteres.	When it comes to any disease that is called "cataract" on those or in the foot, and the disease is ancient, and the medical treatment does not help much, then the treatment is to cauterize with what they cover the two arteries.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief;	Therefore, when you see that the joints are dislocated, it is necessary to make them return to their proper place.
aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel;	After that, rub the limb with a rough cloth until the arteries become visible, then hold the dislocated joint against the entire cloth.
puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues;	Then look at where the blood flows, and if the veins on both sides of the ears are not restored, they are not yet fixed.
puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	Then sign the veins of the ear, then cut both sides with a sharp knife until the vein comes out from the bone, and it should be through the width of the head.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com II dois au traver.	And if you see, pour out the sponge outside the artery and cover it above, cutting in the same way as it should be through the middle.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	And when the vein is cut, let it bleed continuously until it stops on its own.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os;	And if the artery does not open to the touch, then it is necessary to measure the quantity of the space of three fingers, then drill into and through the bone;
et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere;	and put six drops of blood outside if it is necessary to do so, and perhaps a little more or less, depending on what the patient can bear, and the replenishment of the artery;
puis regarde la plaie:	then look at the wound:
s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	if it remains above the bone point do not let any pus come out, then strain the wound and bind it, and the treatment of ointment until it is healed.
de emigrainne	for the head of the shoulder
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	when the ancient head of the shoulder comes, and it is stuck due to the moisture of tears and chills in the temples and old age and similar things, and it is treated by means of medical cures and nothing helps him, then we should cauterize the arteries of the temples and burn, as we have said.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit;	And the manner of their extraction is such that the hairs of his temples face the bad ones, and listen to the artery that opens in the temple, because it opens well by its beating, and is not quickly restored in anyone who is too fat.
et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement;	And if it is restored, hold the neck with some cloths, then rub the limb with some rough cloth, and raise the limb in hot water until the artery opens clearly;
puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	then take the spoon that is here:
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie;	then gently scrape the skin until you come to the artery, then pull it up with pincers, and remove it well from all parts of the cloth;
et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	If the artery is thin, then turn it back to the tip of the needle, then cover that part according to the amount of the two needles.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	But if it is not covered, it will not jump all at once.
Et trai dou sanc des VI c/, jusc’a III;	And draw out a little blood from the vein, just enough to fill three small containers.
et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en II leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc;	If the artery is large, then it is necessary to tie it in two places with a strong silk thread, so that no blood comes before the healing of the wound, and so that it does not cause further bleeding.
puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les II liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez;	Then cover the excess that is between the two knots with a small amount of ointment in the same hour, and then, if you see, if the cautery cutellaire is applied to the bone until the needles are covered.
et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	And this is the work of death, when the pain is not accompanied by fever and it is of a hot constitution.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors:	For the cautery is to finish the moistures:
por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	For it is of greater help against moistures.
Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites;	Or it is necessary for the extraction of arrows that one fills the wound with old cotton and places on top well-made bandages;
et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when they are removed, if necessary apply dry remedies that cause blisters and bandages until they are healed.
et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez;	And if without cutting the artery as you work, then quickly cover it with cauterization, or fill the wound with vinegar and apply it to your hand that the uncut part is not stained.
et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient;	and if you do not have this present, put it on the joint as much as the sinew should not be frozen, and raise the joint from high cold until the sinew ceaselessly, and it should be stretched as it should be.
et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de II pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	and what is more movable and lighter in the extraction of the artery is that you cauterize the vein with this cautery cutting from two parts, but the cutting should be well spaced to last longer in their heat.
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	When instruments are too tight, they hold less heat.
Et doit avoir entre les II coutelz I doit de gros d’espaice, et puis quant tu as signiet d’enche les II leus, et tu mes lou fer ardant sus tant qu’il viegne jusc’a l’os, et cope la voinne en II leus;	And it should have between the two knives one inch of space, and then when you have slit the two veins, and you melt the hot iron over it until it comes just to the bone, and cop the vein in two parts.
et soient esloigniet entre les II chiés car il n’est mie soudez de cest cautere dou tout en tout;	and let them be separated by the two shoulder blades because it is not known how much of this cauterization affects the whole body.
et c’est li forme dou cautere:	and this is the form of the cauterization:
des larmes	of tears
