Quant les larmes des eulz sont dessendans des voinnes que sont sus lou test dou chief de fuer, et il ne profite mie cure de medicine c’on i faice, et tu vois la faice dou malaide enrougir, et sent ou front ambulation si com de fremis;	When the tears of the eyes are descending from the veins that are above the skin of the head, and it does not improve with medical treatment, and you see the face of the patient becoming twisted, and it feels like a tremor.
et sui oil sont tenve et moiste si que li poil des papieres sont cheut, et sont eschaufees les papieres, et escorchies de l’ardor des larmes, si ait mestier de ceste cure.	and they are held and moistened so much that the hairs of the papers are burned, and the papers are charred, and scorched by the heat of the tears, if it is necessary for this treatment.
Et l’apelerent li ancien «cure contuse», et est que tu faices a rere au malaide qui a ceste maladie les poilz qu’il ait ou front, puis li fai III fendures ou front igalment selonc la longesce dou front;	And they called the old "wound healer," and you should do this for the painful part that has this disease, whether it has hair or not, then make three cuts evenly along the length of the forehead.
et soit l’une des fendures ausi com II doi tout emmi lou front en avalant aval jusc’a neif, et les autres II as II costelz par desus les papieres, et te garde de l’incision des arteres que sont as II costez par desus les papieres;	And either one of the cuts as two downwards from the forehead, and the others two along the ribs, above the ribs, and be careful not to incise the arteries that are above the ribs.
et aloigne ta main de la continuation des II mandibules, et soit chescune plaie la quantiteit de III dois au traver joins;	And keep your hand away from the continuity of the two jaws, and let each wound have the quantity of three drops through the joints.
et aies apparillie une piece d’esponge et mout de drapelz ses por essuer lou sanc, puis boute le spatumile agut de II pars de coi ci est li forme:	and have prepared a piece of sponge and much of cloth to wipe away the blood, then boil the spatula in two parts of water that is this form:
des l’incision qui est dever la temple jusc’a la seconde incision;	from the incision which is from the temple to the second incision;
et escorche tout le keur qui est entre les II fendures a tot lou syfac qui est sus l’os, puis fai autreteil des la moiene incision jusc’a l’autre seconde, et puis estrai fuer cest spatumile.	and scrape all that is between the two cuts to the entire face which is above the bone, then make another part from the same incision to the other second, and then stretch forth this spatula.
si boute en la premiere fendure l’estrument qui est apelez «cultellaire», et est tresbien trenchans d’une part, et d’autre part est souef, ne mie trenchans, et c’est li forme:	If you insert the instrument called "curette" into the first cut, it is very sharp on one side and dull on the other, and this is its shape:
Et met le costeit taillant vers la char aerse au keur, et lou costeit souef vers l’os, et lou boute tant qu’il veigne a la moiene fendure.	And place the sharp side of the curette towards the eye and the dull side towards the bone, and continue scraping until it reaches the same cut.
Et cope toz les vasselz que dessendent dou chief as eulz tant que l’incision soit continue jusc’a ceu qui apert dou keur, et puis autreteil fai en la moiene fendure jusc’a l’autre defuer;	And copper all the vessels that descend from the head as those which are so long as the incision is continued to what opens the face, and then make another part in the same cut to the other side.
et puis estrai dou sanc igalment, et espresse lou leu por le sanc pris;	then evenly extract the blood, and express the joint for the blood taken;
puis met en chescune fendure une tente de viel coton, et met sus drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile et en aisil, et garde que apostemes chaus n’i veigne;	then place a piece of old cloth in each wound, and put on dressings soaked in wine and oil and vinegar, and make sure that abscesses do not come.
et au tier jor deslie lou liien, et i amenistre grant planteit d’aigue tede, puis lou cure d’oignement basilicon avec oile roset, et d’autres cures dont on cure plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and at the end of the day, release the joint, and apply a great amount of salt, then the healing poultice with red oil, and other remedies to heal wounds, until they are healthy.
dou reume des eulz	renewing of the eyes
Quant a aucun vienent catarre agut acostumeement, et tu vois les eulz tenves et petis, et afoiblir la veue, et les papieres brulees;	When anyone comes for the usual cauterization, and you see the eyes tightly closed and small, and weakened vision, and burnt papers;
et li poil chieent, et ou chief en parfont a dolor ague, et li malaides esternue;	and the hairs prick, and where the hair meets the skin, it causes sharp pain, and the hairs are discharged.
adonques saiches par ces accidens que celles matieres et cil catharre ne vient fuer que de maintes voines, et li muedre cure que i est, si est ceste.	therefore, avoid these accidents that these matters and this cautery do not come from many veins, and the movement that is, is this.
Et est que tu comande au malaide a rere son front, puis fai une grant fendure emmi lou front, et une autre dou large I poc.	And it is that you command the patient to turn his head back, then make a deep cut into the forehead, and another one wide at the forehead.
Et comence des la fendure de la temple senestre a la temple destre, et soit li incision jusc’a l’os;	and begins at the cut of the right temple to the left temple, and let the incision just to the bone.
et esloigne ta main des ners des temples que muevent au mengier;	and move your hand away from the nerves of the temples that cause pain.
et quant li os est descovers, si essue tout le sanc a une esponge, et puis desevre entre les II levres de la fendure et i met coton viel, et tentes de lin;	and when the bone is exposed, soak up all the blood with a sponge, and then clean between the two lips of the cut and put wool, and test with linen.
puis lie desus drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile, et te garde d’aposteme chaut;	then lay strips of cloth soaked in wine and oil above it, and guard against abscess.
quant il est ostez, si covient que tu frottes l’os tant que chars i comence a naistre, puis le cure de choses exiccatives, que font enjanrer char.	when it is removed, it is necessary that you rub the bone until charcoal begins to form, then treat with things that cause vomiting, like char.
En teil maniere:	In a similar manner:
pren II parties de flor de froment, et de colofoine IIII parties, et en fai emplaustre;	take two parts of wheat flour and four parts of cologne earth, and make a poultice.
et l’aministre en ces plaies por enjanrer char per tout.	and administer it in these wounds to cause vomiting throughout.
de l’estoupement des oreilles	of ear deafness
Tout ceu que chiet ens oreilles est une des IIII choses:	All that which enters our ears is one of the four things:
ou grains, ou beste, ou piere de mine ou semblans chose si com fer;	or grains, or beasts, or stones from the mine or similar things like iron.
ou semence, si com jaisses, feves, pois;	ou semence, si com jaisses, feves, pois;
ou chose defluans si com aigue et aisilz et semblans choses.	For the fire cautery, instruct the patient to let the hairs grow long and even; and if they prick at their base, hold the eyes steady so they do not move until they grow.
Quant il chiet en l’oreille piere ou autre maniere de chose que ne s’ajoste mie a l’oreille, ne ne croist en l’oreille, si met l’oreille au solel.	When it chiefs in the ear pebble or other kind of thing that does not fit well in the ear, does not grow in the ear, then put the ear to the sun.
Se tu vois la piere, si distille aucun poc d’oile violet ou oile de sisament, puis i amenistre extraction;	If you see a stone, spill a little purple oil or sesame oil, then moisten the extraction.
et lou fai esternuer de condisi, et li estoupe les narines quant li esternuemens vient, et met entor l’oreille pieces de drapelz ou laine;	and the patient should spit out the condition, and stop up the nostrils when the sneezing comes, and place pieces of cloth or wool around the ear.
et estent l’oreille au desus.	and hold the ear upwards.
Mout de fois vient fuer par ceste cure;	Many times it comes from this treatment.
et s’elle ne vient fuer, se li amenistre extraction as pinceures subtilz, de coi ci est li forme:	And if it does not come forth, apply gentle extraction with fine tweezers, of which this is the form:
S’elle saut fuer as pinceures, c’est boin;	If it comes out with the tweezers, that is good.
se ceu non, si amenistre extraction a l’oncine subtil de petite doubleure;	If not, apply gentle extraction with a fine needle;
et s’elle ne saut par ceu, si fai une caine d’arain et boute lou chief de la cainne ou pertuis de l’oreille fort, et estoupe ceu qui est entor la cainne de cire mole si que li vens n’i puisse entrer avec la cainne;	And if it does not come out with the needle, make a small hole in the rain and pour water into the top of the hole or the ear canal very strongly, and stop up the hole with melted wax so that nothing can enter with the needle.
puis le trai fuer forment, car mout de fois vient fuer si com nos avons dit;	Then remove it properly, as it often comes out as we have said.
et s’elle ne vient fuer en teil maniere, si prent glut de coi en prent les oisiaus, et met en som aucun estrument qui soit a point por ceu faire, et met un poc de coton entor;	and if it does not come out in some way, she takes glue from some means, and puts it on the wound, and places any instrument that is sharp to this purpose, and puts a little cotton around;
puis presse le glut sus la piere ou quel chose que ce soit, et trai fuer.	then press the glue over the stone or whatever, and pull it out.
Et s’elle ne saut fuer de toutes ces choses que nos avons dit, si te haste de fendre l’oreille ainsois que aposteme chalz i veigne, et spasme;	And if she does not do any of these things that we have said, then you must quickly cut the ear as soon as an abscess forms and pus comes out, and spasm;
et li maniere de la fendure si est que tu faices premier sainier lou malaide de la cephalique, et estrai dou sanc selonc la mesure de sa vertu, puis fai seoir lou malaide entre tes mains et li torne l’oreille au desus, et fent une petite fendure en la racine de l’oreille a la graisse ou leu dependant;	and the way of the cut is that you first make a small incision into the painful part of the ear, and extract the pus according to its strength, then place the wound between your hands and turn the ear upwards, and make a small incision at the base of the ear where the grease or fat lies;
et soit li fendure ausi com une lune, tant que tu viegnes a la piere, puis l’oste selonc ton pooir, et la suce hastanment a ta bouche;	and let the cut be as wide as a crescent moon, until you reach the stone, then remove it according to your ability, and suck the poison into your mouth.
et la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat it until it is healed.
Et se c’est grains qui est ens et il enfle, si aministre extraction;	And if it is small and swells up, administer extraction.
et si’il ne puet issir, si amenistre I spatumile tenve subtil selonc ceste forme:	and if it cannot come out, then administer the following subtle method according to this form:
et amenistre incision de celui grain.	and administer an incision to that small one.
Mais ne faire mie ceu quant tu penses que li grains est moistes por la moistor de l’oreille, tant que tu en aies fait maintes pieces;	But do not crush it immediately if you think the grain is wet due to earwax, until you have made many pieces of it.
puis l’estrai as pinceures subtilz et au succier, si com nos avons dit, si que li estractions soit aligie.	then extract it with small tweezers and the suction, as we have said, so that the extraction is aligned.
En l’aigue donques que chiet en l’oreille covient que li malaides use d’esternuement de condisi premiers, et ample l’oreille de viel coton.	In the acute case when it is in the ear, it is necessary that the hairs use blowing of a soft condition first, and widen the ear with old cotton.
Et soit gisans sus celle oreille meisme ou li aigue est.	And let it lie across the very ear itself where the sharp is.
s’elle saut fuer per ceu, c’est boin.	If it jumps out because of the sky, it's good.
se ceu non, si prent maintes pieres selonc li longesce de ton doit tenves et legieres, et les eschaufe un poc au feu;	If not, take many small, sharp needles according to the length of your hand, and heat them slightly in the fire.
et em mette li malaides une ou pertus de son oreille, et saille sus i. de ses piez d’autre part, et fiere d’une autre piere sus la piere qui est en l’oreille;	And place the hairs one or a pinch of their ear, and go up to the other foot from its other part, and pierce with another needle through the ear which is in the ear.
et ne cesse de faire ceu de piere em piere tant que li aigue isse toute fuer, et ensi saut elle toute fuer;	And do not stop pricking with needle after needle until the sharp pain is all gone, and thus it will all go away.
et se tu vues, si prent I jonc, et boute l’un des chiés en l’oreille, et l’autre chief emprent de feu tant que li plus dou jonc soit ars;	And if you see, take a reed, and boil one of the needles in the ear, and the other head take from the fire until the thinnest reed is hard.
puis refai autreteil d’autres jons tant que li aigue isse toute, si com nos avons dit en la piere.	Then repeat the process for other joints until the sharp pain is gone, as we have said in the stone.
En l’estraction de la beste, s’elle est de petit cors, si com puce et semblans chose, cure la si com nos avons dit en la division;	In the extraction of an animal, if it is small like a mouse and similar, treat it as we have said in the division.
mais s’elle est de grant cors c’on la puisse sentir, si amenistre extraction de pinceures;	But if it is of large size that one can feel, then anesthetize extraction of pins.
et c’est li chose plus legiere a oster qui soit en l’oreille.	And the thing to remove that is in the ear is the least difficult.
En l’estraction des vers enjanrez as oreilles, quant tu lou cures si com nos avons dit en la division et ou traitier des distillations, et li cure ne profite mie, si covient que tu regardes l’oreille au soleil:	In the extraction of worms from the ears, if you treat them as we have said in the division and do not help much, then you should look at the ear in the sunlight.
s’il i apert nulz vers, si les trai as pinceures subtilz, et s’il n’aperent, si prent la cainne de coi ci est li forme:	If there are no open wounds, if they prick at their base with small needles, and if they do not open, then take the cannula of which this is the form:
Et soit estroite desoz et large desus.	And it should be tight below and wide above.
Et boute lou plus subtil chief en l’oreille selonc la quantiteit de la soffrance dou malaide, puis succe forment a tot la caine;	And push the more slender needle into the ear according to the amount of pain, then it is successful throughout the cannula;
fai ceu sovent tant que tuit li ver issent.	Do this often until all the blood flows out.
Et s’il n’obeissent a issir, si estoupe entor la cainne de coton si com j’ai dit en la piere;	And if they do not obey to flow out, then apply pressure around the cannula of cotton as I have said in the stone;
et s’il ne saillent fuer si com nos avons dit, si aministre distillations que li ancien ont esprovees en l’ocision des vers, et tu les troveras ou traitier des distillations;	and if they do not succeed as we have said, then administer distillations that the ancients have experienced in the opening of veins, and you will find them where to treat distillations;
et si distille tes oiles et tes medicines en l’oreille a tout cest estrument, de coi ci est li forme si com tu vois:	And if you drip your oils and medicines into the ear of this instrument, as you see here:
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain estrois desoz a I petis pertuis, et desus overs por distiller;	And it should be made of silver or tin with small holes below and larger ones above to drip;
et por presser dedens la distillation a I estrument d’arain bien fait por ceu, et se tu vues pren I raseur et envoloupe entor la pointe avenanment coton;	And to press within the distillation of the tin instrument well made for this purpose, and if you see take the razor and wrap it evenly with cotton around the tip;
puis i giete ton oile ou ton jus, et ceu que tu vues de tes medicines en la cainne, et li caine soit en l’oreille;	Then pour your oil or juice, and whatever you see of your medicines into the canal, and the canal should be in the ear;
puis boute dedens lou raseur a tout lou coton, et presse ta main tempreement tant que li oile soit distilleit ou chevement de l’oreille;	Then press inside the razor with all the cotton, and press your hand evenly until the oil is distilled or gently from the ear;
et lou sente li malaides dedens, et soit li distillations I poc eschaufee au feu ainsois c’on la distille en l’oreille;	and the patient feels the pain inside, and the distilled water should be slightly warmed over the fire as it is poured into the ear.
et garde qu’elle ne soit trop froide, car li medicine ne seroit mie si bone.	and be careful that it is not too cold, for the medicine would not be very good.
de l’estoupement des oreilles	of ear deafness
Aucun enfant naissent qui n’ont nul pertus ens oreilles;	No child is born without any deformity in their ears.
et ceste meisme chose avient as homes par estoupement de plaie, ou de char nee dedens l’oreille, et cist estoupemens vient aucune fois em parfont en l’oreille, si c’on ne lou puet veoir;	And the same thing happens to men due to the swelling of a wound or a foreign body inside the ear, and this swelling never occurs from within the ear, if one cannot see it.
et aucune fois avient I poc defuer lou pertus, et lou voit om bien.	And the same thing never happens to the water outside of the ear, and one can see it well.
Celle donques que vient em parfont, si c’on ne la puet veoir, est de grief sanation em plusors dispositions, et en cele c’on voit covient que tu mettes l’oreille dou malaide au soleil;	Therefore, if one cannot see it, it is a severe illness in many positions, and in this one where one sees, one must put the ear of the bad hair to the sun.
et regarde dedens:	and look inside:
se tu vois l’opilation apparent, si la oevre a tot cest spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	if you see the operation apparent, if the work has all this span of time because of which here is the form:
Et soit agus et trenchans devant et derrier tout plain, si qu’il ne blece l’oreille;	And let it be smooth and thin in front and behind all plain, so that it does not blind the ear;
se li opilation est de char nee ou cors de l’oreille, si la tien as pinceures subtilz, et la cope legierement, tant que celle chars soit toute ostee.	if the operation is of bone or the ear canal, if your pinchers are thin and the coping lightly, until that bone is completely removed.
Et se li opilations est em parfont en l’oreille, si pren I raseur subtil legier et l’eschaufe un petit au feu, puis li met ou cors de l’oreille.	And if the wart is inside the ear, then take a fine razor and slightly warm it at the fire, then put it on the skin of the ear.
Se tu sens l’opilation dont li malaides sent grieteit a l’oïr, perce legierement, et garde que tu ne grever les ners de l’oreille;	If you feel the inflammation that the hairs cause pain to hear, lightly puncture, and ensure that you do not injure the nerves of the ear.
puis met en l’oreille une tente selonc la largesce dou pertus, et la moille en l’oignement egyptien.	Then place a tent according to the width of the pustule in the ear, and insert it using the Egyptian method.
Fai ceu aucun jor tant que li plaie soit soudee, ou tu pren une tente et la moille en aigue rose, et poudre sus vitriole broiet;	Do not do anything until the wound is healed, or you take a tent and insert it using acute rose, and powder above vitriol broken.
et se tu vois enflee l’oreille, si couvient que tu traies la tente et remue une autre tente moillie en cerote qui soit fait d’oile roset et de cire, tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	And if you see the ear swell, then it is advisable to remove the tent and insert another tent inserted using rose oil and wax, until the swelling is removed.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then the healer as long as they are healthy.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si plonge une esponge et drapelz en aigue froide, et le met sus l’oreille, et use d’autres cures qui oste lou decorrement de sanc qui sont ou traitier des destillations. de la char des papieres	of the charred papers
Cist althelul que vienent em papieres des eulz quant ils sont moiste et sont sec, si covient que tu les estendes de tenailles et de pinceures, et le cope d’un spatumile de ses racines;	This is the method that comes on papers from the eyes when they are wet and dry, if it is necessary to extend them with forceps and pincers, and the lid of a spatula from their roots;
puis met sor le leu vitriole broiet.	Then put on the broken glass leg.
Et se sans en decort, si le cauterize dou cautere lenticulaire subtil, et li cauterizeir aprés l’incision vaut mues;	And if without de-corticating, then cauterize the subtle lens with the fine cauterizer, and the cauterizer after the incision is valuable;
et maintes fois repairent, cant aucune chose demoure de lor racines;	and many times repair them, but nothing remains from their roots.
et quant elles sont cauterizees par feu, si sont arses celles racines et ne revienent mie.	And when they are cauterized by fire, those roots are burned and do not return.
de la gresle	of the gravel
Maintes fois vienent em papieres des eulz unes choses que semblent gresle en sa forme et en sa duresce, et por ceu est ceste maladie apelee «grandine», et est une assemblee de moistor grosse en la papiere desus et desoz;	Often in papers come things that seem gravelly in their form and hardness, and because of this disease is called "hail," and is an assembly of large moisture above and below the paper.
li ovraiges est telz:	The work is such as follows:
pren warde se li grandine se muet d’une part et d’autre, et c’est legiere chose a savoir;	Take care if the hail moves from one side to another, and this is an easy thing to know.
fent la donques dou large, puis l’escorche de chescune partie legierement, puis la prent as pinceures, et la cope.	Then make the wounds wide, then scrape each part lightly, then take them with tweezers and cover.
se tu ne la pues coper sens percier un poc la papiere, si ne grieve rien au malaide;	If you do not cover it without pricking the paper a little, it will not hurt the patient.
et se li fendure est grans, si l’assemble a une costure, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee;	If the wound is large, it should be sutured with a stitch, and the care should continue until it is healed.
et s’elle est petite, si n’i faire point de force, car li oignemens la restoure tantost et enjanre char.	If it is small, do not force it, for the wounds heal quickly and easily.
Et se li grandine est dessendans au dedens de l’oreille vers la partie desus, si enverse la papiere, et estent la grandine a unes pinceures, et la cope et presse d’une part et d’autre;	And if the grain is falling down into the inside of the ear towards the upper part, turn the paper, and catch the grain with some tweezers, and cover it and press from both sides.
et se li papiere est esloignie par l’incision, ce ne grieve rien;	And if the paper is separated by the incision, it does not matter.
et quant li grandine est copee, si leive l’oil d’aigue salee, et cure le leu de ceu qui enjanre char tant que li malaides soit sanez.	And when the grain is removed, apply a solution of strong salt water, and care for the wound until it heals.
de la graisse des eulz	of the fat of the eyes
Exinach est une graisse qui est enjanree en toiles des papieres desus, et ce avient plus as enfans c’a nules gens, et grieve mout a lor eulz, et li vienent li catharre as matinees, et ne pueent regardeir la lumiere dou soleil por ceu que les larmes se hastent a lor eulz;	Exinach is a grease that is soaked in threads of paper above, and it has more effect on children than adults, and it causes great pain to their eyes, and they have diarrhea in the morning, and they cannot look at the light of the sun because their tears rush to their eyes.
et por ceu se couchent il sor lor faices adés, et dorment sus, et sont lor papieres desoz lor sorcilz moistes que li enfleure et li apparance ont covert de l’exinach qui apert en l’oil.	And because of this, they sleep on their faces down, and lie on their backs, and their papers are moist under their pillows that the grease enters and covers them with its appearance.
Et quant tu presses lou leu a tes dois et sent l’exirnach entr’ous.	And when you press the limb to your ears and feel the cracking sound between them.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain;	And the manner of the work is such that the evils put their head in your hand;
et puis pren I drapeil de lin, et appareille une tente em maniere d’un cercle selonc la quantiteit que conteigne exirnach de chescune partie, puis le met sus li;	and then take a linen cloth, and make a tent in the shape of a circle according to the quantity that contains the external parts of each part, then put it on top of him.
et presse a tes dois d’une part et d’autre, si que li exirnach soit assemblez emmi le cercle;	and press with your fingers on both sides, so that the external parts are assembled inside the circle.
puis fent em mileu de la moistor au spatumile trenchant une fendure dou large, et ne soit mie plus grans que li plaie c’on fait a la sainie de voinne;	then make in the middle of the moisture with a sharp spatula a cut of a wide size, and it should not be any wider than the wound that is made at the vein opening.
et fent le cuir em parfont tant que tu veignes a l’exirnach;	and make the skin in front until you reach the external parts.
et em plusors dispositions vient exirnach de la fendure, selonc la forme d’une piece de graisse blainche.	and in many positions come the external parts of the cut, in the shape of a piece of white fat.
Estrai la donques a tout une piece de drap charpit entre tes dois au defuer, et torne ta main a destre et a senestre tant qu’il soit espars;	Extract the bandage from all over the piece of cloth between your two hands, and turn your hand to the right and left until it is spread out.
et garde que tu n’ajoster en la fendure, que tu ne viegnes a tout le spatumile jusc’a l’oil, que tu ne le bleces.	And make sure you do not tuck it into the wound, that you do not bring the whole length of the bandage to the oil, that you do not hurt it.
Et se li exirnach n’apert en l’encomencement de la fendure, si acroi un poc la fendure legierement tant qu’il apere;	And if it does not open at the beginning of the wound, slightly scratch the wound until it opens.
puis l’estrai si com nos avons dit, puis moille drapelz en aisil et en aigue, et met sus le leu, et estrain de bendelz.	Then extract it as we have said, then wipe the bandages in soft and sharp, and put on the limb, and spread out evenly.
Et si a de tels homes qui broient seil et mettent sus por corrompre cele moistor qui est demoree.	And if there are such men who breathe and place on to corrupt the moisture that is remaining.
Puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then, let the healer as long as they are healthy.
Et s’il vient au leu aposteme chaut, si lou cure d’emplaustres assouajant tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the healer comes to the abscess, let them apply wet dressings until they are healthy.
des poilz des papieres	of hairs of papers
Quant em papieres naissent poilz ajostez autre que li naturez, et sont enveillit, si nuisent as eulz, et font venir manieres de maladies si com larmes acostumees et mollifications des papieres et albugine, tant que c’est cause de la destruction des eulz;	When hairs are artificially placed or arranged other than their natural way, and are awakened, they can harm the eyes, and bring about diseases such as tears accustomed to and softening of the papers and cornea, until this is caused by the destruction of the eyes.
et est li cure selonc IIII manieres:	And there are four ways of treatment:
ou par cautere ensamble feu, ou par medicine ague selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre de cautere, et est fais ou par incision et costure ou par caines, selonc ceu que je dirai.	or by cauterization with fire together, or by medicine as the case may be, according to what is before or in the chapter of cauterization, and it is done either by incision and stitching, or by caines, according to what I will say.
Il covient que tu mettes lou chief dou malaide en ton sain, puis torne la papiere de l’oil a ta main senestre;	It is necessary for you to place the head of the hairs in your hand, then return the paper of the oil to your right hand;
s’elle est convertie, c’est boin;	If she is converted, it is good;
se ceu non, si i boute une aguille a tout I fil desus;	if not, then prick with a needle at the top of each thread;
et soit ce delez la marge de la papiere ou li poil naissent delez ces poilz, et trai I fil au desus a tout la papiere, et la torne au raseur;	and let it be either on the edge of the paper or where the hair grows above these hairs, and pull the thread up from under the paper, and turn the blade to the razor;
puis fent en la partie desoz la papiere, desoz les poilz ajostez, a tout le spatumile copant, des le grant larmier jusc’au petit;	then cut in the part outside the paper, outside the hairs, and smooth out the skin, from the large arm to the small one;
puis estrai I fil, et met desoz la papiere une petite tente de couton et de drapeil, puis seigne sus la papiere une figure d’enche, si com la fuelle de mirte, et toutevoie il covient que li figure soit selonc la quantiteit que tu vues eslever la papiere qui est devisez a toz.	then pull the thread, and place outside the paper a small cotton and linen tent, then above the paper, a figure of a wheel, like the fuller's wheel, and all the while it should be according to the quantity that you saw raise the paper which is divided into each one.
Et si a teil qui a mestier c’on cope grant quantiteit de la papiere selonc ceu que li papiere est mollifie;	And if for a person who has skill, one should copiously apply a great quantity of paper according to how the paper is softened;
puis fent a tout le spatumile sus les II lignes que tu as signiet, et comence des lou grant larmier jusc’a petit;	then make all the space above the two lines that you have marked, and begin from the large calf to the small;
et soit li une des fendures pres des poilz naturez en la groissece d’un raiz, puis boute l’oncine en l’un des II angles dou keur, puis l’escorche toute;	and let one of the cuts be near the hairs naturally in the large root, then bury the needle in one of the two angles of the curve, then scrape the whole;
puis assemble les II levres a une costure d’une aguille a tout I fil de laine subtil, et essue le sanc, et fai aerdre la superfluiteit des filz sus les II sorcilz a tout aucunes choses gluans, se tu vues faire ce;	then gather the two lips to one stitch of a needle with all the thread of fine linen, and suck the blood, and remove the excess hairs above the two edges at any things glued, if you see this being done.
et se ce non, si n’en aies cure, puis laisse la costure et les filz jusc’a III jors ou IIII;	and if not, then do not worry about it, leave the stitches and threads in place for three or four days.
puis cure la plaie sens costure de choses sechans et constrignans, car li papiere se relive au soudement de la plaie et l’assemblement de li, mais li costure est muedre (si com dirent li ancien), et c’est ovraiges sens paor;	then heal the wound from the side of the stitches with dry and constricting substances, because the paper swells at the moment of the wound and brings together the parts, but the stitches are dissolved (as the ancients said), and this is without fear.
et si a une autre maniere:	and if another way:
et est que tu seignes la papiere d’une figure qui soit ausi com li fuelle de mirte, si com nos avons conteit, a III oncines desevrez selonc la forme qui est ci:	and you should shape the paper into a form that is like the fleece of wool, as we have described, and cut it into three pieces according to the form that is here:
puis cope ceu qui sormonte as petites forces igalment selonc la forme qui est ci:	then copper which surmounts as small equal forces according to the form which is here:
Et se tu n’as pooir de tenir les tenailles, et li chose n’est mie igalz, si prent une aguille ou il ait I fil, et la boute emmi la figure;	And if you cannot hold the needles, and the thing is not even, take a needle or one with a thread, and bring it into the shape.
et boute I autre fil delez lou grant larmier, et lou secont fil delez lou petit, et assemble entre tes dois les filz igalment;	and put another thread over the large arm, and the second thread over the small one, and bring the threads together evenly between your two fingers.
puis lieve ta main igalment, et lieve tout le cuir sus coi tu as signiet, si com nos avons conteit, puis assemble les II levres de la plaie par costure, et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	then lift your hand evenly, and lift the skin over where you have sewn, as we have said, then gather the two lips of the wound by stitching, and treat it until it is healed.
et se aposteme vient a ton incision, si l’apaise de cerote et de semblans oignement assouajans;	and if an abscess comes to your incision, soothe it with ointments and similar soothing substances.
et aucune fois avient que li poil de la papiere sont convertit:	and never has it happened that the hairs of the paper are converted.
si covient que tu uses ceu que nos avons dit de l’incision;	if you should use what we have said about incision;
mais li costure en l’une et en l’autre est plus artificialz.	but the stitching in one and the other is more artificial.
Li cure des caines si est selonc ceste forme:	The treatment of wounds is as follows:
et est que tu convertisses la papiere et la fent dedens selonc ceu que j’ai dit, et puis fai II caines par art, et II liiens subtilz ausi lonc com li papiere et li largesce dou spatumile est;	and you should convert the paper and make the incision inside as I have said, then make two wounds by art, and two ligatures as thin as the paper and the width of the space is;
et cope as II chiés de II pars ou tu tiens les filz;	and tie them as the two threads of which you hold the thread;
puis assemble l’un et l’autre subtilment sus ceu que sormonte de la papiere de l’oil, et estrain les II cainnes des II parties forment;	then bring them together thinly above the paper of the oil, and strain the two wounds from the two parts formed;
et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, et li cuir qui iert estrainte morra et nercira et porrira, tant qu’il cherra par lui.	and it leaves it thus for several days, and the skin that is stretched will die and rot and putrefy, until it falls off from it.
S’il tarde, si le cope a unes forces, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	If it takes too long, if the copper has some strength, then cure it until it is healed.
et quant li plaie iert soudee, et si ert levee li papiere, et ne poindront plus li poil;	And when the wound is soaked, and if it is raised with paper, and they will not grow back.
et c’est li forme des II cainnes que tu feras selonc ceste figure, et selonc ceste quantiteit de lonc et de large:	And this is the shape of the two needles that you will make according to this figure, and according to this quantity of length and width:
li ovraiges est telz que tu preignes une aguille subtil, et i boute I fil de soie souef et subtil;	The work is such that you grasp a thin needle, and pull the silk thread soft and thin;
puis assemble les chiés et noe l’un et l’autre subtilment, et soit li longesce des filz une palme de lonc;	Then gently gather the shoulder blades and bend them slightly, and let the arms hang down by their own length, a span long.
puis ordene en la chasse I autre fil subtil de soie briément, et noe les chief dou fil;	Then order the other arm to be raised quickly and slightly, and bend the shoulder blades of the other arm.
puis mette li malaides son chief en ton sain;	Then put the misaligned joints in their proper place.
et soit delez lou soleil si que li ovraiges soit declairiez, car c’est uns ovraiges subtilz et menus, puis boute l’aguille a tout la chasse en la racine dou poil ajosteit, et la fai percier en la papiere hastanment tant que tu la traies desus lou poil natureil;	And let the work be done in the shade so that the work is not too difficult, for it is a delicate and small task, then push the needle through the entire arm at the base of the hair, and pierce it gently into the paper until you draw it out above the natural hair.
puis estrai le poil jusque sus la chasse, et boute en la chasse celui poil, s’il en i a I ou II ou III ou plusors;	Then remove the hair up to the skin, and cut off the hair that is in the skin, if there is one or two or three or more.
puis estrai ta main tant que li poilz veigne fuers a tout la chasse en la papiere avec lou poil natureil.	Then remove your hand until the hairs come out of all the skin in the paper with the natural hair.
Et se li chasse est traite et li poilz ne vient fuer avec li, si trairas la chasse au desoz a tout le fil que tu i as ordeneit, tant que li chasse veigne fuer dou pertus desus et que tu la voies par la vision de l’oil;	And if the skin is treated and the hairs do not come out with it, then treat the skin with the discharge until it comes out completely and you can see through the oil.
adonques si trairas la chasse et le fil, et clo l’oil et lou laisse clo II jors ou III, tant que li poil s’aerde en son leu et naisse li char sus;	Then treat the skin and the thread, and close the oil and leave it closed for two or three days, until the hair grows back in its place and grows on top.
et se li poilz est petis, si acompaigne I poil lonc des chevoulz naturez, et soit alevez avec celui ou tu le laisse, tant qu’il soit eslongiez et puis le lieve.	If the hairs are short, accompany them with long hairs from goats, and lift them with that which you leave, until they are lengthened and then let it go.
de la porriture de l’oil	of the stirring of the oil
Quant ceste maladie qui est apelee «aleacrati» ou li porriture vient en l’oil, si en i a de II manieres:	When this disease, which is called "aleacrati" or the pimples, comes in the oil, there are two ways:
l’une natureil, et l’autre innatureil.	one natural, and the other unnatural.
Et avient par soudement de plaie, ou de tailleure ou de cautere, et par semblans choses.	And it comes by wounding, or cutting, or cauterization, and similar things.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige en li est que tu fendes celle soudure, et dessevre les levres de li, et met dedens tentes de lin, et la lie tant qu’elle soit sanee;	And the way of the work in it is that you break that sewage, and dehydrate the lips from it, and put inside tents of linen, and hold it until it is healed.
et ne covient mie que tu uses en la cure de li de choses que sechent et restraignent.	and you should only use in the treatment of it things that dry and restrict.
Car se tu fais ceu, si revient li maladie pire que li premiere;	If you do this, the disease returns worse than the first;
mais i oevre de choses amollissans, si com fenugreic;	but I work with things that soften, like fenugreek;
et l’arose d’aigue ou altee et semence de lin soient cuites, et oignemens dyaquilon fondut en aucun des oiles, et i envoloupe une tente, et le cure de ceu.	and the rose of sharp or high and seed of linen be cooked, and stinging nettle boiled in any of the oils, and it is wrapped in a tent, and the cure for this.
Et li tresors de ta cure si est que tu te dones en garde qu’ele ne soude mie selonc la forme qu’elle fut devant;	And the treasures of your cure are that you take care not to let it spoil according to the form it was before;
et cist ovraiges que nos avons dit nen est fuers que adresemens de ceste maladie, qu’elle ne reviegne selonc la forme qu’elle fut devant.	and these works that we have said are only to bring it back to the form it was before.
de la char qui vient en l’oil	of the oil that comes in the ear
Ceste maladie que est desoz qui vraiement est apelee «axacrati», et est naturelz et accidens.	This disease that is truly called "axacrati", and is natural and accidental.
Li accidens vient de plaie et de fendure et de cautere et de choses semblans;	The accident comes from wounds and cuts and cauterization and similar things.
et li voie de l’ovraige en li si est que tu preignes un aguille, en coi il ait I fil double, et la fiche en la char, et li fai percier des le senestre larmier tant c’a destre, si que li filz veigne en II chiés de la char;	And the method of the work is such that you hold a needle with a double thread, and the thread in the shuttle, and make it pierce from the right arm to the left, so that the thread comes out on both sides.
puis estent la char au desus a tout l’aguille, et la cope a I spatumile large.	Then the shuttle is above all the needle, and the copes at the span width.
Et se li figure de la papiere revient selonc ceu qu’il covient, c’est boin;	And if it appears like paper according to what is necessary, it is good.
se ceu non, si pren I raseur et le met en la fendure, et torne la papiere, et fent II fendures ou costeit dedens la papiere;	If not, take the razor and put it in the cut, and turn the paper, and make two cuts or where it costs inside the paper.
et soient li chiés des II fendures des II angles de l’incision que tu as copeit, et soit fais uns angles si que quant elles sont assemblees, que li figure soit ausi com li figure d’une lettre qui a non «I griesche»;	et soient les chiés des deux fendures des deux angles de l'incision que tu as copeit, et fais des angles si que lorsque elles sont assemblées, que le figure soit ausi com le figure d'une lettre qui a non «I griesche»;
puis oste celle char, selonc la quantiteit que ses costez est agus desoz, de ceu qui enseut la papiere, puis ajoste les II parties desevrees, et les cout d’un fil de lainne;	then remove that char, according to the quantity that its cost is of, from what teaches the paper, then add the two parts severed, and the cut of a thread of linen;
puis lou cure de ceu que nos avons dit des medicines mollifians, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez.	then apply the care that we have said about the softening medicines and tents, until it is healed.
Et se li maladie vient de fendure ou de costure ou de cautere, si covient que tu fendes une fendure plainne desoz les poilz des papieres, et selonc ceu qui est ci devant;	And if the disease comes from a cut or stitch or cauterization, then it is necessary that you make a plain cut outside of the hairs of the paper, and according to what is above;
puis desevre entre les II leivres d’une tente, si com j’ai dit;	Then separate between the two leaves of a tent, as I have said.
et doit on faire l’ovraige selonc la forme de la maladie, car elle est mout diverse en forme, et li saiges maistres appareille engien de tout som pooir coment il faice revenir la figure a sa forme natureil;	And one should perform the operation according to the form of the disease, for it is very diverse in shape, and the wise masters compare all possible means to how they can make the figure return to its natural shape.
et li malaides meisme, selonc ceu qu’il i covient d’ovraige et d’estrumens em plusors dispositions.	And the misaligned joints themselves, according to what is necessary for operation and instruments in many positions.
dou soudement de la papiere	and of the paper
Quant ceste soudure avient a mains homes en teil maniere que li papiere desus est sodee avec le blanc de l’oil, et ne puet movoir ne faire ses ovraiges naturez, si covient donques que tu i boutes la pointe d’un raseur desoz la papiere, et la lieve en haut;	When this sewing is done by hand in a somewhat manner that the paper above is glued with the white of an egg, and cannot move or do its natural workings, then it is necessary that you bring the point of a razor outside the paper, and lift it up.
et l’estent as pinceures, tant que tu copes ceu qui est aert au spatumile subtil, qui ne soit mie trop agus ne trop trenchans, si que li malaides ne puisse soffrir que li spatumile trop agus ne blecent l’oil;	and it is set with pins, until you copy what is on the needle's subtle edge, which should not be too sharp or too blunt, so that the pain does not suffer from the needle being too sharp or too dull.
et soit ton incision, dont tu escorche celle assemblee, legierement, si que li papiere reviegne selonc sa forme natureil;	and let your incision, from which you scrape that assembly, lightly, so that the paper returns to its natural shape.
et est sanee toute celle assemblee, et font aucune fois en l’oil aigue salee, et le leve d’aigue douce, et de coliere;	and it is healed completely, and never in the sharp salt oil, and lift it with the gentle sweet, and of vinegar.
puis met entre la papiere et l’oil une tente de lin, et met sus l’oil laine moillie en abun d’uef;	then place between the paper and oil a linen cloth, and place above the oil wool moistened with plenty of honey.
et aprés le tier jor use dou coliere et des choses soudans tant qu’il soit sanez.	and after the third day, use a cold compress and unclean things until they are healed.
de l’ungle de l’oil	of the elbow joint of the oil
Saiches que li ungle est selonc II manieres:	There are two ways to do it:
elle est nervouse et semblans a I dur syfac, et une autre qui n’est mie nervouse, mais est semblans a blainche moistor congelee, que quant on la touche de fer et on la cuide panre as pinceures, si ne puet om;	It is either nervous and similar to the hard sphacelus, or it is not nervous but similar to a white frozen moisture, which when touched with iron and cut with knives, does not move.
et l’une et l’autre semblance encomence devers le grant larmier, et croist poc et poc tant qu’ele cuevre toute la veue et toute la lumiere et le movement de l’oil.	Both start from the great arm and grow slowly until they cover the entire eye and light and movement of the oil.
Et li maniere de l’incision si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, puis li oevre les eulz;	And the manner of incision is that the evil ones put their head in your healthy place, then they work the eyes.
et lieve la papiere a ta main, puis coil l’ungle as pinceures de petite doubleure, et l’estent au desus;	and gently hold the paper to your hand, then bend the angle with small forceps, and extend it above;
puis pren une aguille, et i met I poil de cheval, ou de vaiche, ou de buef, et I fil fort;	then take a needle, and put horsehair, or goat hair, or beef hair, and thread it tightly;
et double la pointe de l’aguille un poc et la fiche emmi l’ungle, et la perce a tout l’aguille, et lie l’ungle d’un fil et l’estent au desus, et escorche a tout lou poil le costeit de l’ungle qui enseut la prunele et la soie au poil jusc’au chief, puis cope lou remanant en la racine dou larmier a tout lou spatumile subtil et as petites forces, et laisse la char natureil ou larmier, si que par l’incision ne veigne li cors des larmes acostumeement;	and double the tip of the needle a little and insert it into the angle, and push the needle through the entire angle, and tie the angle with a thread and extend it above, and scrape all the hair on the side of the angle that faces the prickle and silk to the skin at the top, then cut the remaining in the root of the arm at every subtle hair and with small forces, and leave the natural flesh or the arm, so that by the incision it does not usually bleed;
et aucune fois s’estent li ungle a l’oncine soulement, et au fil, si com nos avons dit;	and never has the joint remained out of place alone, and over time, as we have said.
puis l’escorche on a tout le spatumile souef de coi ci est li forme:	then the skin is removed to reveal all the soft tissue that gives it its shape:
Et garde que li spatumile ne touche la toile charnue et la rompe, et que li prunele ne soit percie;	And beware that the soft tissue does not touch the raw flesh and break it, and that the bone is not pierced;
et aprés l’incision giete en l’oil un poc de seil broiet, et dou coliere fait de litargire, et le laisse jusc’a l’autre jor;	and after the incision pour in a little broken silk oil, and a poultice made of litharge, and let it rest on the other side;
puis le cure de ceu qu’il i covient tant qu’il soit sanez.	then the care that is needed until it is healed.
Et se li ungle n’est mie nervouse, et tu ne pues bouter l’aguille, et li uncines n’i puet entrer, maintes fois est curee ceste semblance d’ungle de medicines;	And if the joint is not nervous, and you cannot insert the needle, and the incisions cannot enter, often this remedy of joints is cured by medicines;
et naissent sicom j’ai conteit en la division, et se tu la vues coper, si oevre l’oil dou malaide, et pren le spatumile legier poc agut selonc ceste forme:	and grow like I have described in the previous section, and if you see it covered, work with the oil of the hairs, and take the sharp needle lightly as follows:
Et reis l’ungle desus subtilment, et se tu vois qu’elle amenuise point et li rasion i apresse, si distille de ta bouche en l’oil coliere fait de litargire et dou coliere rouge et seil broiet, et estoupe l’oil jusc’a l’autre jor;	and gently scrape the edge above, and if you see that it does not soften and the razor is sharp, then drip from your mouth into the oil of the candle made of litargire and the red wax and silk thread, and stir the oil just after;
puis rencomence l’autre ovraige selonc ceste meisme oevre, tant qu’elle soit toute ostee.	then begin the other work according to this same work, until it is completely open.
Se aucune chose ne t’est contraire en l’oil, si com aposteme chaus, adonques la lait, et cure premier l’aposteme chaut tant qu’il soit sanez, puis rencomence l’ovraige si com devant, tant qu’il soit sanez.	If nothing is contrary in the oil, such as an abscess, then milk it, and first cure the abscess until it is healed, then continue the work as before, until it is completely healed.
Et se li apparance de la chair dou larmier nuit en l’oil par grant nuisement, si la sospent a l’oncine, et en cope une partie et non mie tot, que cors de larmes n’i viegne;	and if the appearance of the flesh of the arm appears in the oil by great harm, then remove it at once, and take a part and not all at once, so that tears do not come to it;
puis distille en l’oil coliere rouge qui est fais de litargire.	Then apply a red wine oil infusion made of litargire.
de la char qui naist sus la prunelle	of the flesh that grows above the pupil
Es eulz d’aucuns homes naist aucune fois char rouge, et cuevre la prunele et restraint sus les papieres et les torne au defuer, et semble une rose de balauste;	Some men are born with no red hair, and cover the prunelle and hold it above the papers and turn them to the defuer, and it seems like a baldust rose.
et li ovraiges si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, puis li oevre les eulz, et coil toute celle char as uncines convenaubles a ceu, et la sostien a la force;	And the work is such that the hairs put their head in your clean, then they do the eyes, and with all that red hair, it is convenient for this, and support it at the force.
puis cope la premiere char, et vai tout copant au raseur jusc’a la fin, et te garde que tu ne bleces l’oil a l’ovraige;	Then cover the first hair, and go all scraping to the razor just at the end, and make sure you do not smear the oil at the work.
et soit li incision dou spatumile que nos avons dit en l’incision de l’ungle et as petites forces de coi on oste lou sebel, si com li forme aprés cest chapistre lou demostre;	and let the incision be made with the space-like method that we have mentioned in the incision of the nail and with small forces to remove the base, as it forms after this chapter demonstrates.
et quant li incision est acomplie et ostee toute li char, si emple l’oil de seil broiet ou tu i distille coliere rouge et semblans medicines corrosives, et met sus l’oil defuer coton avec abin d’uef, si qu’il soit asseurez d’aposteme chaut;	and when the incision is made and all the char is removed, use the oil of silk that you distill or red mercury and similar corrosive medicines, and put it on top of the oil with cotton wool, so that it is ensured to be a healthy wound.
et s’il i demore rien, et li sans chaus te sormonte, et tu doutes aposteme chaut, si laisse l’oil et cure l’aposteme de choses apaisant aposteme chaut;	and if nothing remains and the sinus is overhanging, and you doubt an abscess is forming, leave the oil and treat the abscess with calming remedies for a healthy wound.
puis revien a ton ovraige tant qu’il soit sanez, et ensi fai cant chars est ajostee en l’oil par ceste semblance.	Then return to your work until it is healed, and thus make the same charms cast into oil by this similarity.
Mais toutevoie il covient que tu aliges la cure de chescun oil foible de la voie natureil;	But it is necessary that you add the cure of each weak oil from its natural source;
et de la voie accident, en ovraige de fer;	and of the accidental way, in ironwork;
et ne bouter mie ta main en aucun de ces ovraiges tant que tu voies que cist membres soit soffrans celui ovraige.	and do not put your hand into any of these workings until you see that this limb is suffering from that working.
des voines des eulz	of the eyes
Sebel sont voinnes rouges que sont covertes sus l’oil, et tolent a la veue son ovraige et afoiblissent l’oil toz jors.	which are red veins that cover over the eye, and take away its work and weaken the eye always.
Mestier est donques au premier que tu regardes se li oil, en coi sebel est, est fors, et n’i a autre maladie fuers que lou sebel;	The work is therefore to the first that you look at this oil, in which previously was, and outside, and there is no other disease besides the previous one;
adonques le coil en teil maniere:	then the joint should be bent in a certain way:
comande au malaide qu’il mette son chief en ton sain, puis sospent celles voines a tout l’oncine selonc sa sapience, et soit li oncines subtilz double selonc ceste forme:	instruct the patient to put his head in your healthy hand, then bend those vertebrae along the spine according to their wisdom, and let the vertebrae be slightly doubled according to this form:
Et soient dui oncine par degrez en I cors selonc ceste forme:	And let them be done twice a degree in one course according to this form:
puis c’on coil as forces celles voinnes subtilment, et essue lou sanc houre aprés autre, tant que tu voies removoir celles voines fuers de l’oil;	then bend those vertebrae gently, and squeeze the blood out of them hour after hour, until you can remove those vertebrae from the joint;
et garde que tu ne blecier l’oil as pointes des spatumiles, et fai cest ovraige a houre de midi devant lou soleil, et soies mout fervans en ton ovraige si que tu ne copes fuer que celles voinnes;	and be careful not to bleed the joint with sharp points of the spatula, and do this work at noon in front of the sun, and be very hot in your work so that you do not cut those vertebrae;
et quant tu avras ce fait, si distille en l’oil coliere vert et rouge por corrumpre ceu qui est demorez dou sebel.	And when you have done this, if you distill green and red oil of turpentine to corrupt the humor that remains above.
Et se tu n’as pooir de coillir tout ceu en celle houre, si fai emplastre sus l’oil de choses apaisans la dolor des eulz, et le laisse aucuns jors tant que li dolors soit apaisie et soit asseurez d’aposteme chaut, puis rencomence selonc ceste maniere qui est devant tant qu’il soit sanez;	And if you cannot collect all the humor in that hour, then make a poultice on the oil of things calming the pain of the eyes, and let it stay for some time until the pain is eased and the abscess is securely healed, then continue according to this method until they are healed;
et c’est li forme des forces:	and this is the form of the forces:
de la fistule de l’oil	of the oil fistula
Li mire si nomment «arissati» fistule:	The master calls it "arissati" fistula:
quant tu la cures per cautere et par medicine ague ardant selonc ceu que j’ai devant dit, et elle n’est mie sanee, si est engien en li que tu fendes sus l’aposteme, lai ou il doit meurer, et trai toute la moistor que i est, tant que li os soit descovers.	When you cure it by cauterization and with medicine boiling according to the humor that I have before said, and it is not healed, then engage in what you did above the abscess, where it should rot, and remove all the moisture that is there, until the bone is discovered.
Et quant li os iert descovers, et tu verras la corruption et la noiror, si la reis a tout l’estrument de coi ci est li forme;	And when the tooth is exposed, and you see the corruption and the blackness, if the forceps of all the instruments used here are in its form;
et est apelez «aspre chief», et soit fait de feir inde a I chief reont, et soit pointoiez si com une lime si com il est en la presente forme:	and it is called "rough file," and it should be made of iron from the same as the tooth, and it should be pointed as a needle, as it is in the present form:
Et met sus lou leu de l’os corrumput, puis le torne entre tes dois, et presse ta main un poc tant que tu saiches que celle corruption est rese;	And put it on the surface of the rotten tooth, then turn it between your fingers, and press your hand a little until you feel that that corruption is removed;
et fai ceu aucune fois, puis restoure lou leu de medicines exiccatives.	and do not do it again, then restore the tooth with drying remedies.
se li leus est soudez, et char i naist, et li cors de la bowe est soudez, et remaint ensi XL jors, et il ne renovele et n’est mie apostemez, et accidens mavais n’i vient, saiches qu’il est sanez;	If the joint is reset and the limb is straight, and the body of the bow is straight, it remains thus for forty days, and it does not recur and is not postponed, and no bad accident happens to it, so it is considered healed.
se ceu non, si n’i a autre engien que de ramener la fistule au pertus dou neif selonc ceste forme:	If not, there is no other means than to return the fistula to its proper position according to this form:
et est que tu descuevre de l’os la seconde fois par fer, et par medicines agues, et quant il iert descovers si prent I foret selonc ceste forme, et soit li chiés de fer a III angles, et li fust soit atenuis jusc’a chief si com tu vois ci:	And you must dislocate the bone the second time with iron and with medicines, and when it is discovered, take the fork according to this form, and the nail should be bent at three angles, and the fistula should be attenuated from the top as you see here:
puis le met sus l’os delez lou larmier, et esloigne ta main de l’oil I poc, puis torne a tot le foret tant qu’il perce l’os et le sent li malaides par ceu que li vens en ist s’il tient sa main sus son neif;	Then place it on top of the bone of the arm, and move your hand away from the oil and pores, then turn to the full extent of the forearm until it pierces the bone and the patient feels pain as it comes in that position if he holds his hand above his shoulder.
et pues restoure lou leu de medicines seches, si com je t’ai ensigniet, et quant li char naist et endurcist li leus, si vait li matiere au neif;	And then restore the joint of dry medicines as I have indicated, and when the char is born and hardens the limbs, it goes to the shoulder.
si est plus legiere chose au malaide.	If it is a lighter thing for the pain.
de l’issue de l’oil	from the oil
Quant li eulz apert fuer dou tout en tout, et il ne vient point de destorbier au nef, ne amenuisement, si covient que tu lies lou malaide;	When the eyes are wide open all at once, and it does not come to dislocate at the shoulder, nor is it discomforting, then you must bind the pain.
puis le saine, puis li met ventouses ou haterel sens ferir por succier, puis met sus l’oil I liien fait d’acaice et de aloe et d’encens et de sarcocolle, et puis estrain l’oil, et l’emplaustre sus de bendes et de drapelz;	then the healthy one, then it places leeches or hatchets to draw blood, then it applies oil mixed with acid, aloe, incense, and sarcocollis, and then strains the oil, and applies the ointment with bandages and cloths;
et li maniere des drapelz si est que tu preignes drapelz assez molz, et double chescun en IIII, et puis met l’un sus l’autre selonc la quantiteit que li eulz en ait mestier;	and the way of the cloths is that you press cloths that are enough soft, and double each one into four, and then place one on top of the other according to the quantity they have to do;
puis l’estrain par desus d’un bendeil dur forment, et rencomence les ventouses por succier sens ferir;	then strain it through a cloth that is strong and firm, and then restart the leeches to draw blood;
puis oste les ventouses et laisse l’oil estraint jor et nuit, et se li liiens amolist, si covient que tu l’estraignes mout;	then remove the suction cups and let the oil remain on it day and night, and if the joints are dislocated, it is necessary to strongly restrain them.
puis oste lou liien aprés le jor et la nut, et se tu vois l’oil repairier, c’est boin;	then remove the joint after the day and night, and if you see the oil return, it is good.
se ce non;	if not;
si rencomence l’emplaustre et les drapelz et lou liien et les ventouses tant qu’il soit sanez.	then restart the plaster and bandages and the joint and the suction cups until they are healed.
dou derrompement de toile uvee	For the tearing of a vein, instruct the patient to let the hairs grow long and even; and if
Quant disruptions vient en la toile uvee, puis apert, et vient fuer des papieres si com I grain de resins, et est espoantauble a veoir;	When dislocations occur in the woven cloth, then open it, and come forth with papers like the grain of resin, and is expansible to see.
adonques se tu la vues coper, li ovraiges est telz que tu boutes une aguille en la racine des la partie desoz jusc’a celi desus, puis boute une autre aguille ou il ait I fil double des la partie dou larmier;	then if you see the joint, the work is such that you should poke a needle into the root of the part below this one above, then poke another needle where the tendon of the elbow is double.
et la fai percier, et laisse la premiere aguille selonc la disposition;	and make it pierce, and let the first needle follow its position;
puis cope lou leu dou fil double et lie une partie de l’uve entor, et l’estraint bien, puis estrai l’aguille et met sus l’oil lainne moillie en abun d’uef;	then cover the arm with a piece of cloth and tie it tightly, then pull out the needle and put oil on the wound in abundance.
et le laisse tant que li filz chiece avec l’uve, puis cure l’oil de choses confortans tant que li plaie soit sanee;	and let it stay until the child's wound heals with the cloth, then care for the oil with comforting things until the wound is healed.
et aucune fois li plaie est restrainte par l’uve chescune part d’un cercle de drap, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	and never a wound is restrained by the use of each part of a circle of cloth, until it is healed.
Et se li eulz done grant apparance, si le perce au spatumile subtil qui viegne em parfont de l’oil, et corre la moistor albuginé et dessende li eulz, et entre ens tantost;	And if they appear very large, then pierce the thin spatula that comes from the oil, and wipe away the yellowish moisture and clean the hairs, and enter immediately.
puis l’estrai tant qu’il soit sanez.	then extract it until it is healed.
de la bowe de l’oil	from under the oil
Ceste maladie qui est apelee «alcunnati» nen est fuers que bowe qui est assemblee en l’oil, semblant a aigue dessendant, et ce n’est mie aigue;	This disease which is called "alcunnati" is nothing more than boils that are gathered in the oil, resembling sharp droplets, and it is not sharp.
et li maniere de l’apparance de l’ovraige si est que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege appareilliet et droit, puis prent le chief entre tes mains de II pars, et lou muef tant que tu voies la bowe venir au desus a tes eulz;	and the manner of the appearance of the work is such that you make the dislocated joint sit properly on its seat and straight, then take the head between your hands from both sides, and move it until you see the bone coming above to your eyes;
puis soit ens fichie, et ne dessende et soit descombree li lumiere, et voie li malaides les choses si com il soloit;	then let it be released, and do not descend and be disassembled the light, and see the dislocated things as they should be;
et s’elle ne dessent desoz, saiches que c’est aigue, et se li dessendemens de la bowe n’est appareilliez si com nos avons dit.	and if it does not descend, then it is acute, and do not straighten the bone as we have said.
si fai seoir lou malaide entre tes mains, puis prent le spatumile subtil et fent sus la toile cornee I poc par la continuation de la conjunctive avec la toile cornee et la corone, tant que li bowe isse;	then make the dislocated joint between your hands, then take the thin spatula and put it under the eye lid from the continuation of the conjunctiva with the eyelid and the eyebrow, until the bone is;
et quant elle ert issue, si distille en l’oil aigue chaude mellee a miel, ou aigue ou fenugreic est boillis et miel, puis soit curee d’autre cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	et when she was born, if she is distilled in hot vinegar mixed with honey, or hot or fenugreek is boiled and honey, then she is cured of other cures until she is healed.
des aigues de l’oil	of the oils of the oil
Nos avons jai les semblances des aigues en la division, et ceu qu’il covient por percier;	We have similarities in the divisions, and what is needed to pierce it.
si en oevre selonc la santeit.	if in work according to health.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains croisiet, fuers de la lumiere por le soleil, et li lie l’oil sain et estreint mout fort;	It is necessary that you make the pain between your crossed hands sit, outside of the light for the sun, and the oil is clean and tightened very tightly.
puis met la papiere de l’oil a ta main senestre se li eulz est senestres, ou a ta main destre se li eulz est destres;	Then put the paper of the oil to your right hand if the eyes are on the right, or to your left hand if the eyes are on the left.
puis prent en ta main destre, se li eulz est senestres, l’estrument qui est apelez «almagda», ou a ta main senestre, se li eulz est destre;	then take in your right hand, if the eyes are on the left, the tool called «almagda», or in your left hand, if the eyes are on the right.
puis met la pointe de l’estrument delez la corone par la groissece d’un rait en celle blenchor de l’oil a la partie dou menor larmier, puis boute l’estrument qui est apelez «almagda» vertuousement, et trestorne ta main tant qu’il perce en la blenchor de l’oil, et sente que almagda viegne a la chose vuide;	then place the tip of the tool above the crown by the thickness of a pen in the part of the oil that is called «almagda», then strike the tool called «almagda» firmly, and withdraw your hand until it pierces into the part of the oil, and feel that «almagda» is empty;
et covient que li mesure de la voie almagda soit au parfont de la mesure des l’espaice qui est des la prunele jusc’a la fin de la noirour;	and it is necessary that the measure of the opening «almagda» be at the length of the space from the nail to the end of the finger.
et c’est li corone de l’oil;	and this is the crown of oil;
si verras l’os en celle papiere por la clarteit de la toile cornee, et pues met l’estrument jusc’a leu ou li aigue est, puis l’espresse desoz une voie aprés autre.	if you see the bone in that paper for the clarity of the cloth, then put the instrument just above it where it is sharp, and press out the blood one after another through a hole.
se li aigue dessent maintenant, si voit li malaides devant lui et l’estrument en son oil.	if he is now sharp, then he sees the hairs in front of him and the instrument in his eye.
Aprés repose I petit, et se li aigue remonte la seconde voie, met la fuer avec l’estrument, et quant elle est ens fichie et ele ne monte, si estrai almagda legierement en tornoiant ta main poc et poc;	After a short rest, and if the sharpness returns the second time, put the force with the instrument, and when it is stuck and does not rise, gently twist around your hand little by little.
et puis remette en aigue un poc de seil gemme, et leive de ceu l’oil dedens.	and then put a small silk thread, and leave the oil inside.
Puis met par defuer l’oil estoupes ou lainne moillie en oile roset et en abun d’uef, et lie avec l’oil sain.	Then apply a warm compress or wet cloth soaked in rose oil and plenty of honey, and bind it with clean oil.
Nos, et cil qui sont de nostre tens, mettons sus comin broiet avec abun d’uef.	And those who are from our time, apply it with plenty of honey.
Et se almagda n’i puet entrer en l’oil par sa duresce, car il i a de teilz homes qui ont trop durs les eulz, si covient que tu preignes l’estrument qui est apelez «alberit», de coi ci est li forme:	And if it cannot enter the eye due to its hardness, because there are some people who have very hard eyes, then you must use the tool called "alberit", of which this is the form:
Et perce donques la conjunctive soulement, et n’aler mie trop em parfont, mais fai I leu subtil, puis i boute almagda, si com nos avons dit;	And then pierce only the connective tissue, and do not go too far in front, but make the sharp instrument, then press gently, as we have said.
et au complissement de l’uevre appareille au malaide I dorteur avenant, en coi il dorme sus son dos en I leu tenebrous;	and at the completion of the work appears the evil of sleepiness that happens, in which he sleeps on his back in a dark place;
et soit deveez de toz movemens, et preigne legieres viandes, et ne mueve son chief ne a destre ne a senestre, et soit liiez selonc sa disposition jusc’a tier jor;	and it should be done with all movements, and take light foods, and do not move his head to the right or left, and it should be tied according to its position just above the eye;
puis le deslie en cele maison meisme tenebrouse, et esprueve sa veue, et lou fai veoir aucunes choses, et puis li remet lou lien jusc’a septime jor;	then reset the dislocation in that same dark place, and prove his sight, and let him see some things, and then return the bone to its position just before sleep;
et ne covient mie que tu faices ceu en l’oure de la cure ou aprés l’incision maintenant, mais il covient que tu aliges ceu, por ceu que li aigue monte hastanment.	and it should not be done only in the morning or after the incision, but it should be done when the pain is at its peak.
se apostemes chaus vient, que tu desliies l’oil devant le septime jor, et l’adrece de ceu qui assouaige aposteme;	when abscesses come, then you should apply oil in front of the seventh hour, and it will alleviate the abscess.
et quant il est apaisiez, si deslie la veue et met sus sa faice I orilliet por covrir aucun jor, et soit adés en celle maison tenebrouse.	and when it is calmed, then remove the bandage and put on its face a gold coin to cover any light, and let it stay in that dark house.
Et puis isse de la maison poc et poc, et se convertisse en ses cas;	And then slowly go out of the house and return to his own home;
et saiches que nulz deciples ne se doit entremettre en cest cas.	and tell that no one should interfere in this case.
Et uns vint a nos qui estoit de la Yrach, qui nos dist que en som pais faisoit om almagda perciet, a coi on succe l’aigue, mais toutevoie je n’en vis onques nul en nostre terre, ne je ne lou lis onques en livres des anciens;	And some came to us who were of the Yrach, who told us that in their country people used to do something like this, because of which the arrowhead would stick, but I have never seen any such thing in our land, nor have I read it in any books of the ancients;
et par aventure c’est une novele chose.	and perhaps it is a new thing.
Et ce sont les semblances des formes de almagda, por ceu que cil qui ne les conoit les voie;	And these are the similar forms of the almond, because those who do not know them see it as such;
et soient d’arain proprement:	and they are truly made of rain:
Et soient li chief d’aus de ceste meisme subtiliteit, et li derriene en III angles ague.	And they are the masters of this very subtlety, and the others in three angles awake.
de la char sor le neis	of the sinus headache
Aucune fois naissent ou neis chars ajostees diverses, de coi il i a aucunes qui semblent scorpions a mout de piez;	Never do charred or burned arrows of various kinds appear, because there are some that seem like scorpions at the tip;
et si i a de telz ou il ait char enchancree de fuxe color, et si a char souef de bone color.	and if there are such with enhanced burnt color, and if the arrow has a good color.
En celle donques de ces chars qui est souef, et ne mie enchancree, covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains encontre lou soleil;	In that case of those arrows that are good and not enhanced, it is appropriate to make the pain between your hands against the sun;
et oevre ses narines, et giete l’oncine a celles chars, et les trai fuers;	and work his nostrils, and pour the liquid into those charms, and pull them out;
pues cope ceu que tu em pues sostenir au spatumile subtil agut d’une part, tant que tu saiches que celle char est toute ostee.	so that you can hold it in your hand at the subtle tip of a needle, until you know that that char is entirely hardened.
Et s’il en remaint aucune chose c’on ne puisse coper, si l’ovrez a tout I des estrumens subtil legierement, si qu’il n’i demoure rien;	And if there remains nothing that can be held, open it with all the delicate instruments lightly, so that nothing remains.
et se sans te sormonte, ou aposteme chaus, si lou secort si com il covient;	and if without harming yourself, an abscess bursts, then let the pus drain as it should.
et se c’est apostemes malignes, si te haste et lou cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez et soient ostees toutes les chars, puis giete ou neis aisil et aigue ou vin.	And if they are malignant abscesses, then quickly and cauterize it until the wound is not moist and all the charms are removed, then pour in clean, cool water or vinegar.
Se li neis oevre, et moistors en vient jusc’a palais, saiches qu’il est sanez;	When the shoulder is injured, and moisture comes to the palm, remove it so that it is healthy.
et se moistors ne perce si com il covient, saiches qu’il i a char nee en l’os desus, a coi li estrumens ne vient mie por taillier:	And if the moisture does not penetrate as it should, remove it because there is cartilage above the bone, so that the tools do not come out for cutting.
adonques covient il que tu i boutes I fil de lin un poc gros, et soit noez de mains nous, et ait entre chescun nout d’espaice I doit ou moins;	Therefore, it is necessary that you insert a thread of linen slightly thick, and soak it in our hands, and put space between each one as much or little as needed.
et mette li malaides lou chiés dou fil en son neif a som pooir, et traie en odorant tant qu’il viegne par lou neif dedens la bouche;	And put the hairs of the injured person in the thread of the needle at the top, and pull through as far as it comes out of the needle through the mouth.
et maintes fois font ensi li enfant as escoles, et c’est legiere chose a celui qui le vuet faire;	And often they do this to children in schools, and it is an easy thing for those who wish to do it.
puis tien le chief qui vient par lou neif a une main, et l’autre chief qui vient par la bouche a l’autre main, et saiche l’un aprés l’autre en soiant as nous qui sont ou fil.	Then hold the child's head with one hand, and the other child's head with the other hand, and alternate them back and forth as we have shown in the picture.
Fai ceu tant que tu saiches que li nout ont corrompue celle char, puis trai lou filz, essue le sanc, et moille lou fil en oignement egiptien, et le remet derechief au neis si com devant;	Do this until you feel that the teeth have not been corrupted by that charm, then draw out the child's tooth, suck the blood, and wipe the wound with an Egyptian egg, and return it to its place as before.
fai ceu III jors ou plus, tant que li oignemens corrode tout ceu qui est demorez de char;	Do this three times or more, until the wound has eaten away everything that remains of the charm.
et puis met ou neis une caine de plonc aucuns jors tant qu’il soit sanez, et s’il a mestier de medicines sechans, si en use;	and then place or remove a bandage as needed for several days until it is healed, and if there is a need for medicines, use them.
et c’est li forme de l’estrument por purgier lou chief, a coi on distille les oiles et les medicines ou neis:	and this is the shape of the instrument for purging the head, with which one distills oils and medicines that are applied.
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain, semblant a une lampe overte, si com une cainne, et li conduis ausi;	And it should be of silver or tin, shaped like an open lamp, like a tube, and the conductor is also like this.
et se tu vues, si fai une cainne close, et soit li estrumens plains por espurgier lou chief;	and if you see, then make a closed tube, and the instrument is polished to purge the head.
et ait I mainche au chief por lou tenir quant on chaufe l’oile ou aucune liquor.	and it should have a handle at the top to hold when heating the oil or any liquid.
de la char sor le neis	of the sinus headache
Maintes fois naist au chief dou neis une maladie qui est apelee «telul», et croist et devient grans adés, tant qu’il est vis chose au regarder;	Many times a disease is born at the head of the neck, which is called "tulum", and grows and becomes large in size, as it appears to be seen.
et por ceu covient que tu lou copes au comencement, et l’oste tout fuer, puis met sor leu lou cautere ou la medicine ardant;	And for this reason, you should cover it at the beginning, and the bone is all bruised, then put the fire cauterizer or hot medicine on it.
et s’on le tarde a coper tant qu’il soit grans, si pren warde s’il est durs, de fuxe color, de povre sens:	And if you delay in covering it for so long, if it is hard, of poor color, and without feeling, then take heed.
si ne lou touchier mie de fer car c’est uns apostemes enchancrez, car quant on le cope aucune fois, si en vient grant malice au malaide;	If you do not touch it with a little iron because it is an infected abscess, for when it is covered once, then great harm comes to the pain.
