et se li apostemes est de soef touchement, non mie de fuxe color, et tu vois c’on le puisse tout coper, si vuide le malaide et lou cope sens paor, et cure le leu de choses sechans et restraignans.	and if they are abscesses, gently touch them, not with burning hot, and you see that one can cover the whole, if the pain and fear allow, and cure the limb of things that are tight and restrictive.
quant li neis est copez et cosus	when the bone is cut and sewn
Saiches que quant solutions de continuation vient en une de ces cartillagines ovraiges, i profite poc, fuer que en aucuns homes.	However, when the solution comes in one of these cartilaginous places, it is of little use, as it is not beneficial to everyone.
Il covient donques cant ceu avient a aucun, si regarde se li plaie est fresche a tout son sanc;	It is therefore necessary to wait until the wound has no blood, if you look and see that the wound is fresh and full of blood throughout.
et adonques ajoste les II levres a une costure, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	and then apply both lips to a seam, then cure it until it is healed.
et se les levres sont ja desevrees d’une part et d’autre, si covient que tu escorches toutes les parties de lor keur tant qu’elles sainent, puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et l’estraint, et poudre sus poudre de sanc de dragon, et encens broiet;	and if the lips are already decayed from one side and the other, then it is necessary to scrape all the parts of their edge until they heal, then assemble both lips to a seam, and hold them together, and powder with powder of blood of dragon, and broken incense.
et met sus les poudres une piece d’emplaustre de fort ou d’autre emplaustre soudant, et le laisse tant qu’il chiece par lui, puis le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	and apply powders on top of the plaster of strong or other healing plaster, and leave it until it heals through it, then treat the wound with ointment until it is healed.
Li maniere de la costure si est que tu assembles la solution:	The manner of the suture is that you assemble the solution:
ou par aguilles, si com nos avons dit en la costure dou ventre;	or with needles, as we have said in the stitching of the abdomen;
ou par fil, si com je le t’ai fait savoir.	or with thread, as I have told you.
des apostemes des levres	of abscesses on the lips
A mains homes avient dedens les levres aposteme dur, semblans a grains de veces, et menor et plus grant;	In some people, there are abscesses inside the lips, similar to grains, and smaller and larger;
adonques couvient que tu tornes les levres, et fendes sus chescun nout, et le prent as pinceures et le cope en chescune partie;	therefore it is necessary that you turn the lips, and cut above each one, and take them with forceps and clean each part;
puis emple lou leu aprés l’incision de vitriole broiet, tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	Then apply the limb after the incision of broken glass, until the wound is cleansed.
et puis lou leive d’aisil, et cure lou leu de choses seches tant qu’il soit sanez.	And then apply a dry bandage to the limb and treat it with dry things until it is healed.
de la char des gencives	of the crown of the teeth
Maintes fois naist sus les gencives char ajostee, que li ancien apelent «albulus»;	Often gums rise above the teeth, which the ancients called "albulus".
si covient que tu la sostienes as tenailles, et la cope a sa racine, et laisse corre la bowe ou le sanc;	If necessary, hold it with pliers and cut at its root, and let the blood or pus flow out.
puis met sor le leu vitriole broiet, ou autres poudres restraignans et desiccatives;	Then apply the limb broken glass, or other astringent and desiccating powders.
et se celle char revient aprés l’incision, et maintes fois avient, si la cope la seconde fois, et la cauterize:	And if that swells again after the incision, and often does, then cut it the second time and cauterize it.
si ne revient mie aprés le cautere;	if it does not return slightly after the burn;
et ce sont les formes des estrumens por coper.	and these are the forms of instruments to cover.
des sordens	of the deaf
Aucunes fois sont assemblees au chief des dens, dedens la bouche entre les gencives, escorces qui sont laides et aspres;	Sometimes they are gathered at the root of the teeth, within the mouth between the gums, scraps that are unpleasant and sharp;
et aucune fois sont li dent noir et citrin et vers, tant que li corruption vient a la gencive, et sont li dent puant;	and sometimes they are associated with black and yellow and green teeth, as far as the corruption reaches the gum, and are with foul-smelling teeth;
si covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains, et ses chiés soit en ton saint, et reis les dens ou les escorces aperent, tant qu’il n’i demore rien;	if it is necessary for you to remove the pain between your hands, and its roots are in your holy place, and remove the teeth or scraps that appear, as long as nothing remains;
et ensi fai de la noiror et de la verdor, et de la jaunice et des autres taiches, tant qu’elles soient mondees;	And thus make of the black and green, and yellow and other stains, until they are removed.
et s’on oste ceu que i est a la premiere rasion, c’est boin;	And if it is taken out what is at the first layer, it is good.
se ceu non, si rencomence a rere le secont jor et lou tier, tant que tu aies tout reis;	If not, start again from the second layer and the third, until you have removed everything.
et saiches que li dent ont mestier de diverses formes d’estrumens por reire, selonc ceu que li oevre lou demoustre, por ceu que li raseur dont on reit defuer les dens ont autres formes que cil dont on reit entre les dens;	And wash the teeth with various instruments to remove, according to what the operator demonstrates, because the razor that is used to remove the teeth has other shapes than the one used between the teeth.
et cestes formes et autres soient avec toi appareillies.	And these forms and others be with you prepared.
Il covient quant tu cures lou dent de sa dolor que tu tardes dou traire tant com tu pues, car ce ne doit om mie faire;	When you are treating a tooth for pain that you delay pulling as much as you can, because no one should do this.
car c’est une substance mout haute jusc’a donc c’on n’ait point d’excusation dou raier.	because it is a very high substance from which we have no excuse to pull it.
Adonques quant li malaides est constrains dou traire, si covient que tu soies certains dou dent doillant.	Therefore, when the toothache is extremely painful, you should be certain that the tooth is dead.
Maintes fois desoit li dolor lou malaide, et cuide qu’elle soit ou dent saint, et fait traire le boin dent;	Many times the pain of the misaligned tooth, and take care that it is either a holy tooth, and pull out the good tooth.
et toutevoie ne se depart mie li dolor per ceu, tant que li malvais estrais, car nos l’avons ja veut faire a ces sainors;	And in any way do not leave the pain because of it, until the bad ones are removed, for we have already done this to these sinners.
et quant tu es bien certains dou dent doillant, si covient que tu escorches entor lou dent a tout i. spatumile fort por warder la gencive de toutes pars;	And when you are well certain of the painful tooth, it is necessary that you burn around the tooth on all sides. with a strong iron rod to protect the gum from all parts.
puis le mues a tes dois ou as tenailles subtilz au premier poc et poc, tant qu’il soit bien eslochiés, puis i afferme bien les tenailles;	then move the joint gently with your fingers or thin needles at the first point and point, until it is well dislocated, then firmly fix the needles.
et soit li chiés dou malaide en ton saint entre tes genous, et lou tien bien si qu’il ne se mueve.	and either the painful part between your knees and ankles, and keep it still so that it does not move.
Aprés estrai lou dent droitement sens brisier, et s’il ne saut fuer, si prent aucun de ces estrumens et le boute dedens de chescune part legierement, et lou remuef si com tu as fait premier.	After extracting the tooth correctly without breaking it, and if it does not jump out, take one of these tools and push it gently into each part lightly, and shake it as you did first.
Et se li dens est perciez et mengiez, si covient que tu l’emplisses de drapelz, lai ou li pertus sont;	And if the dense part is punctured and damaged, then it is necessary to fill it with cloths where the pores are.
et si l’estraint subtilment as tenailles, que il ne brise a l’estraindre;	and if the thin needles are firmly held, so that they do not break when being pulled out.
et covient mout saigement ovrer entor la gencive por deschaucier lou dent.	and it is necessary to carefully wrap around the gum to dislodge the tooth.
Et te done bien en warde que tu ne le brises, et en remaigne une partie, et reveigne au malaide par la malice de la racine plus grans dolors de la premiere.	And be careful not to break it and leave a part, and again cause the pain by the evil of the root more great pains of the first.
Et te warde que tu ne faices mie ensi com font li ignorant sainor, qui par lor haste et par lor hardiesce brisent aucune fois le charreit, et n’i amenistrent mie ceu que nos avons conteit;	And beware that you do not act in such a way as the ignorant sainors, who by their haste and boldness break everything at once, and never amend what we have told.
mais font venir aucune fois par l’oquison de ceu grant maladie por les racines que i demorent, ou por lou charreit qu’il brisent, si com nos avons sovent veut;	but bring forth every time by the wise one of this great disease because of the roots that they delay, or for the cart that they break, as we have often seen.
et quant li dens est trais, si lavez lou leu de vin ou d’aisil et de seil;	and when the tooth is drawn, wash the mouth with wine or sage and salt;
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, que sovent avient, si emple lou leu de vitriole broiet;	and if blood comes out and often does, then use the mouth with broken glass wine;
et se ceu ne vaut, si le cauterize.	and if it does not heal, then cauterize it.
Les formes des estrumens, a coi om muet les dens premier, soient a longes pointes et a gros mainches, qu’il ne doublent mie quant tu trairas le dent;	The forms of instruments used to remove teeth should be long and thick-handled, so they do not double over when you pull the tooth.
et ce sont les formes:	These are the shapes:
Et soient de gros membres si qu’il ne ploient mie au traire, et soient de fer inde bien fait, et soient dentez por mues tenir.	And they should be thick-bodied so they do not bend when pulling, and they should be made of well-made iron, and they should be pointed to hold the tooth.
de la racine des dens	from the root of the tooth
Quant li racine demoure au traire, si covient que tu mettes sor le leu coton moilliet em burre I jor ou II, tant que li leus soit amolis, pues i boute les tenailles qui sont apelees «algefri», de coi li chiés semblet bec de soigne;	When the root remains in the tooth, it is necessary to place a moistened cotton ball on the tooth for I or II hours until the tooth is softened, then extract the forceps called "algefri," which are shaped like a beak.
et soient dedens faites ausi com une lime et c’est li forme:	and they should be made inside as well as a lime and that is the shape:
Et se les racines ne vuellent issir a tout ces tenailles, si covient que tu descuevre la char tot entor la racine, et i met l’estrument qui est apelez «althali», c’est a savoir palainche, de coi ci est li forme:	And if the roots do not wish to come out at all these needles, it is necessary that you dig around the root completely, and put the tool called "althali", which is a spoon-shaped instrument, in order to:
Et soit fors et gros si qu’il ne brise mie, et se li racine saut par ceu, c’est boin;	And if it is large, so that it does not break, and if its root springs up through the sky, it is good.
se ceu non, si t’aide de toz les estrumens, de coi les formes vienent ci aprés:	If not, with all the instruments, from which the forms come after this:
Et si s’aide on de cest estrument qui ait II rains, de coi ci est li forme:	And if you use this tool that has two prongs, with which comes the shape:
et d’autres ferremens qui sont devant en la rasion des dens, et de cest estrument qui semble unes grans tenailles, dont ci est li forme:	and other tools that are before in the realm of the teeth, and with this tool that looks like large needles, from which comes the shape:
Et soit cist estrumens fors qu’il ne puisse brisier, et saiches que mout d’estrumens de dens sont;	And let these instruments be such that they cannot break, and they are many of dense ones.
et ausi d’autres estrumens, qui ne sont mie contez;	and also other instruments, which are not counted.
et li saiges maistres subtilz trueve par soi meisme son estrument, selonc ceu que ses ovraiges et li maladie li demoustre, car il i a de teilz maladies ou li ancien n’enseignerent point d’estrument por la diversiteit d’au;s et s’om brise point dou charreit ou des autres os, ou il porrit, si i cerche as estrumens qu’il i covient, que je t’ai dit, et t’aide des gestes, de coi ci est li forme:	And the wise masters find their own instrument by themselves, according to their works and the disease shows them, because there are some diseases where the ancients did not teach the instrument for the diversity of the others and it has not broken the cart or other bones, or it has not helped, if he searches for the instruments that he needs, which I have told you, and helps with gestures, from which these forms come:
Et soient gros et bien tenant por tenir l’os, qu’il n’eschaipe, mais le puisse tenir et oster;	And let there be thick and strong bands to hold the bone, that it not escape, but be able to hold and remove.
et puis restoure lou leu de medicines convenant a ceu, et s’il ait en l’os porriture, et elle est petite, si la reis a tout cest estrument:	Then restore the limb to its proper position with suitable medicines, and if there is any pus in the bone, and it is small, then remove all of this tool:
Quant li dent apperent ne mie selonc lou cors natureil, et li forme est laide, et meismement en femmes puceles, si covient que tu saiches se li dens est neis aprés lou dent, et n’est mie en droit leu, et on ne lou puet soier ne limer:	When the tooth appears not in accordance with its natural position, and its form is ugly, and especially in young women, then it is necessary to remove the tooth if it is not in the right place, and cannot be straightened or cleaned.
adonques lou raie;	Then the root:
et s’il est aers avec lou dent, si prent cest estrument dont ci est li forme, et est semblans a I petit bec, et soit de fer inde agut en som:	and if he is held by the tooth, take this instrument which has the following form, and it is similar to a small beak, and let it be made of iron, sharp at the end:
Et lou cope poc et poc em mains jors por la duresce dou dent, et por ceu que tu ne mueves les autres, et s’il est apparans c’on le puisse limer, si lou lime d’une teil lime com ci est li forme:	And the copper bit by bit in your hands for the hardness of the tooth, and because you do not move the others, and if it appears that one can be removed, then the copper bit by bit like this is the form:
et est ausi com li lime de coi on fait les aguilles;	and it is also like the lip of which one makes arrows;
et en lime lou dent poc et poc em mains jors legierement, si qu’il ne se mueve tant qu’il chiece;	and in the lip of the tooth, lightly and carefully, so that it does not move until it is cut;
puis la plaine en la fin a tout aucun raseur, et se li dens est trop trenchans et il blece la lengue, si covient limer l’aspreteit tant qu’il soit igalz, si qu’il ne blece la lengue ne ne corrompe la parole.	then the flat end of it to any razor, and if the tooth is too sharp and it cuts the tongue, then one must file the sharpness until it is even, so that it does not cut the tongue or corrupt the speech.
quant li dent lochent	when they are missing
Quant li dent devant lochent, ou par percussion ou par cheoir, et li malaides ne puet presser sus ceu qu’il menjue qu’il ne chient, et tu les as curez de medicines restrignans, et ceu ne vaut;	When the tooth is knocked out, whether by impact or falling, and the pain cannot be relieved by pressing on the gum where it was located, and you treat it with restricting remedies, and it does not help.
si les covient restraindre d’un fil d’or, car li filz d’argent devient vert et porrit, mais li ors ne se mue onques;	if they need to be restricted with a gold wire, because the silver thread becomes green and rotten, but the gold never changes.
et soit li filz moiens ne trop gros ne trop menus, selonc la quantiteit de l’espaice entre les dens;	and it should be neither too thin nor too thick, according to the amount of space between the teeth.
et se tu vues adrecier les dens, si pren lou fil et lou boute double entre les II dens sains, puis met les chiés entre les dens meus, s’il en i a I ou plusors, tant que tu veignes saigement jusc’au dent sain d’autre part;	and if you see that the teeth are moving, take the wire and double it between the two healthy teeth, then place the injured tooth between the other teeth, as many as there are, until you can safely chew on the healthy tooth on the other side.
puis rencomence la coverture jusc’a la partie ou tu encomensas, et estrains ta main subtilment et saigement, tant qu’il ne se mueve point;	Then, reapply the covering just to the part where you began, and gently and skillfully stretch your hand, until it does not move at all.
et soit ta lieeure a la racine dou dent si qu’il ne puist eschaper.	And let your fingers be tied to the root of the tooth so that it cannot escape.
Puis cope les chiés dou fil a unes tenailles, et les assemble, et les repont entre le dent sain, et le met ensi qu’il ne blece la lengue;	Then cut the roots of the teeth with some needles, and assemble them, and put them back between the healthy tooth, and place it in such a way that it does not bleed on the tongue.
et puis le laisse ensi estroit tant com il puet demorer, et s’il deslie, ou li filz ront, si l’estraint d’un autre fil;	Then leave it so tight as it can stay, and if it dislocates, or the thread breaks, then tighten it with another thread.
si demorrait et servira ensi tout son tens, et c’est li forme des dens et li figure de l’adrecement des II dens sains, et des II meus, si com tu vois:	If it persists and serves in this manner for the entire duration, it is the form of the teeth and the alignment of the second molars, and the second incisors, as you see.
Et quant li dent chiet, si lou remet on en son leu, de fres en fres, si com nos avons dit;	And when the tooth breaks, if it is reset in its place, from fresh to fresh, as we have said.
et ne s’en entremette mie qui n’est saiges et soffrans, et aucune fois fait on la forme d’un dent d’os de vaiche, et lou met on au leu ou li defaute est, et l’estraint on si com nos avons dit, et demore et sert ensi lonc tens.	And it does not interfere with any other teeth that are wise and painful, and never is the shape of a goat's bone made, and it is reset in the place where the defect is, and it is held as we have said, and it persists and serves for the entire duration.
de coper lou liien de la lengue	to cut the tongue's ligament
Aucune fois est cist liiens qui vient desoz la lengue ou naturez, que on naist ensi;	Never are these joints that come out of their place from the tongue or naturally, which one is born thus.
ou par accident de plaie soudee;	or by accident of a burned wound;
et li ovraiges est telz que tu oevre la bouche dou malaide, et ait sa teste en ton sain, et li lieve la lengue;	and the works are such that you work the mouth of the dislocated joint, and have their head in your safe place, and they lift the tongue;
puis cope lou liien nervous dou large, tant que li lengue soit desloie de son tenement, et se il i a duresce ou nout, et c’est de soudement de plaie, si i boute l’uncine et cope dou large celui liement;	then press the nerve with a wide, until the tongue is dislocated from its place, and if it has hardness or no, and it is by burned wound, then beat the thin one and press the wide one gently;
et garde que li fendure ne soit mie trop em parfont, por l’artere qui est desoz;	and be careful that the cut is not too deep, for the artery that is out;
et quant tu as fait, si leve le leu d’aigue rose et d’aisil, ou d’aigue froide, puis met desoz la lengue une tente de lin;	When you have done this, lift the limb of high rose or ash, or high cold, then place a tent of linen over the tongue;
et la teigne li malaides chescune nuit, que li leus ne puisse soder.	and apply the tent to the hairs every night, so that the limbs cannot move.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si met sor le leu vitriole broiet;	And if blood flows out, put a piece of broken glass on the limb;
et se li sans te vaint, si le cauterize au cautere lentiginout, qui est boin a ceu;	and if the blood does not stop flowing, then cauterize it with the slow-burning cautery, which is good for healing.
puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez,	then use other treatments until it is healed.
et se tu lou vois de fusse color ou noir ou dur, si que li malaides ne lou sent, si n’i touchier point, car c’est chancre;	and if you see that the wound is yellow or black or hard, and the patient does not feel pain, do not touch it, because it is a chancre.
et s’il est declinans a blenchor, et il i a moistor, si i giete l’oncine, et lou fent d’un spatumile subtil, et lou delivre d’une part et d’autre;	If it is leaning towards the wound, and there is moisture, then pour the needle, and the opening of a thin spatula, and deliver from one side and the other.
et se li sans te vaint a ton ovraige, si met sus vitriole broiet tant qu’il soit estainchiez, puis revien a ton ovraige tant que tu traies tout fuer;	And if it does not want to enter your work, then place the broken glass shards on top as long as it is cleaned, then return to your work until you remove all the foreign matter.
puis leve lou leu d’aisil et de seil, et le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then lift the limb from above and below, and treat other wounds until it is healed.
des apostemes de la gorge	of throat abscesses
Aucune fois vient dedens la gorge boces qui sont apelees «godath», et les apele on proprement les II amandres, et quant tu les cures, si com nos avons dit en la division, et elles ne sont sanees, si pren garde:	No one ever comes from within the throat wounds that are called "godath", and they are properly called the II mandibles, and when you treat them, as we have said in the division, and they are not healed, then be careful:
se c’est apostemes dur de petit sens et de fusse color, si ne lou touchier mie de fer.	If abscesses are hard to feel with a small sense and of fuzzy color, then do not touch them with a little iron.
Et s’il est rouges et li racine est grosse, si ne lou touchier mie de fer, ausi por lou decorrement de sanc;	And if it is red and the root is large, then do not touch them with a little iron, also for the running of blood.
mais lou laisse tant qu’il soit meur, et adonques tu lou partiras, ou il rompirait par soi;	But let it be until it is ripe, and then you will break it, or it will break by itself.
et s’il est de blainche color reont, et li racine est subtilz, si aies apareilliet l’estrument por coper, mais regarde premierement se li apostemes chalz repose et est apaisiez.	And if it is of white color and the root is thin, then prepare the instrument to cover, but first check if the abscess has settled and is calm.
Adonques fai seoir lou malaide devant lou soleil, et ses chiés soit en ton sain, et li oevre la bouche et lou preigne li serjans entre ses mains, et presse la lengue desoz a tout l’estrument, de coi ci est li forme;	Then let the pain sit in front of the sun, and its heads be in your healthy hand, and the work the mouth and the arrow that the soldiers have between their hands, and press the tongue away from all the instrument, because of which is the shape.
et soit d’argent ou d’arain subtil ausi com uns coutelz:	and let it be of silver or thin brass like some knives:
Cant tu presses la lengue a tout cest estrument, et tu vois l’aposteme, si pren l’oncine et lou fiche en l’amandre, et la trai fuer au desus plus que tu pues;	if you press the tongue with this instrument, and you see the abscess, take the point and chip it in the amber, and draw it out above as much as you can;
et trai aucune chose des toiles avec, puis la cope a l’estrument, de coi ci est li forme, que semble unes forces;	and take nothing with from the threads, then cover the instrument with a cloth, of which this is the shape, which seems like forceps;
et toutevoie li chief sont corbé, et l’un endroit l’autre, et sont molt agut, et est fait de fer inde ou d’andainne:	and all the heads are hooked, one on top of the other, and they are very sharp, and it is made of iron or steel;
Et se tu n’as cest estrument present, si lou cope as tenailles, de coi ci est li forme:	And if you do not have this instrument present, with a hook, of which this is the form:
Et soit trenchans d’une part, et d’autre part nom;	and let it be cutting on one side, and on the other not;
et quant tu as copeit l’une des amandres, si cope l’autre selonc cele meisme maniere, et aprés l’incision gargarize li malaides aigue chaude, et aigue et aisil, et se decorremens de sanc avient, si gargarize li malaides aigue, ou escorces de pomes grenates soient cuites, ou fuelles de mirte, et semblans choses, tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	When you have cut one of the splints, cut the other according to the same method, and after the incision gargle the sharp pain with hot, hot, and salty water, and if there is blood flowing, gargle the sharp pain with hot water, or use pounded green pomegranate skins, or similar things, until the wound is cleansed.
puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then treat it until it is healed.
et aucune fois naissent en la gorge autres apostemes que les II amandres, si les cope donques ensi com les II amandres igament.	And never any other abscesses than the two splints are born in the throat, so cut them then as the two splints should be.
Et je medicinai une femme d’un aposteme que li estoit neis dedens la gorge, c’est a savoir I aposteme de petit sens;	And I treated a woman with an abscess that was lodged within her throat, specifically a small abscess.
et avoit jai bien pres close toute la gorge, si que li femme ne pooit expirer por le conduit qui estoit estoupez, et ne pooit ne mengier ne boivre, et fust morte s’elle demorast ensi I jor ou II.	And she had almost completely closed her throat, so that the woman could not breathe due to the condition that was choking her, and could not eat or drink, and died if she continued like this for a day or two.
Et li apostemes estoit jai si montez qu’il avoit fuer mis II rains par les II pertuis dou neis.	And the abscess was so large that it had been inserted with two needles through both nostrils.
Je hastai donques tantost, et fichai en l’un I oncine, puis lou traï fuers, et en traï grant porcion de bowe;	I therefore acted quickly, and inserted it into one incision, then removed the rest, and removed a large portion of blood.
puis refis autreteil en l’autre pertus dou neis, et li ovrai la bouche et li pressai la lengue;	Then I inserted it into another incision through the throat, and performed the operation on the mouth and pressed her tongue.
aprés fichai l’oncine en ces apostemes, et en copai une partie, et n’en issit fuers que un poc de sanc;	After I had extracted these abscesses, and I took out a part of it, and it did not stop bleeding until a little blood came out.
et ensi fut destoupez li conduis de la gorge la femme, et comensa maintenant a boivre aigue et puis vin, et ne cessai de taillier de cel aposteme par lonc tens;	And thus the woman's throat was cut, and she began to drink water and then wine, and did not stop cutting into that abscess by a long stretch.
et li apostemes recroissoit adés, et remplissoit lou leu que je avoie vuidiet, tant qu’il refut mout gros;	And the abscesses kept recurring, and filled up the space that I had emptied, until it became very large.
adonques je l’engignai et lou cauterizai dedens la gorge:	Therefore, I advised her to cauterize it internally in the throat:
ensi demora sens croistre;	Thus, she did not grow without it.
et me partis de ces parties, et ne soi que Deus fist de li aprés moi.	And I departed from these parts, and knew not what God would do after me.
de l’uve	of the eye
Quant reume dessent a l’uve, et elle est enflee et elle est longe, si est apelee «perpendiculaire»;	When referring to the eye, and it is inflamed and long, it is called "perpendicular".
et s’elle est desoz grosse et reonde, si est apelee «uve».	And if it is large and round, it is called "uvula".
Quant elle est curee si com nos avons dit en la division, et li cure ne profite mie, et tu vois que li chaus apostemes est apaisiez, et elle est subtilz, si covient que tu la copes;	When it is treated as we have said in the division, and the cure does not help much, and you see that the abscess has been relieved, and it is small, then you must lance it.
et celle qui est reonde assemblee et n’est mie longe;	And the one that is round and not long;
et elle est sanguine ou de fusse color ou noire, si covient que tu eschues l’incision de li.	and it is bloody or of a dark or black color, then you must avoid the incision of the latter.
Car il i a grant peril sus lou malaide.	Because there is great danger in the pain.
Il covient donques, quant tu la vois, selonc la maniere que j’ai dit, de sa blenchor et de sa longesce, que tu faices seoir le malaide devant lou soleil, et li presse la lengue a l’estrument dont nos avons fait la remembrance ci devant;	Therefore, when you see it, according to the manner that I have said, of its size and length, you should place the pain in front of the sun, and press the tongue with the tool that we have mentioned earlier.
puis fiche l’oncine en l’uve, et la trai desoz, et la cope a I des II estrumens que j’ai dit en l’incision des II amandres.	Then fish the thorn out of the wound, and remove it, and wrap it with one or two of the tools that I have mentioned in the incision of the two mandibles.
Et covient que tu ne coper mie fuer que la superfluiteit qui est outre le termine natureil;	And it is necessary that you cover only the excess that is beyond the natural limit;
car se tu en copes plus, si grieves a la voix, et a la parolle;	for if you cover more, it hurts the voice and speech;
et aprés l’incision, use de ceu que nos avons dit en l’incision des II amandres, et le cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	And after the incision, use what we have said in the incision of the second rib, and treat it until it is healed.
Et se li malaides a paor dou coper, si covient que tu i use d’engien a la cauterization de li sens paor.	And if the pain is too great for the copper, then you must use an engine for the cauterization of the sensitive pain.
Et li maniere dou cautere si est aigue ague.	And the manner of the cauterization is sharp and hot.
Et est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, et puis li presse la lengue a l’estrument que nos avons dit ou chapistre de cautere, et confis avec aigue vive chaus, si qu’elle ne soit mie trop espesse ne trop clere;	And if the hairs put their head in your clean hand, and then press the tongue against the instrument we have said or in the chapter of cautery, and fix it with a sharp, live knife, so that it is not too thick or too clear;
et en emple le chevement de cest estrument, de coi ci est li forme:	and use the movement of this instrument, which has this form:
Et ait ou chief une cheveure ou om met la medecine, si com li chevemens d’une cuillier, et met l’estrument a tout la medicine sus l’uve;	And it should have one hair or how the man puts the medicine, like the movement of a spoon, and put the instrument on all the medicine over the eye;
et li malaides soit gisans sus son costeit, si que li salive et li muscillaige corre de sa bouche de la medicine dedens, si qu’ele ne dessende a la gorge, et lou blece;	and the hairs lie across his chest, so that saliva and muscle juice from his mouth flow into the medicine inside, so it does not drip down his throat and into his stomach.
puis tien ta main a tout la medicine et la presse sus l’uve, la quantiteit de la moitiet d’une houre, tant que tu la vois nercie et li mordications de la medicine soit apaisie;	then hold your hand over the entire medicine and press it on the eye, the quantity of half an hour, until you see the medicine is softened and the bitter taste of the medicine is eased.
et se tu vues, pren coton et l’envoloupe sus aucun estrument, et moille lou coton en la medicine, et boute l’estrument a tout le couton en la cainne desus, tant que li coton s’aerde sus l’uve;	and if you see, take cotton and wrap it around any instrument, and wipe the cotton in the medicine, and blow the instrument through all the cotton into the corner above, until the cotton becomes red on the eye.
et fai ceu sovent, tant que li cauteres soit parfais, puis la laisse elle seche, et chiet aprés IIII jors ou V.	And do this often, until the cautery is perfect, then let it dry, and wait for several hours or five.
Et se tu as mestier de rencomencier lou cautere de la medicine, si le rencomence, et aprés le cautere l’essue entor l’uve, de couton embut em burre, et mundifie ceu qui est entor de la medicine;	And if you have the skill to restart the cauterization of the eye, then restart it, and after the cauterization, wrap it around the eye with cotton soaked in butter, and clean what is around the eye.
et soit arosez d’aigue froide, et soit curez de gargarismes tant qu’il soit sanez.	And either apply a cold sharp instrument, and treat with gargling until they are healthy.
Ceste cure est plus save de l’incision, ne que li cautere;	This treatment is more saved from incision than from the cauterization;
s’elle est curee de fumigation selonc ceste maniere, pren calament et ysope et origanum et rue et camomille et avronne et semblans herbes, et les assemble toutes ou aucunes d’eles en I pot, et i met aisil, et fai bullir;	If it is treated with fumigation in this manner, take chamomile and hyssop and origanum and rue and camomile and avronne and similar herbs, and gather all or some of them in one pot, and add vinegar, and make it boil;
et li potz soit bien gluez de fort terre, et enmi le pot ait I estrument cheveit selonc ceste maniere:	And the pot should be well sealed with strong earth, and inside the pot there should be an instrument like this:
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain, et soit li uns des chiés boutez en la bouche dou malaide tant que li vapor monte a l’uve par la caine, tant que li uve soit mortifie;	And it should be of silver or tin, and one end of the instrument should be inserted into the mouth of the patient until the steam rises to the brain through the nose, until the brain is dead.
aprés lou rencomence sovent, tant que li uve seche, et garde que tu ne faices ceu au comencement de l’avenement de l’aposteme chaut, car plusors choses i avienent;	After that, it is often repeated until the brain dries, and make sure you do not apply this at the beginning of the onset of the abscess, for many things happen.
et ne faire mie ceu fuer que a la declination d’aposteme chaut.	And do not apply it until the decline of the abscess.
Et se cist estrument n’est presens, si pren une caine et met dedens lou chief une craiffe d’uef, si que li bouche au malaide n’ait mie trop chaut;	And if this instrument is not present, take a knife and place it inside the head, so that the mouth does not close too much.
car li craiffe d’uef ne lait mie la vapor grever la bouche, et c’est bone cure ensamble salut.	because the knife does not cause excessive vapor to burden the mouth, and this is a good remedy together with saving life.
Maintes fois s’aert a la gorge os ou espinee de poisson, ou aucune chose;	Many times it is asserted at the throat with an object or fish bone, or nothing;
si covient donc que tu traies ceu que tu pues veoir, et li presse la lengue au soleil a tout l’estrument, si que tu voies mues la chose;	so it is necessary that you remove what you can see, and press the tongue against the sun at all times, so that you see the thing;
et ceu que ne t’apert mie et est reponus en la gorge, covient que tu faices vomir le malaide ainsois que li viande soit cuite en l’estomac;	and what you cannot see and is pushed back into the throat, it is necessary that you make vomit the thing as soon as the food is cooked in the stomach;
par aventure si istra li chose aerse par le vomissement;	If by chance, the thing is also moved by vomiting;
ou li malaides englutisse une piece d’esponge, ou une piece de navel, ou une racine de laitue, ou I morceil de pain sec;	or the hairs have swallowed a piece of sponge, or a piece of naval, or a root of lettuce, or some piece of dry bread;
et lie a l’esponge I fil, et puis la transglutisse;	and it has tied the thread to the sponge, and then swallowed it again;
et quant elle venra au leu, si s’aerdra, et puis trairas fuer;	and when she comes to the shoulder, she will be caught, and then drawn out forcefully;
et s’elle ne vient fuer de ceu que nos avons dit, si pren I estrument de plonc selonc ceste forme:	and if she does not come out as we have said, take the instrument of force according to this form:
Et soit li estrumens corbés au chief si qu’il puist plus legierement entrer en la gorge, et ait le chief en haut leveit;	And let the instrument be curved at the head so that it can more easily enter the throat, and have the head raised high;
et warde que tu ne touchier l’epiglote, que li tous ne li viegne, ne ne bouter mie l’os dedens;	and guard that you do not touch the epiglottis, that it does not come out, or push the bone inside;
et mues vaut que li malaides i boute l’estrument, por ceu qu’il seit mues ou li chose est aerse;	and move the hairs and push the instrument, because it is more or less or the thing is as such;
si la boute aval, ou il la traie fuer a tout l’estrument igalment, tant qu’elle soit fuer.	if the pushing goes down, or it pulls the instrument evenly, as far as it is strong.
de la sansue de la gorge	of the throat wound
Aucune fois est medicinee li sansue, si com j’ai dit en la division, par la cure de medicines;	Never use the saliva, as I said in the division, by the cure of medicines;
et quant ceu ne profite mie, adonques regarde en la gorge dou malaide au soleil, puis que tu li presses la lengue a l’estrument que je t’ai dit.	and when it does not profit, then look in the throat of the hairs to the sun, then you press the tongue against the instrument that I have told you.
Et se tu vois la sansue, si la trai a tout I petit uncine, ou as tenailles subtilz que valent a ceu.	And if you see the sandal, take it to all the small nails, or with thin needles that are worth for this.
Et se ceu ne vaut, si pren une caine chevee, et la boute en la gorge dou malaide, puis boute ou chevement de la caine I fer chaut, et fai ce sovent.	And if it does not work, take a hairy rope, and push it into the throat of the misaligned joint, then push or move the rope with the sharp iron, and do this often.
Et se teigne li malaides d’aigue toute jor.	And if the misaligned joint is stiff all day.
puis pren plein I voirre d’aigue froide, et oevre la bouche, et la giete ens sens englutir, et la mueve a sa main sovent;	then take full handfuls of sharp, cold iron, and work the mouth, and pour in water against swallowing, and move it frequently to your hand.
et si tost com li sansue sent l’aigue, si chiet.	and if the tongue soon feels the sharpness, it will spit.
Et s’elle ne chiet si com nos avons dit, si subfumige lou malaide d’asefetide, a l’estrument que j’ai dit en la fumigation de l’uve;	and if it does not spit as we have said, then smoke the bad breath with asafetida, with the instrument I mentioned in the fumigation of the grape;
fai ceu maintes fois, car elle cherra sens targier.	do this many times, for it will eventually stop.
Et li maniere de la fumigation si est que tu preignes I pot ou il ait charbons vis, et soit li pos covert d’un coverseil perciet en mileu, et en celui pertus soit li chiés de l’estrument;	and the way of the fumigation is that you hold the pot with charcoal inside, and place it in a covered dish, and in the middle of it put the instrument;
puis i giete ta fumigation, et li malaides mette lou chief de la cainne en sa bouche, et cloie la bouche, si que li fumee n’en isse mie, mais viegne jusc’a la sansue;	then give your steam, and the painful one puts the head of the snake in its mouth, and closes its mouth, so that the smoke does not come out, but comes up to the nose.
et la sansue cherra maintenant, et s’elle ne chiet, si rencomence la fumigation par maintes fois;	and the nose will now drip, and if it does not drip, then repeat the steam many times.
et soffre li malaides soif, et menjuce choses salees et als, et ne boive point d’aigue;	and suffer the painful one thirst, and give it salty and sour things, and do not let it drink anything sharp.
et adonques li iert mestier qu’elle isse fuer par cest governement.	and then it will have the task of being cured by this treatment.
Et li forme de l’estrument a coi on trait la sansue, si est, quant on la puet veoir, semblans a tenailles corbés por mues entrer en la gorge;	And the shape of the instrument used to treat the nose, so is, when one can see it, similar to curved needles for mucous membranes to enter into the throat;
et ait semblance au bec de soigne, et i ait asperiteit de lime, si que ceu qu’elle prent, elle ne puet lassier;	and it resembles the beak of a bird, and there is an abrasiveness to the lime, so that whatever it takes, it cannot wear out.
et vez ci la forme:	and it has this shape:
li chapistres des apostemes	the chapters on abscesses
Mout de semblances d’aposteme sont, selonc ceu que li remembrance vient ci aprés d’un et d’autre en cest livre, et sont diver en perforation et en taille;	Many types of abscesses are, according to what the memory comes with after one and another in this book, and they differ in puncture and cut.
et c’est en II manieres dont l’une est en sa semblance meisme, et de ceu qu’il tient moistor.	and it is in two ways that one is in its very appearance, and because it holds moisture.
Et li seconde maniere si est por les leus ou il sont au cors.	And the second method is for the bones or when they are broken.
car li apostemes dou chief est autres que cil dou fondement, et li apostemes dou leu charnut est autres que cil qui vient en jointures, et chescuns ait son jugement en l’uevre.	For the abscesses of the head are different from those of the foundation, and the abscesses of the thigh bone are different from those that come in joints, and each has its own judgment in the work.
Et si a apostemes c’on ne doit mie percier, tant que li bowe est meure selonc son acomplissement;	And if to abscesses there is one that should not be punctured, until the hole is completed according to its completion.
et si a de telz qu’il covient percier quant il sont crut, et ne meurent mie selonc lor acomplissement, si com aposteme qui sont delez jointures.	And if there are such that it is necessary to pierce when they are ripe, and do not die according to their completion, like abscesses which are beyond the joints.
Car quant apostemes vient delez jointures, et on le laisse tant qu’il est porris entor, par aventure si sont corrumput li liien et li nerf de la jointure, par coi ce est cause de contraction en celui membre.	For when abscesses come beyond joints, and it is left until it is swollen around, perhaps the ligament and nerve of the joint are corrupted, by which this is the cause of contraction in that member.
Ou li aposteme est delez lou membre principel, et se tu tardes la perforation tant qu’il soit meurez, si nuira au membre principeil;	When the abscess is beyond the main member, and if you delay the piercing until it dies, it will harm the main member.
ou il est delez lou fondement, si le perce on ainsois qu’il soit meurs;	When it is beyond the foundation, if you pierce it while it is dead, it will harm it.
et ne covient mie que tu perces aposteme crut sens digestion acomplie, fuers que celui qui est delez lou fondement, qu’il ne porrisse em parfont, et soit alongiez dedens, et i viegne fistule;	And it is necessary that you pierce the abscess when it is ripe for digestion completed, rather than that which is beyond the foundation, so that it does not putrefy and be long inside, and a fistula will come.
et ne puisse saner en grant termine.	and cannot heal in a long time.
Et covient que tu saiches l’oure de la perforation de l’aposteme qui est meur selonc l’acomplissement, et c’est quant li dolor est apaisie, et li departemens de la fievre, et l’amenuisement de la dolor et de la roujor, et dou debatement et de l’aguisement dou chief de l’aposteme, et les autres signes;	and it is recommended that you scrape the head of the abscess perforation according to its completion, and this is when the pain is eased, and the departure of fever, and the lessening of pain and swelling, and the decrease in debatement and relief of the main symptoms of the abscess, and the others.
et covient que tu faices seoir la perforation ou plus dependant leu de l’aposteme, et la ou il apert mues;	and it is recommended that you make the perforation sit lower than the abscess, and where it opens more widely.
et soit li perforation dou lonc dou cors, et se li apostemes est as mains ou as piez, ou en jointures et au ners et as arteres, et en toz leus igalz ou il n’a point de ploieure.	and the perforation should be long and straight, and if the abscess is in the hands or feet, or in joints and nerves and arteries, and in all these places evenly without any bleeding.
En ces que ploient, par selonc celui membre.	In these cases, according to the position of that limb.
Et quant apostemes est en leu charnut, si vaut mues que tu laisses la perforation tant qu’il soit confermez en digestion acomplie, si com nos avons dit.	And when abscesses are in the chest, it is better to leave the incision until it is confirmed that digestion has been completed, as we have said.
Car se tu lou perces devant ceu, si iert alongiez li cors dou venim de lui, et est plains de mout d’ordure;	For if you pierce it before heaven, then the blood of the vein flows along with it, and it is full of much filth.
et par aventure endurcissent les levres et li parfondetez de lui.	And perhaps they harden the lips and pierce through them.
Et si a aucun aposteme que sont perciet selonc le large dou cors, selonc ceu que li membres en ait mestier.	And if any abscess that is pierced according to the width of the arm, according to what the limb has need of.
Et covient que tu amenistres em petis apostemes, petis pertus;	And it is necessary that you apply small abscesses, small holes.
et en grans apostemes, grans pertus, et maintes fendures selonc la semblance de la grandor de l’aposteme;	And in large abscesses, large holes, and many cuts according to the resemblance of the size of the abscess.
et si a de tels apostemes ou il covient chever lou keur, et coper;	And if there are such abscesses or it is necessary to cover and protect them.
quant il est jai devenus ausi com I drapelz, et est amortis, si covient faire ausi com on fait as bubes:	When it has become just like the cloth, and is softened, then you should do as one does with rags.
et si a de telz que sont fendut en III angles, et si a de telz dont on cope ausi com la fuelle de mirte, si com apostemes des angres;	and if there are some that are cut into three angles, and if there are some that are treated as the back of a mullet, as in abscesses;
et si a de telz ou on fait une reonde taille, et autres tailles et semblant copeure.	and if there are some where one makes a round incision, and other incisions and similar coverings.
Cil qui n’ont point de chief, si com aposteme souef superficial, il covient que tu lou perces plainnement;	Those who have no head, as in superficial abscesses, it is necessary that you puncture clearly;
et covient quant li apostemes est gros, et il a coillit grant bowe, et tu lou perces, si ne traire mie toute la bowe en celle houre, mais en trai une partie;	and when the abscess is large, and it has much pus, and you puncture, do not draw out all the pus in that hour, but a part of it;
puis estoupe l’aposteme jusc’a l’autre jor, puis en trai aucune chose derechief;	then flatten the abscess just after, then draw out nothing else immediately;
fai ceu par maintes fois de greit en greit, tant que li bowe isse toute;	Repeat the procedure for many times until the bowels are completely empty.
meismement se li malaides est de foible vertut, ou femme portans, ou petis enfes, ou viez hons decrepites.	Even if the patient has weak vitality, is pregnant, or a small child, or an elderly person with decrepit bones.
Car li esperis tressaut aucune fois avec l’issue de la bowe, que par aventure muert li malaides, et tu ne t’en persois.	For the experienced never treats the wound once with the outflow of the pus, because by chance the abscess may die, and you will not be harmed.
Eschuez donques cest chapistre par grant cautele, et quant tu as perciet ton aposteme, si essue la plaie, et regarde se li plaie de l’aposteme est petite;	Therefore avoid this chapter with great caution, and when you have pierced your abscess, dress the wound, and check if the wound from the abscess is small;
et se c’est une tailleure plainne, si amenistre tentes de lin ou de viez coton;	and if it is a large opening, apply bandages of linen or old cotton.
et se c’est uns grans apostemes, et il i a mout de pertus, si covient que tu boutes en chescun une tente si qu’ele viegne l’une contre l’autre;	and if there are large abscesses and much pus, it is necessary that you place a bandage in each one so that they come together against each other.
et se tu as copeit en l’aposteme une partie dou cuir, et tu l’as cheveit entor, si covient que tu l’emplisses de viel couton ou de rasure de dras de lin sens moistor, et le lie jusc’au tier jor;	and if you have pierced a part of the skin in an abscess, and you have wrapped it around, then you must fill it with old cotton or shredded linen against moisture, and bind it to the wound with a bandage.
puis l’oste, et le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	then the bone, and the ointment for the wound until it is healed.
Et se decorremens de sanc avient a ton ovraige, si amenistre aigue froide et aisil, et moille I drapeil, et met sor le leu decorrant par maintes fois.	And if there is blood when working on your task, apply sharp cold and wet, and clean the instrument, and place it on the dislocated joint multiple times.
Et se li decorremens de sanc persevere, se i amenistre governement et cure, et les poudres que j’ai dit em mains leus en cest livre, et se c’est ou tens d’iver, et li leus ou li apostemes est est mout nervous, si couvient que tu mettes sus tentes et drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile chaut;	and if the bleeding persists, and is not stopped by government and treatment, and the powders that I have mentioned in this book are not effective, and if it is very painful, then it is recommended to apply leeches and damp cloths soaked in wine and oil.
et se c’est en esteit, et li leus est charnus, si covient que tu mes sus drapelz moilliez en aigue et en oile, ou en vin et en oile froit, jusc’au tier jor, si com nos avons dit;	If it is in this state, and the joint is charred, then you must apply warm cloths soaked in vinegar and oil, or in wine and oil heated, as we have said.
et puis deslie l’aposteme et l’essue et le cure, si com il covient, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then drain the abscess and dress it, and treat it as necessary until it is healed.
Et ceu covient il conoistre universement en cures des apostemes:	And it is necessary to know universally in the treatment of abscesses:
or vos ai dit coment on doit aler avant as cures des apostemes, et vez ci le chapistre.	as I have told you how to proceed before treating abscesses, and see the chapter.
des soros	des soros
Ou keur dou chief vienent petis apostemes, et sont manieres de nous que sont en toiles, ausi com li josier d’une geline, et mout en i a de semblances.	When small abscesses come from the head, and there are ways of them that are in cloths, like the lance of a swallow, and many there are.
Il en i a de gras et de telz ou il a moistor ausi com poulz;	There are some and such as have moisture like chickens;
et si a de telz qui sont dur et pierous au taillier, et n’i a point de doutance se li artere n’i fait contraire.	And for those who are hard and rough to cut, there is no doubt if the artery is not cut against.
Et li ovraiges de la taille si est que tu esprueve a tout I estrument qui est apelez «entromissoire», de coi li forme vient ci aprés, quel chose il contient.	And the work of the cut is such that you prove with all the tool called "entromissoire", from which the form comes after, what thing it contains.
Car s’il contient moistor, si lou fent par desus dou lonc.	If it contains moisture, then it makes it from above downwards long.
Et quant li moistor est vuidie, si escorche sens rien laissier la peil qui contient celle moistor, car il revient adés quant on i laisse rien;	And when the moisture is drained, scrape off without leaving any hair that contains that moisture, for it will return if left alone.
puis plonge coton en oignement egiptien, s’il est presens;	Then soak cotton in Egyptian oil, if present.
se ceu non, en aigue et en seil, et en emple la plaie, et la laisse jusc’a l’autre jor;	If not, use vinegar and salt, and apply to the wound, and leave it there until the next day.
et ceu corront ceu qui est demorez dou nit.	And cover it with a clean cloth that remains at night.
Et pues rencomence lou coton, si com devant, le second jor, et lou tier, tant que tu saiches bien qu’il ne demoure point dou nit;	And then restart the cotton, as before, on the second day, and the dressing, until you are sure it will not remain at night.
puis cure la plaie d’oignement a ceu convenauble, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat the wound of inflammation according to what is suitable, until it is healed.
Et se li apostemes tient I nout gras, si le cope selonc ceste forme, dou lonc;	And if the abscess remains large, then cut it according to this form, long.
et i giete tes oncines, et l’escorche de toutes pars, et met toute ta cure de traire fuer la cotte ou il gist;	And pour your salves and the scar tissue from all parts, and put all your care into drawing out the pus where it is located.
et se li artere te fait contraire, si fai ceu que je t’ai dit aprés.	And if the artery makes it difficult, then do what I told you afterwards.
Et ausi fai de l’aposteme s’il est pierous, et dou taillier et dou curer si com je t’ai dit.	And so do with the abscess if it is piercing, and cut and cure as I have told you.
Et li taille sus l’aposteme pierous et le moiste, si est plus legiere, car il sont de poc de sanc.	And when cutting into the piercing abscess and the moist, it is lighter, for they are of little blood.
Et si a aucuns de ces apostemes ou chief ou il n’a point de moistor, et de ces fut I apostemes que je copai ou chief d’une vielle femme;	And if any of these abscesses or wounds do not have moisture, and are from the type of old woman that I copied or wrote about;
et trovai l’aposteme ausi com une piere xourde, aspre et blainche, et ne pooit brisier;	and found the abscess like a hard, rough, and white stone, which could not be broken.
et s’on en eust ferut aucun, on li eust ausi bien fait plaie com d’une piere.	and if they had made any incision, it would have been just as bad as a stone wound.
En autres apostemes venans ou chief, fuer que ces qui vienent as chief des enfans et as racines des oreilles, li overture si soit toz jors au plus dependant leu, por mues issir la bowe;	In other abscesses coming or near, it was because those who come to the head of children and roots of ears, the opening should always be at the most dependent part, so that the pus can come out.
et les cure si com il covient.	and treat them as appropriate.
des scrophules	of tumors
Maintes fois avienent cist aposteme au col, et desoz les asseles, et ens angres, et aucune fois vienent autre part ou cors, et sont mout, et sont enjanrees l’une avec l’autre.	Many times there are abscesses at the neck, and they are removed with forceps, and then they are opened, and sometimes they come from other parts of the body or chest, and they are large, and they are joined together.
Et chescune scrophule est proprement dedens sa cote, si com li nout et li aposteme dou chief, si com nos avons dit;	And each scrofulous swelling is properly within its side, like the neck and abscess of the head, as we have said.
et les semblances de ces scrophules sont maintes.	and similar scrofula are many.
Il i a de teles que contienent moistor, et si a de malignes qui ne vuellent obeir a santeit.	There are some things that contain moisture, and if there are evil ones who do not want to obey health.
en celle donques que tu vois de bone disposition au tochier, et est semblans a la color dou cors, et muet de chescune part et n’est mie aerse as ners dou col ne a l’artere ne au conduit, et n’est mie parfonde;	in that one you see of good disposition to the touch, and similar in color to the flesh, and moves from every part and is not attached to the bone or the artery or the vessel, and is not deeply rooted;
si covient que tu la copes par desus, et l’escorche de chescune partie, et estent les II levres dou keur as oncines, se tu en as mestier, si com nos avons dit en apostemes dou chief;	if it is necessary to remove it from above, and scrape every part, and place the two lips of the wound together as one, if you have skill, as we have said in abscesses of the head;
et la trai poc et poc, et soies seur que tu ne coper lou nerf ne la voine, et ne soit mie li spatumile agus ne trenchans, que li mains n’eschaipe, et ne voise trop avant, que tu ne coper mie ceu que tu ne dois.	and pull it out slowly and carefully, and be sure that you do not cover the nerve or the vein, and is not too thin or too sharp, so that the hand does not slip, and do not expose it too soon, until you have covered what you should.
Et se tu copes la voinne ou l’artere, et ceu ne te laisse ovrer, si met en la plaie vitriole broiet, ou aucunes poudres que restainchent sanc, et estraint la plaie;	And if you cut the vein or artery, and it does not stop bleeding, pour vitriol broth or some powders that stop blood flow into the wound, and apply pressure.
et la laisse tant que li apostemes soit apaisiez, et soit amollie li plaie, et encomence a porrir.	and let it bleed until the abscess is calmed, and the wound is soothed, and then begin to bind it.
Et quant li sans est estainchiez, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que tu l’acomplisses;	And when the wound is cleansed, return to your work until you complete it.
puis quier a ton doit indice s’il i demoure nules petites scrophules, si les cope et les munde.	Then check if there are any remaining small pus pockets, and cut them out and drain them.
Et s’il a en la racine de la scrophule voinne grant, si ne covient mie que tu copes celle scrophule en sa racine, mais la lie d’un fil double fort, et la laisse cheoir par li, sens nuisement;	And if there is a large vein in the base of the abscess, it is not recommended that you cut that abscess at its base, but tie it with a strong doubled thread, and let it drop through, without causing harm.
puis emple la plaie de viel coton plongiet en oignement egiptien, puis la cure.	Then apply a wound of old cotton soaked in Egyptian ointment, then the treatment.
Et se tu copes toute la scrophule, si covient que tu assembles les II levres de la plaie, et les cout maintenant, puis qu’il n’i a point demoreit de superfluiteit por la grandor de la scrophule.	And if you have completely removed the scab, it is necessary that you gather the two lips of the wound and hold them together, then as there is no excess due to the size of the scab.
si covient que tu entendes a coper la racine de li, et traire fuer, et la cout si com nos avons dit.	and you should cover the root of it with a bandage and pull out the thorn, and hold it as we have said.
Celles scrophules que tienent superfluiteit, perce lai ou il apert meure;	Those abscesses that hold excess fluid, pierce where it opens and dies;
et la perce ensi com celle devant dite, en dependant, puis i amenistre tentes avec oignement et semblans choses, si qu’elle corrompe ceu qui est demorez de la corruption;	And pierce it in such a way as the one previously mentioned, depending, then apply bandages with ointment and similar things, so that it corrupts what remains of the corruption;
et quant li plaie est bien mundee, si la cure d’oignement enjanrant char, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when the wound is well bandaged, the treatment with healing ointment until it is healed.
de squinance	of the dislocation
Li ancien dirent et parlerent de la tailleure de la gorge;	The ancients said and spoke of the throat cutter;
mais je ne vis onques en nostre terre qui la feist, et c’est li escripture de lor parole.	but I have never seen such a thing in our land, and it is their written account of their words.
A ces qui ont squinance, il covient que li fendure de la gorge qui est apelee «epiglote» soit eschuee;	For those who have hernias, the neck's part called "epiglottis" must be avoided.
et c’on ne faice aide par ceu, por ceu que toutes les voines et li pormon dou malaide sont a ces qui ont aposteme chaut en la bouche, ou en la gorge ou en II amandres.	and it cannot be helped by this, because all the veins and the root of the evil are in those who have abscesses full in the mouth, or in the throat or in the armpits.
Quant li maladie est en la chenal dou pormon, il covient coper l’epiglote por fuir la perdition qui vient de l’estranglement.	When the disease is in the throat pore, it is necessary to cover the epiglottis to avoid the danger of strangulation.
Il covient donques, quant nos volons fendre l’epiglote, que nos le fendons desoz III cercles ou IIII une petite fendure dou travers, entre les II cercles ou par la quantiteit de la fendure dou syfac, ne mie en la cartillaige;	Therefore, when we want to cut the epiglottis, we must cut it outside three circles or four a small cut across, between the two circles or by the quantity of the cut of the throat, not in the cartilage.
et cil leus si est covenaubles a la section de l’epiglote qu’il n’i a point de char, et li vasseil sont lonc d’enqui.	and those who are not accustomed to the section of the epiglottis, as there is no cartilage, and the valves are long and narrow.
Et se li maistres est paourous, si covient qu’il estende le cuir de la gorge a tout l’oncine, puis fende lou keur tant qu’il viegne a la cheneil;	And if the master is cowardly, then it is necessary to stretch the skin of the neck all around, then cut the throat until it reaches the windpipe.
et eschue les vasselz de sanc, se tu vois aucune chose, et puis cope lou syfac, si com nos avons dit;	And avoid the blood vessels of blood, if you see anything, and then cut the sinew, as we have said.
et est demostrez par la section dou fleume de la cheneil ki saut fuer par le leu qui est rompus, et par la defaute de la voix;	And it is demonstrated by the section of the flap of the windpipe that jumps out through the limb that is broken, and by the lack of voice.
et laisse la plaie overte une piece.	and leave the wound open for a piece.
Et quant li houre est passee de coi on doute l’estranglement, assemble les II levres de la plaie dou keur, et la cout toute soule sens la cartillaige;	And when the hour is passed for which we doubt strangulation, bring together the two lips of the wound carefully, and stitch it all together without the cartilage;
puis aministre medicines qui font naistre char, tant qu’il soit sanez.	then administer medicines that cause heat to rise until they are healed.
Albucasim dist c’on ne faice ce jusc’a tant que li gorge est toute estoupee, et li malaides est jugiez a mort, et li defaut li alaine.	Albucasim says that one should not do this unless the throat is completely stunned, and the limbs are judged to be dead, and the defect is paralyzed.
Adonques cope on l’epiglote por ceu que li malaides ne puet alener, et il respire par la plaie, et ensi est gardez de mort;	Therefore, one must cover the epiglottis because the hairs cannot keep it in place, and he breathes through the wound, and thus is kept from death;
et por ce commanderent li anciain a laissier la plaie overte tant que li malice de la maladie soit passee, et elle est passee en III jors ou en IIII Et adonques il comanderent a coudre la plaie et curer, tant qu’elle fut curee;	and because the ancients ordered to leave the wound open until the malice of the disease has passed, and it has passed in three days or four, and then they ordered to stitch the wound and heal, as long as it was healed;
et je vos dirai ceu que je vis.	and I will tell you what I saw.
Je vis que une damoisele prist I coutel, et le ficha en sa gorge, et copa partie des chenelz dou pormon;	I saw a young lady take a knife and stab herself in the throat, cutting part of her jugular vein.
et je fui apelez por li curer, et la trovai ausi com morte.	and I was called to cure her, and found her as if dead.
Je descovris la plaie, et trovai le sanc qui en estoit issus, et soi bien qu’elle n’avoit mie copeit voine ne conduit fuer que la gorge, et li vens issoit fuer par la plaie.	I discovered the wound, and found the arrow that had come out of it, and although she had not bled much from the vein except for the throat, and the blood flowed through the wound.
Je me hastai, et cousi la plaie, et la curai tant qu’elle fut sanee;	I hurried, and sewed the wound, and healed it until she was well.
et n’avint a la damoisele fuer qu’elle fut roge de voix, et revint aprés a sa disposition;	and there was nothing left to the young lady but that she was hoarse, and returned to her usual state.
por ceu di je que en la tailleure de l’epiglote n’ait mie paour.	because I know that in the throat there is no fear.
de la grosse gorge	of the large throat
Cist apostemes est apelez «hernie de gorge», et est uns grans apostemes en color d’une jaisse, et est molt en femmes;	This abscess is called "hernia of the throat", and is a large abscess in the color of pus, and is very common in women;
et est selonc II manieres:	and there are two ways:
naturez, et accidens;	natural, and accidental;
ou natureil n’a point d’engien.	or natural, without cause.
Et li accidens est selonc II manieres, de coi l’une est semblans a gras nous, et li autre maniere est semblans a aposteme qui vient de nous d’artere;	And accidental is in two ways, one of which is similar to our gout, and the other way is similar to an abscess that comes from us through the artery.
et il i ait paour, et ne covient mie ovrer de feir fuers que en celi qui est petite, et le prueve et cerche a tout l’intromissoire:	and there is fear, and it does not require to be treated with fire except in the small one, and the proof and search are made throughout the whole body:
se tu le trueves ausi com I nout gras, et ne pent a nulle voine, si le cope, si com on cope les nous, et le trai a tout sa coife, s’il en i a point;	if you treat it as you would gout, and cannot find any vein, if the copper, as we do for ours, and bring it to all its clothing, if there is none.
et encerche bien tot, et le cure si com il covient, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	and search for it quickly, and treat it as it should be, until it is healed perfectly.
des nous	of us
Maintes manieres de nous sont, dont je dirai toutes les semblances;	Many methods we have, of which I will say all the similarities;
et or covient que je die toute la difference qui est entre nout et issue.	and now it is fitting that I tell you all the differences between us and them.
Je dis que issue est chalors et fievre tenans, tant que li ebulicions est passee, et est acomplie li porriture;	I say that they are hot and feverish, until the boils have passed, and is accomplished by the pustulation;
adonques repose li fievre et li chalor.	therefore the fever and heat subside.
Avec lou nout n’a ne chalor ne fievre ne dolor, et contient I syfac, qui est ses propres sac et est selonc la color dou cors, et encomence ausi com une jaisse, et devient gros;	With us there is no heat or fever or pain, and it contains the abscess, which is its own pus and is according to the color of the skin, and begins like a small sore, and becomes large;
et sont selonc II semblances, ou grais, ou moiste, et mout de color sont si com j’ai dit en la division.	And there are two kinds, dry or moist, and many colors, as I have said in the division.
Il covient, quant tu viens a la cure dou nout, que tu esprueves et l’enquier premierement a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «entromissoire», selonc ce que sa forme venra ou chapistre qui est aprés.	It is necessary, when coming to the care of a new patient, to first test and inquire about the "entromissoire" instrument, according to its form as it appears in the following chapter or book.
Et li maniere de l’inquisicion des apostemes des nous est que tu preignes ou plus moiste leu que tu trueves en l’aposteme, et torne tes dois poc et poc, tant que tu saiches que li estrumens ait perciet le keur, puis que ce soit selonc la grandor de l’aposteme;	And the method for examining abscesses of ours is that you grasp or slightly moistened cloth that you insert into the abscess, and turn your fingers gently, until you feel that the instrument has pierced the core, then it is according to the size of the abscess;
puis estrai l’entromissoire, et pren garde en ceu que saut fuer.	then extract the contents, and be careful that it does not spray.
Se moistor corrans cort, queil color elle ait, si le fent si com j’ai dit des autres apostemes;	If the running wound is moist, of whatever color it has, make it as I have said for other abscesses.
et se aprés l’entromissoire nen vient moistor, saiches qu’il est gras, si le fent donques en croix, et le prent as pinceures, et l’escorche legierement de chescune part et warde la cotte ou il gist que tu la traies saine avec le nout;	and if afterwards the joint becomes moist, take away the grease, then cut it in a cross shape, and take pincers, and lightly scrape off every part and wash the coat or where it was with clean water;
et se tu ne la pues traire saine, si la trai par pieces si qu’il n’i demoure rien.	and if you cannot remove it cleanly, then tear it in pieces so that nothing remains.
Car s’il i demoure rien, si revient li nous par maintes fois;	For if anything remains, it returns to us many times;
et s’il en demore un poc, et li sans te grieve, si emple la plaie d’aucunes poudres corrosives agues, et estraint la plaie, et met sus choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	and if it remains for a little while and does not bother you, then apply some corrosive powders to the wound, and strain the wound, and put on things that calm abscesses, and treat other cures until it is healed.
et se li nous est grans, si cout les II levres de la plaie, et le cure de ceu qui enjanre char.	and if it is large, use two fingers of the wound, and treat the wound with charcoal.
et se li voine batans t’est contraire ou autre si te haste et emple le leu de vitriole broiet, et lou laisse liiet II jors ou III, tant que li plaie porrisse, et repose li ebulicion dou sanc;	and if it is against or other if you hasten and fill the wound with broken glass, and leave it for two hours or three, until the wound heals, and rest the discharge of blood;
puis revien au coper ceu que i est demoreit dou nout.	then return to the copper that is left out of the water.
Vez ci les formes des estrumens entromissoires, et sont de III manieres:	See the shapes of the instruments inserted, and they are of three kinds:
grans et moien et petit;	large and medium and small;
et s’en i a III quarrez qui sont apelez «albaret», et I qui est apelez «breb», et s’en i a de III manieres:	and there are three kinds of quarters that are called "albaret", and one that is called "breb", and there are three ways:
grant, moien, et petit, por encerchier les apostemes de fistule;	great, medium, and small, to search for the abscesses of fistulas.
et sont ausi com les aguilles dont on cout les sorceles, et sont d’arain citrin, ou de fer, ou d’argent, et mues valent cil qui sont jaune, et sont plus esprovez de plonc noir por encerchier les corbeures de fistule;	They are also like the needles used to extract them, and are of gold, or iron, or silver, and cost as much as those that are yellow, and are more experienced at removing black pus from fistula boils.
et sont de III manieres:	And there are three ways:
grans, moiens, et petis, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce des pertus.	great, medium, and small, according to the amount of the size of the fistulas.
Les formes des oncines sont de mout de semblances, si com tu vois ci:	The shapes of needles are of many similarities, such as you see here:
grans, moiens, et petis;	great, medium, and small.
et si a oncines qui ont II corbeures de III manieres ausi;	And if there are bones with two crowns of three kinds;
et si a oncines qui ont III corbeures, et sont ausi de III manieres;	And if there are bones with three crowns, and they are also of three kinds;
et si a oncines qui ont II corbeures, et oncines d’une corbeure soulement, et sont de III manieres;	And if there are bones with two crowns, and bones of one crown only, and they are also of three kinds;
et tuit cist sont necessaire en lor leu.	And all these are necessary in their place.
Li chief de ces a coi on fent sont trenchant, et de telz i a qui ne taillent mie fuer que d’une part, dont on escorche les nous, por ceu c’on ne cope la voine ne le nerf;	The main ones of which they are made are cutting, and there are some that do not cut much more than one part, from which we peel the flesh, because otherwise they would cut the vein or the nerve;
et de ces intromissoires sont les alemeles reponues en mainches, si que li malaide ne s’en persoivent a l’overture des apostemes;	And among these intermediaries are the awls inserted into handles, so that the pain does not persist at the opening of the abscesses;
et sont de III manieres:	There are three ways:
grant, petit, et moien, si com tu vois;	great, small, and medium, as you see.
et n’en use on mie fuer que en leu charnut, si com jambes, et bras, et mameles, et as angres, et en semblans leus;	and we only use them in the joints, such as knees, arms, shoulders, and similar joints.
et aucune fois fait on I autre estrument petit, semblant a escorces de fistices, selonc ceste forme, a coi on estainche sanc:	and never made another small instrument like the scrapers of pustules, according to this form, with which we drain blood.
et le met on aucune fois au leu qui saine a copement des voines, et as arteres, et aucune fois reont selonc ceste grant forme:	and it is never placed back into its proper position which can cope with veins, and arteries, and it always returns according to this great form:
Aucune fois enflent les mameles d’aucuns homes quant cil encomencent estre corrumput, tant qu’eles semblent mameles de feme;	Never inflate the breasts of some men when they begin to rot, until they seem like the breasts of a woman.
et demorent laides et enflees, et qui les vuet curer, si le covient soier selonc ceste forme des ceste ligne .b. jusques a .g.:	and they remain swollen and infected, and whoever wants to heal them, if it is necessary according to this form of this line from b to g:
puis escorche la graisse, et emple la plaie de medicine enjanrant char, puis assemble les II levres de la plaie a costure, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee;	Then scrape off the fat, and fill the wound with healing ointment, then sew together the two lips of the wound by stitching, and care for it until it is healed.
et se li mamele cline aval, et est amolie por sa grandor si com il avient as femmes, si la fent en II costelz desus, par II semblans fendures;	And if the wound is large and widespread, like those seen in women, then make incisions in two places above, similar to tears.
de coi l’une soit tenans a l’autre a la fin de l’une et de l’autre, si que li plus grans ligne conteigne la menor selonc ceste forme, des ceste ligne .b. jusc’a la ligne .g.;	To hold the one to the other at the end of one and the other, so that the larger line contains the smaller according to this form, from this line .b. to the line .g.
puis escorche le cuir qui est entre les II levres, et oste la graisse, et i amenistre ceu que nos avons dit de costure et de poudres, et ceu qui est necessaire en la cure, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then scrape off the skin that is between the two lips, and remove the fat, and follow what we have said about stitching and powders, and what is necessary in care until it is healed.
et s’il n’est sanez, ou li incision n’est mie toute faite, por ceu que li malaides ne vuet reposer, ou por le decorrement de sanc, si covient que tu emplisses la plaie de coton moilliet en oignement corrosif;	If it is not well-healed, or the incision is not completely made, because the hairs do not want to rest, or due to the flow of blood, then you must fill the wound with cotton moistened in a caustic ointment.
et le laisse tant qu’il menjuce le remenant et la graisse, puis le cure tant qu’il soit saneis.	Let it remain until it melts the remaining and the grease, then cure it until it is healed.
des apostemes des asselles	of abscesses of the ankles
Cist apostemes que vienent desoz les asseles sont manieres de scrophules dures ou il ait cotes, et s’en i a que contienent moistor.	These abscesses that come from the ankles are ways of hard scrofula or when there are pustules, and they contain moisture.
Cil donques qui contienent moistor covient qu’il soient copez selonc ceste forme, des la ligne .b. jusc’a la ligne .g.:	Those that contain moisture should be cut according to this form, from the line b to the line g:
Et quant toute li bowe qui est en l’aposteme est vuidie, si emple la plaie de viel coton, et la laisse jusc’a l’autre jor, puis oste tout le coton, et cure d’oignement avenant a ceu tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when all the pus in the abscess is drained, apply old cotton to the wound and leave it until the next day, then remove all the cotton and care for the wound with a poultice until it is healed.
Et se li apostemes est de semblances de scrophules, si le fent si com nos avons dit en fendures des scrophules, et se li plaie rent bowe, si amenistre cautere si com nos avons dit devant.	And if the abscesses are similar to scrofula, then cut them as we have said in incisions of scrofula, and if the wound does not heal, then cauterize it as we have said before.
de la routure de l’artere	of the tearing of the artery
Quant li artere est route, et li cuir est soudez qui est sus, si en vient maintes fois apostemes, et tout aussi avient il a la voine enflee et aposteme;	When the artery is cut, and the skin above it is dry, often abscesses form, and just as often there is bleeding from the vein and abscess.
