puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac, et depart ceu qui est derrier l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac;	Then push your index finger into the place that leads to the bone, between the white skin that is outside the ribs and between the second skin, and behind the rib, and between the second skin.
et pues muef a la main destre dedens lou keur des coions, et estent lou blanc syfac en haut a ta main senestre, et lieve l’uef a tout lou syfac devers la taille;	and then move the finger to the right inside the curve of the nail, and place the white thread on top of your left hand, and lift the eyelid over the entire face towards the waist;
et comande au ministre qu’il estende l’uef en haut, et deslie ceu qui est aers derrier le liement;	and command the minister to extend the eyelid upwards, and release what is behind the lower lid;
et quier a tes dois s’il a point de l’intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz;	and ask if he has any intestine wrapped or white thread hard, and if you find nothing, then let him blow into the belly outwards;
puis pren une aguille ou il ait I gros fil fait de X filz, et la boute en la derriere partie dou syfac, qui est aprés lou cuir des coions;	then take a needle or a thick thread made of several threads, and blow into the back part of the eyelid, which is after the skin of the nail;
aprés la taille, puis cope les chiés qui apperent des filz, tant qu’il i ait IIII filz;	After the waist, then cut the tendons that appear from the hairs, until there are four hairs.
puis les assemble l’un sus l’autre en maniere de croix, et en lie lou syfac, dont nos avons dit qui est desoz lou cuir des coions, d’un fort liien de II pars;	Then assemble them one above the other in the shape of a cross, and tie it with a thread of two parts from the skin of pigs, which we have said is strong.
puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de II pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n’i viegne;	Then wrap the tendons of hairs, and tie them in two parts, so that none of the wounds that they cause can enter into the flesh, so that an abscess does not occur.
et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc II dois de celui, et aprés ces II liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d’un doi;	And then put the thread along the first thread of two parts of that, and after these two threads leave the thread which is from the skin of pigs, the great one of a dozen.
et aprés tout l’autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte;	and then all the other according to the roundness that the horse carries.
puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant;	then cut in the part that is outside the skin of the hooves, as we have said before.
puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.	then apply a moistened linen cloth in oil, and put it on the wounds, and apply the remedy that we have mentioned.
Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	And never cauterize the white facial wound that we have mentioned, after incision, due to fear of blood clotting.
Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui;	for this has happened many times, and leave the cloth until it heals through it.
et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece;	and if it is slow to fall off, then soak in hot vinegar, and put on what we have said until it heals.
puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	then treat the wound with other treatment, until it is healed perfectly.
de hernie carnouse	of hernia carbuncle
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	In this branch, I have never seen anyone dare to perform the cure by iron.
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz;	And the ancients said that it is made so as to be like the branch that is together with the view, in a way that you bind the vessels, after the cut slightly above the leg lightly.
puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient;	then cover it with a cloth, and treat the abscess of that which works, until the vessels die.
et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and the treatment as we have said, until it is healed.
Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus;	Never comes rupture and tears, as we have said, and open the veins;
et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres;	and do not make any incisions into the intestines, and if they do, it is rare, and repair them hourly.
et toutevoie s’il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent;	and in any case, if it remains too long in this state, the wound or abscess will continue to spread until the intestines are exposed.
et ceu avient par l’estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert;	and this will happen due to the extension of the abscess which is at the angles, as we have said, because it is stretched, then softened and inflated and opened.
et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit;	and the treatment is by cauterization, as we have previously mentioned.
et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere:	and never is the treatment done in this way:
et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de III dois;	and it is that the misaligned bones are often pushed up against their back between your hands, then wrap the joint with a cloth inflated to the size of three fingers;
et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l’ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac;	then strain the sinew that is outside the skin that toughens it, then take the raw and put it on top of the joint appearing from the sinew;
et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les II leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l’un et l’autre;	and press against the front of the belly, then cut the two joints appearing from the sinew above the head of the raw, and cut both;
puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n’estendre l’uef n’autre chose, si com je t’ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines;	then strain the head of the raw, and do not cover the sinew nor extend the belly or anything else, as I have told you in the treatment of the broken rib;
puis le cure par la cure des plaies.	Then, treat with the treatment of wounds.
Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	And when you cut the ligaments, defend and heal the wound until it is healed.
Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	The wound is closed, and does not appear in the tear, and the cauterization is quiet in this limb, and closer to healing.
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	of the softening of the leather of the shoes
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir;	Many times, the leather of the knees is softened in some men, because the chariots that are inside are softened, and it is to be seen.
et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil;	And it is a matter, when one wants to cure it, that one makes the painful part lie on its back, and the copper on the softened skin over the natural skin;
puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a III costures ou IIII fermement;	then gather the two lips to a seam, and if you see, cut off the excess of the softened skin at three or four seams;
puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	then cover between the seams, and treat it like other wounds, until it is healed, and cut off the thread.
dou chastrement	tremblingly
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre;	Since it is customary in our law to use such things, and because I would prefer not to speak of them in this book;
et n’est necessaires fuer que por II manieres:	and they are only necessary for two purposes:
dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure;	one is that the patient may answer when asked, and in seclusion, the care;
et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes.	and the other is because we often have need of castration for animals to help us, such as goats and sheep and rams and others.
Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc II manieres:	I say therefore that castration is done in two ways:
ou par atraction, ou par fendure.	or by traction, or by cutting.
En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant;	In what we do by traction, let us sit the animal in high heat, until the ligaments are softened and during.
puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.	Then pinch them with your hand, until they are returned and you no longer feel them.
Du chastrement de taille:	Of the severe treatment of the waist:
covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a I cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez;	You should sterilize the animal, and press the skin of the ligaments with your right hand, then tie the suspensory, and scorch each one as you have them.
et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz;	And leave no pus or subtle pus that is on the tendons;
et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure;	And this method of severe treatment is more effective than that which is done by traction, because at traction something remains in the ligaments, by which the animal desires to luxate.
puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	Then treat the wound until it is healed.
des hermofrodites	For hermaphrodites
Hermofrodie est selonc II manieres as homes:	There are two main methods for men:
l’une si est que entre les II coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.	One method is that between the two testicles, open as wide as the natural shape of a woman, with hair, and sometimes cutting into the urine.
Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et II coions.	And the other method is in women, and it is like a finger as a rod and two knives.
Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies;	And the treatment of the man and the woman is that you cut off all the hair around the wounds, and treat them as other wounds;
en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	In the second method, men who urinate through the skin of the testicles have no treatment.
de la tentigene	of the tentigen
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir;	Shaving is hair that grows above the natural part, as long as it is too ugly to see;
et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure.	and some women have had it as large as a hand, and this is the care.
Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement;	It is necessary that you remove excessive swelling from your hand or fingers, and gently rub it.
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	and do not move it too much, as blood does not come, then treat other wounds until it is healed.
et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee».	and in another case where a child is born with a marshy mouth, and it is used, and sometimes it jumps out, and it is similar to a cow, and because of this they called the old "cow disease".
Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	If it is necessary to clean it as we have said the tenting, and the cure until it is healed.
de erratique	1. For the fire cautery, instruct
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis;	It is erratic whether the nature of the woman is not perceived, or the pustules are small.
et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est;	and is natural by birth, or accidental by disease that has come.
ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit;	or it is by fire cauterization, or deep lancing with a sharp knife, and is done in the marsh, or in the ribs, or elsewhere, or as it may be.
et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir;	and they prevent conception, and childbirth, and possibly the flowers to have.
et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile.	and the knowledge of this is by looking at the belly.
Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait.	2. If the patient is close and appears to be in distress, then approach them or go to them.
S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as II leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi:	If it is deep lancing with a sharp knife, and it is close to the liver, then you hurry, and do so thus:
met tes II dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes;	put your two fingers together, and the woman is on her back, spreading her legs;
puis estent les II leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens;	then the two books are formed, as long as the subtle surface is rounded, and is covered by the suppression.
puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder.	Then take linen, and dip it in oil, and place it on the limb, and grind the woman to a man every day, so that he cannot glue it.
Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte.	And if the swelling is hard and sharp, it is necessary to apply a poultice similar to a leaf of mint.
Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope;	If the suppression is of chalk, then dip it in water and cover it.
et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef;	and have the medicines steeped in blood, such as dragon's blood, incense, and an abundance of wax.

puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	then care for other treatments until they are healed.
Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez.	And when in the marsh there comes charcoal, then cover it according to this manner, unless it is an abscess.
Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	For abscess which is in the bone, one should not touch with fire.
des emorroides	for hemorrhoids
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul;	Varicose veins are openings of veins which do not usually heal, and when the varicose veins are old, they become ulcers;
et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation.	and we have had in the division the likes of them, and the signs, and I will say here those that receive treatment.
Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer.	I said that hemorrhoids and thromboses, when they are in the bone and do not open to the touch, can only be treated with fire.
Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer.	Those that are at the opening of the bone, which can be felt, are those that can be treated.
Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses;	Therefore, you should put the woman in a cold house, then stretch the ulcer with needles, and cover it with its roots, then powder over medicines restraining blood, such as acacia and dragon's blood and incense, and similar things;

Et se il estainche, c’est boin.	And if it stains, it's good.

Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when the abscess is at rest, treat the wound with ointment until it is healed.

des apostemes de la marris	of abscesses from the marsh
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division.	Many kinds of abscesses come from the marsh, such as chancre and pustular abscess and herpes and estiomenes and fistulas and hemorrhoids and chronic abscess, and many other diseases that I have mentioned in the section.
Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe;	Therefore, I must advise in this treating the abscess that comes from the marsh, which is not one of the abscesses that are filled with pus.
et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.	And if you know the work of iron, look at the abscess to see if it is agus in the beginning of its arrival, and plain of cholor and fever, and if it becomes red, and if you can see it.
Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie;	Therefore, do not rush to pierce it, but let it cool until the pain is relieved;

et covient que quant tu i vues amenistrer cest estrument, que tu fiches le rait premier ens por savoir la parfondeté de la marris, si que ceu qui entre ens de l’estrument n’i viegne plus em parfont qu’il ne doit, et qu’il ne blece la malaide;	And it is necessary that when you see this instrument to be administered, you first check the sharpness of the blade, so that what enters from the instrument does not come out more than it should, and that it does not cause harm.
et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve;	If the instrument is larger, it is necessary to cover the sharpness of the blade with cloths, so that the instrument does not hurt it.

Et quant li apostemes apert, et on lou fent a la main mol, si le covient coper au chief, au spatumile leit;	And when the abscesses are open, and they do it by hand a lot, then it is necessary to cover the head, at the spatula level.

de l’enfantement	of childbirth
Mestier est premier a la baile qu’elle conoisse la figure de l’enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l’ar:	The midwife is first to the birth that she knows the natural shape of the childbirth, and the signs if it is when you see the woman approaching, and wants to smell the air:
adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir;	then quickly take the child out.
adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui;	then check that this childbirth is according to the natural shape, and it is the first out with its head, and the second with him;
et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost;	and when you see these signs, it is necessary to gently press her belly, so that the child comes out quickly.
car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification;	because when it descends over its head, and the second is with him, and it is cleaned of its excesses by good washing.
et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment.	And this which comes otherwise does not come naturally.
Car il vient aucune fois sus ses piez, et vient fuer li cors ou li chiés, et les mains, ou il vient sus son ventre, ou sovin, et est convertis par aventure sor son col, et par autres figures malvaises;	For it never comes above its feet, and comes from the back or the neck, and the hands, or it comes up its belly, or sometimes, and is turned by chance onto its shoulder, and by other bad figures.
si est mestier a la baile qu’elle soit saige et subtilz en ces choses, et se warse d’error et de decevement, et je vos mostrerai toutes les figures coment on li doit aidier.	If it is the business of the bath that she is wise and skillful in these things, and warns against error and deception, and I will show you all the figures as one should help her.
Se li enfes vient sus son chief par issue natureil, et li femme enfante griement, et li vertus de li est foible, si la fai seoir sus une selle, ou les femmes la tienent;	If the child comes up its head by natural birth, and the woman gives birth with great pain, and the child's strength is weak, then let the midwife sit on a seat, or the women hold her.

de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses piés	from the birth of the child above its feet
Quant li enfes vient sus ses piez, si lou covient bouter en haut;	When the child comes out of its feet, it is necessary to lift it up high.

de l’issue des gemelz	of the issue of twins
Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent III ou IIII;	It is said that gnomes are born many times, and sometimes they are born three or four at a time.
et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.	and this is not an uncommon thing, and it happens often.

je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude;	I know that they are multiplied, and they are destroyed by the sweat that causes them, which is tied to the skin;

de plusors enfans	of many children

si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	if he does according to what is necessary.
de l’enfant mort	of the dead child
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	When you care for the woman of the child dead or belly, as I have said in the division, and it does not come out, and you are forced to work by hand;

et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	and this is the shape of the needle:

et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	and then it is reset by moving from one side to the other, in order to move out, and hold the teeth together as follows:

et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	And if it does not remain, put this jaw higher and continue until it is all out.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement, si covient que tu envoloupes sus I drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	And if one hand comes in front of the other and it cannot be brought back by force, then wrap it around the other arm until it all comes out.
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as II piés.	Then, place the copper in the joint of the foot or the heel, and thus you should do in the other hand, and with two feet.
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee, si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	And if the child's head is large and it is stuck at the neck, or it has a sharp acute assembly, then you should push the spatula with spinous between your fingers, and make the head and extract the sharp.
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	or you break it with the tool called "almidach", from which the form comes with the tools or chapter that is after this one.
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	and thus do the same for the child naturally;
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles, et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	and then pull out the bones with pincers, and if the patient jumps forward and is held by the chin, it should be cut until the moisture that is inside or has come out is removed.
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	and if she cannot get out, cut the copper into pieces and use it to plug the hole.
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	and if it is inflated in the abdomen or out of the ribs, it should be pierced until the moisture runs out.
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	And if the arrow is above its feet, then the light attraction is on its legs, and the advice to the mouth of the marsh is light.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a I drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	and if it is swollen in the abdomen or in the groin, it should be stretched out on a cloth wrapped around your hand.
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	and cut the abdomen or the groin until the moisture that is inside runs out.
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure, si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	and if the other member is broken, and the patient cannot move it, then push the ball of the hand against the marsh, and pull it out through the mouth of the marsh;
puis i boute I oncine ou II, et le trai fuer;	then push the pin or II, and pull it out;
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier, ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	and if the mouth of the marsh is retracted due to an abscess that has come, then it does not need to be forced, but one must manage wet and fat things;
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	and apply poultices, and place in high moistening and softening agents.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	And if the infant is on its side, and you can put it straight, then manage as we have said for the living child;
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	And if they cannot, then let them try by pieces, and leave nothing of the second part.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	And when you have done this, let them treat as we have said in abscesses that come from the marsh.
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	And if an arrow comes out, it should be immediately bandaged and treated with other remedies.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut I autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	I saw a woman in whose belly an infant had died, then consulted the other with that one, and the other died.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After a long time, some abscesses appeared in the armpit, and they swelled up so much that they burst open, and began to cause great pain.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was called to the patient, and I thought for a long time, and could not close the wound.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I applied strong adhesive, and some bones were stuck to it, and after some time others were stuck as well.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I was very surprised because the belly does not have any bones.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	I thought it was the bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em millor point;	I dressed the wound, and in trying to remove the bone, the woman was not improved at all.
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	And the woman remained long like this, and then a little blood came from the wound.
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	And I did not remember this chapter until now because when the masters find something strange, they know how to use help.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	bring the marsh to its place
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres;	Here comes the form of the compressor, by which we apply the books.
et a II tornans as II chiés des II liiens.	And at the second turn, to the second question of the two joints.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	Nevertheless, the horn should be more slender than the restrainer, and be made of smooth or boxwood.
et soit li bouche dou fust I doi de large, et li marge des arbres I doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	And its mouth should be the width of a finger and a half, and the edge of the trees should be one palm and a half long.
et enmi les II liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	And between the two joints should be two additional pieces of this same wood, which are firmly fastened in one and the other, half a palm long or a little more.
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les II cornes.	And these two joints are placed in the mouth of the marsh when turning the two horns.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	Another form, with a more subtle and lighter appearance, should be made of flat iron or boxwood, according to the appearance of tongs.
et ait as II chiés II ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et II dois de large;	And it should have two joints, like you see, of a palm's length, and they should be wide.
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor I lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes, puis boute les II ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	And when you see that the marsh is being opened with all the instruments, then make the woman sit on the bed, with her feet hanging down and her legs open, then place the two joints inside the marsh, and hold the head of the instrument between her thighs.
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	Then work your hand with all the instruments, as you have done evenly, according to the quantity that you see opening the mouth of the marsh, until the bail does what it wants.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances;	These instruments are all above, and are multiplied in their similarities;
et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	And when the mirrors have them all matched, the work is more rapid, and higher as men for their quantity.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	If you do not despise this instrument because you have not prepared it, for their need is not excused.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the second is retained at childbirth, it is necessary that you command the pain to hold its hair, and then let her excrete from condition, and your hands to the mouth and nose;
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	If she jumps through the sky, well then.
Se ceu non, si prent I pot, et fai I pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	If the sky does not, then take a pot, and make a poultice or covering, and put herbs that can open the mouth of the marsh, such as calamint, anise, chamomile, cassia, and centaury.
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu;	All these herbs, or any of them, should be cooked or boiled over the fire.
puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris, et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris;	Then put a cloth or poultice from the pot in her mouth, and the other head in the mouth of the marsh, and let the steam come inside the marsh.
puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	Then make her spit, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	If the second method does not work.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature, et quiere la secondine;	And if she remains after this treatment and is not better, command the midwife to massage her right hand with olive oil or musk oil of high quality, and then rub it in the natural way, and apply the second one.
et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	And when she has found it, grasp and stretch it little by little and straight, so that the husband does not tear it during extraction.
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie;	But move it gently to the right and left, and then pull.
si venra et se desaerdra.	If it comes out and dislodges.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	And if the husband's mouth is stretched and injured, we have said the treatment of vomiting and fumigation of herbs.
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	and if it is not all that we have said, then guard that you do not follow it.
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	but it is necessary that what is in the mouth of the marsh, that you tie it to the breast of the woman, then cleanse it with ointment tetrafarmacon.
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer;	if the pig will return and come back, and will be forced.
mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	but nevertheless, when it returns if it comes with bad smell to the stomach and head, and bleeds the pain.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu:	If therefore, one must do fumigations witchcraft to that:
aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	none of the ancients have experienced fumigation of celery and dried figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The form of the instrument used to smoke the woman at the retention of flowers and the second one is this:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	And it appears like glass, and one places the head subtly in its natural position, and the others wide over the fire;
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	and either the smoke over the coals, and the lice until they are destroyed, and then begin another one.
de percier lou fondement	to pierce the foundation
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Many children are born who do not have the foundation pierced, but it is stopped by some subtle swelling:
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	therefore it is necessary for the midwife to pierce that swelling at its proper place, and not pierce too deeply with the sharp instrument, and remove the position so that it does not touch.
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	then place on the wound a soft cloth in wine and oil, then the treatment of poultice until they are healed.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	And if you doubt that it will not set, place or press a bandage of cloth, and let it remain for some time, and be sure that the child wants to go into the room.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme;	And never comes this stoppage of wound or abscess.
si covient coper celui soudement:	if it is necessary to cover that wound:
si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	if it is treated, as we have said of the dog's flesh.
de la fistule dou fondement	of the deep fistula
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des II parties, si a une fistule ou plusors;	Fistulas that come from the base are nodules, and grow larger than those that come above the base, or in the space between the two parts, if there is one fistula or more.
et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe, et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans;	And when that nodule is old, it works, and grows moist with white or thin blood, and never are those fistulas permanent.
et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	And they are known by the fact that there is outflow or vapor when the wound makes an emission, and perhaps some verses.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge;	And if there are fistulas that protrude from the bladder, and from half of the penis;
et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	and reach up to the joining of the ribs, and out of the mouth.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And thus one knows the fistula by its base, and not by its opening:
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	and you should prick your index finger or base into the fistula when there is no twisting.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou I poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	And if there is twisting, then you should prick it with a thin tent of cloth, or horsehair, until you feel the tent or hair at your finger.
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	and if you do not understand it, and it does not come from perforation, egestion, or wind, as we have said:
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie;	that it does not pierce through;
si te haste dou curer.	if you hasten to cure it.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And when the fistula is persistent near the bladder or near the urethra, if it allows urine to pass, and cannot be healed by medicines.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	If it has pierced through to the joint of the elbow, then the tendon is drawn towards the arm;
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	if there is no twisting and the invention of the pain is not there, then it is that it is dislocated, and there is no medicine or salve that can help;
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	and in these persistent fistulas there is no cure but labor, and the vanity of those who try to treat them.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit, et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos;	In that which is not yet fully formed and is not yet ancient, in hope of healing by fire, as I have experienced, and it is that the hairs lie between your hands on their back;
et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	and the legs are stretched up to their knees, and its knees bent towards its belly;
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	then pour water or mud, if there is twisting, until you clean or the tent comes out.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice, se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet;	If the hairs feel painful at their base, then you must insert your index finger, as if you feel that the tent has pierced it;
et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	and it is discovered or you feel between your teeth the bone or the horn, then spit out that it has passed.
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	if not, do not bother if it cannot be healed.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	It is said that one can heal all things, but this happens rarely.
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	and the aid that is done, if it is to heat the fine cauterization according to the width of the fistula, as it has been said before.
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement;	and the whole mouth is filled in the fistula, until it comes out of the base.
et faice ceu II fois ou III, tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	and do this two or three times, until you know that these bones are broken, which are similar to a quill of an arrow.
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	Then the treatment of burned tent-cloth, until that one is healed, then the treatment of cauterizing with heat and sealing.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	If it is thus sound, it is well.
Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If so, nothing else can be saved;
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	And if it is placed between, and does not pierce just at the spot where it is based, and between your finger and the tent is a thick layer of charcoal or ash, and you see the fistula that results from the covering of care;
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	if the copper at the beginning of the fistula is closed and pushed forward before the tent, and then the cauterizing after, until it reaches the top of the tent;
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra;	and will be delivered from the tent, and fall.
puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	then make sure those charred ones that seem like a goose quill, and none remain denying it.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if you cannot remove it, and cut between you and the work, then cauterize with fire or medicine.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble II bones choses:	For the fire cautery accomplishes two things:
c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	that is to say, the burning of these charred ones, and the stopping of blood and the sealing of moisture.
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	then the treatment of muddied tents with butter or in a mixture broken down, until the lees are poured out, and the charred ones are burned in the pot.
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	then treat the wound of the soaked arrowheads with hard charcoal, and the dry medicines.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	For when it is restored, it is healed and does not return.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	And if the fistula comes from just above the base, and is distant from the body, then press on the top or base, and ask for water.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre II est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des III manieres:	If you feel the tent, and between them is the cloth or the saw or the charcoal where it is near to pierce, if there is no other remedy than hope and faith, by the administration of one of the three methods:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	or you cauterize it as we have said, or you cut it just above, or if you can, put bandages and treat it as first aid.
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	and do not move too much in front, so that you do not cover the part that holds the foundation, and brings the excretions by the way of voluntary movement.
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	then treat it as we have said.
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	If by chance it is fractured, then you will remove that covering and the bandage as soon as it is cut below the foundation, or by tent or by other instrument appointed.
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	Then examine this wound which is in the sore, as you can.
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement:	Then study to restore the wound and to delay the fistula in the part before the foundation.
si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	If it is a lighter thing for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere:	And sometimes fistulas are in this manner:
et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus, si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	And when you place the tent in the fistula, and it is where it costs the foundation below the skin above, then take a tent perforated at the head according to this form.
Et i boute I fil tort en II, et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	And push the thread into the fistula, and push the tent along the entire thread in the fistula until it reaches the top.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	If she is persistent on the edge of the foundation within, then hold the thread of that perforated one, so that you bring your own or foundation.
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les II chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse I jor ou II;	and trace the head of the thread, and gather the two shoulder pieces together, and hold one against the other, and leave it for one or two days.
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	and hold it not once, until the thread covers those charred parts that are between them, and heal.
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	then treat the wound until it is healed and clean.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not perforate, then prick it in all possible ways that you can, but do not make it too thin.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	For it is not good to make the bandage too thin if it is too thin, and then treat it as we have said, until it is healed.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The shape of the spiny bone that is made into a fistula is very sharp and one-sided;
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	And on the other hand, not for the reason that we do not know what we should not do, as you see here:
des emorroydes	des emorroydes
Emorrydes sont selonc II manieres:	There are two ways of doing it:
ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc, et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement;	Or they are inside the foundation, like grains of resin, and there are small and large ones, and some cause bleeding, and there are one or more, and they are under the foundation and at the base of the foundation;
mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor, et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	But those that are underneath have little moisture, and some cause bleeding or a little bit of sharp citrine or a little bit of blood, and they have the color of the body;
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	and for those who have them in the foundation, it is that you command the patient to let the hairs grow long and even, so that they may shine in other chambers, until the foundation is full, and they open the son.
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	if you are in a hurry, and you can do it with pincers, or you hold it at your nail, then cover it in its roots.
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a I drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	and if they cannot hold them with their moistures, then take them with a cloth, or cotton, or a piece of linen.
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	and hold them to your fingers, then cover them, and powder with any hot powders that are in the work of cauterization.
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, pues les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	where you cauterize them as it is said in the chapter of cautery, then treat other ailments until they are healed.
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	and if the base cannot be lifted, apply a sharp and biting cautery to clean what is stuck at the base, so it can be removed openly.
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	if the hairs are tightly attached to the base, and if the base is very deep, then the treatment is light.
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	and you should grasp them with your fingers or pliers, cut them off, then treat them as we have said, until they are healed, and do not fear the incision by iron.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere:	If it is necessary to suture according to this method:
pren I fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les II chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille, et si soit dou large;	Take a thick thread, and make it into a needle, then pull the thread through the top and make the needle pierce from the other side, and turn the two ends of the thread away from the needle, and if it is too wide;
et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse I por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	and hold the thread firmly, then cut the thread, and pull out the needle, and do the same with all the others, and leave one to let the excess blood out;
puis met sus le fondement I drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	then put above the wound a soft cloth dipped in red oil or cerate, and put above the wound, and instruct the patient to rest;
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then let it remain until they have healed, and when they are healed, apply ointment and other treatments until they are healed.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	dryly and without delay at the base
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	often occurs in the intestines and due to constriction of nature, and when the disease is old and medicine does not help.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	It is necessary that you reset it at the tip of a small knife or at your fingernail, which does not allow it to become moist.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	then treat it until it is as it should be.
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	and if it cannot heal, then repeat the scraping more forcefully than before until it is fully healed and scarred.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat it until it is healed.
dou fremit	dry heat
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	Mice are a small appearance that grows on the body and spreads quickly.
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	and never the cold, and they feel it as if they were dying of cold, and it comes to the whole body, and more in the hands than in other parts.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	And the cure is that you take a quill from a goose feather, or a pen of vulture very strong, and place that quill on the cold, until the circle of the quill completely encompasses the cold.
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	Then turn your hand all around the quill until you cover all around the cold, and put it in warm water, and extract the cold from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you see, then make a suture of a needle of rain or iron in this form, and be subtle to remove and raise it up:
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser.	Do not let go, to hold at the two ends, and to press.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	And if you see that the heat of the cautery is too much, as it is before or in the chapter of cautery.
de la forme dou clistere	of the shape of this ointment
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet;	Never do you make a plaster with silver, lead, or tin, whether melted or in powder form.
et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	And never do you make these small and large instruments, according to those that you will bring.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Therefore, those that you should arm yourself with in the care of children and those who are weak and in pain, are small.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The shape of this ointment is above wide, or the belly is bound according to this way:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez;	And if there is a discharge or the belly is tied, as you see, and the wound is inside, then pierce.
et ait a l’un des costez II pertus, et en l’autre I;	And if there are two perforations on one side and one on the other.
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus, et ait entre chescun pertus I doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus I fil fort de fil crut tort en X ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	And if the belly is filled with medicine from a beast's bladder or parchment, and you pierce all around with small perforations, and there is one inch of space between each perforation, then insert a strong thread through each perforation, twist it around ten times, and tie the belly as if it were a goat.
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize;	And when the medicine is inside, if the leg has an instrument in front of a strong thread, then cleanse.
et c’est li forme dou cercle:	And it is in the form of a circle.
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	And let the medicine not be too hot or too cold, and anoint the head of the cleanser with oil or a similar substance, then gently press it in.
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses II mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit, et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet;	Then the minister holds the patient's hands together until it is all visible, then remove the cleanser, and relieve the pain in their legs by holding them parallel, and if the medicine wants to come out, let it come out as much as possible.
et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	And if he sleeps a whole night, it is a greater help.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you apply the poultice in the case of diarrhea, and the patient wants to come out, let him come out as much as possible; and if he is healthy again, continue.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por I enfant;	And if the wound is on the base or an abscess, then the poultice should be as gentle as for a child.
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	And this is the form of the gentle poultice over which the skin is stretched:
des plaies	with wounds:
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies;	We have said in the division the treatment of wounds.
or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	Or we will tell you the remedies for hands and medicine, according to completion.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I say that wounds are different according to how they are made, and according to the limbs or wounds that are made, and from what they are made.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	The things by which wounds are made are from piercing with a stone, and cutting with a sword or dagger, or lance or staff or arrow, or similar things.
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	when they are done according to the laws of the body, such as wounds that bleed above the neck, or above the head, or the foot, or the belly, or the liver, and similar members;
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	and I will tell you the treatment for each wound, and I will begin with simple head wounds, because the remembrance will come in its chapter.
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans, et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut:	I say that when a simple wound comes to the head, and the bone is not broken, then be careful if it is from piercing or similar things, and the skin is completely torn and is large, and you slightly doubt an abscess forming:
si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s’il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree;	if the patient is immediately healthy from the cerebral itself if he comes little of blood from the wound, and let the healing be on the opposite side of the wounded part.
et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.	and avoid the hairs from being replenished with wine and large meats.
Et s’il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char;	And if he does not want to heal, let his food be made mild, and he should not drink wine, nor change his char.
et met sor la plaie, se apostemes chaus i vient, coton moilliet en oile roset soulement, ou en vin stiptice;	and put on the wound, if abscesses come, cotton moistened in rose oil only, or in vinegar stiptic.
et s’il n’i a aposteme chaut, si met sus la plaie, s’elle est fresche a tout son sanc, et elle n’est muee par l’air, poudre, que je dirai un poc ci aprés;	and if there is no abscess, put on the wound, if it is fresh and full of blood, and it is not moved by air, powder that I will say a little later.
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucuns oignemens, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the arm has been moved, put some splints on it until it is healed.
Et se li plaie est grans si com de tailleure d’espee et de semblans, et les levres ne se pueent assembler par tentes, si les assemble par cousture, si com je dirai as plaies dou ventre, de la costure.	And if the wound is large like a sword cut and similar, and the lips cannot be closed by tents, then sew them together as I will say in wounds of the belly, from the stitching.
Se li plaie est descoverte de l’os, et pent, et ne tient mais que a un poc, si le cope;	If the wound is exposed to bone, and can be moved, but only holds at one point, then suture it.
puis cure la plaie de medicine, et restoure char dure en leu de cuir, et comande au malaide a mengier grosses viandes, si com testes et froment cuit, ausi com poulz, et semblans choses.	Then treat the wound with medicine, and replace hard charcoal in place of skin, and instruct the patient to eat less fatty foods, such as meat and cooked grains, like chicken, and similar things.
Et se tu trueves ou cuir porriture, et il n’aert a l’os, si cope lou porrit tot, et giete fuer, puis le cure;	And if you find decayed skin or rotten flesh that does not touch the bone, then cut it all away, and pour vinegar on it, then treat it.
et se il ait artere en la plaie ou voine, dont sans cort, et il ne puet estainchier par medicines, si quier l’artere, et se tu la trueves desloie, si la lie d’un fil;	If he has an artery in the wound or vein, without cutting it, and he cannot stop the bleeding with medicines, then tie the artery, and if you remove the tube, then bind it with a thread.
et se ceu ne profite mie, si la cauterize.	And if it does not help, then cauterize it.
Et se ces plaies sont petites et simples, si est li cure legiere:	And if these wounds are small and simple, then the treatment is light:
et est que tu mettes ens ceste poudre qui soude ainsois que li ars l’ait muee.	and you put in this powder that sours as soon as the wound has moved.
Et li maniere de la poudre si est:	And the way of the powder is:
pren encens une partie;	take incense a part;
sanc de dragon II parties;	blood of dragon two parts;
chalz vive III parties, et le poudre subtilment, et emple la plaie, et l’estraint forment, tant qu’elle s’aerse bien et se joigne a tout son sanc;	Live charcoal in three parts, and the powder finely, and fill the wound, and let it form a scab, until it heals well and joins to all its sinew.
et puis la lie bien, et la laisse sens desliier, s’elle n’enfle;	And then tie it firmly, and leave it undisturbed unless it swells;
car on n’oste la madicine tant qu’ele soit sanee.	for the medicine should not be removed until it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on ceu de chalz soulement, quant on n’ait l’encens ne lou sanc de dragon, mais que li ars n’ait muee la plaie.	And never use only chalk, when one does not have incense or dragon's blood, but that the art has moved the wound.
Et se li ars ait mueit la plaie, meismement en esteit, si n’i met om mie ceste poudre;	And if the wound moves again immediately, then do not put any of this powder;
mais met sus aucuns oignemens digestis, ou poulz de farine d’orge faites d’aigue et de miel, tant qu’ele giete bowe;	but put some digestible ointments or poultices made of barley flour and honey, until it weeps.
puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat other ailments until they are healed.
Et se li brisure d’os vient avec la plaie, et elle est petite, si l’estrai as pinceures subtilz;	And if the fractured bone comes with the wound, and it is small, then use fine forceps to extract it;
et je vos dirai ci aprés les brisures dou chief.	and I will tell you about the main fractures afterwards.
de la plaie dou col	of the wound of the neck
Se plaie vient ou col et elle est simple, si n’a point de difference entre li et celi dou chief, mais se li ners dou col ou li artere est copee.	If the wound comes from the neck and it is simple, there is no difference between this and the previous one, but if the wound of the neck or the artery is cut.
Se c’est li ners, si n’i a autre engien que laissier la cure, et n’i mettre nulle chose restraignant, car il nuit as ners et les fait retraire;	If it is a nerve, there is no other method than to let the wound heal, and not put anything restricting, because it harms nerves and causes them to retract;
et ne mettre sus la plaie rien froit, car li substance des ners est froide, et li continuation d’aus si est avec le cerveil, qui est li plus haus membres;	and do not put anything flat on the wound, because the substance of nerves is cold, and its continuity is with the brain, which is one of the highest members;
mais soit li medicine souez, si com chalz lavee en aigue douce, et mellee avec oile roset, et cucie lavee ausi en aigue douce, et autres pieres de mine selonc ceste maniere, et oignemens moistes.	but if the medicine is wet, like chalk washed in sharp sweet water, and mixed with rose oil, and the cloth washed similarly in sharp sweet water, and other stones in this manner, and moistened with warm water.
Et se li plaie est grans, si la cout et lie de bendes, puis la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the wound is large, then use bandages to bind it, and treat it until it heals.
Et se les plaies sont parfondes et ele est chevee et pleinne de bowe, si la perce ou plus bas leu;	And if the wounds are deep and she is hairy and full of flesh, then prick or lower the limb.
et se li artere est copee, et decorremens de sanc en vient, si la desoivre, et la loie, et la cauterize se mestier est;	and if the artery is cut and there comes out blood, then drain, wash, and cauterize as necessary.
et se li espinee de la gorge est copee, ou li keurs, et li conduiz est gardez, par coi la viande va, si cout le keur sus la cainne de la gorge, et ne touchier la gorge mais la remet selonc sa figure naturel;	and if the arrow is cut from the throat or the wound, and the conduct is kept, by which the meat goes, then cut the arrow above the back of the throat, and do not touch the throat but put it back according to its natural shape.
et puis l’estraint avenanment, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le cure d’oignemens desechans tant qu’il soit sanez;	and then gradually release it, and let it rest for some time, then treat the wounds until they are healed;
et se li plaie a fait empression en l’os, si la quier;	if the wound has made an impression on the bone, if necessary;
et s’il i a pieces d’os, si les trai fuers toz se tu pues, et ces que tu ne pues avoir, si laisse tant que li plaie porrisse, et soit desevree et aligie li issue;	and if there are pieces of bone, try to remove them all if possible, and those you cannot remove, leave until the wound heals, and then disinfect and align the fracture;
et se li plaie est fresche, si poudre sus la poudre que j’ai dit.	and if the wound is fresh, apply the powder that I have mentioned.
Et s’il a en la plaie os et il i a fistule, si la cure ensi com j’ai dit en son chapistre.	And if he has bone in the wound and there is a fistula, then the treatment as I have described in his chapter.
de la plaie de lance ou de coutel	of the wound of spear or of dagger
Se c’est cop de lance ou de coutel, et li plaie est parfonde, si regarde se de la plaie saut ventositez cant li malaides alainne:	If it is a spear or dagger wound, and the wound is deep, look to see if there is any whiteness or foul smell coming from the wound:
saiches adonques que li plaie est mortelz;	Then immediately apply bandages to stop the bleeding, as if the wound is mortal.
et s’elle n’est parfonde, et elle est fresche a tout son sanc, si n’i mettre mie a la premiere houre la poudre, ne ne la liier mie por le sanc que ne demorse em parfont, et reviegne au cuer, et ocie lou malaide;	And if it is not deep and fresh with blood throughout the wound, do not apply powder or bandage immediately for the first hour, so that it does not stick to the wound and prevent healing from occurring.
mais i met oignement atractif, et le lie II fois le jor;	But apply an attractive ointment, and bind it twice a day.
et se tu n’as oignement, si met en la plaie viel coton por succier fuers la moistor, et fai dormir le malaide sus la plaie III jors, ou IIII, ou plusors;	And if you do not have an ointment, put old cotton in the wound to absorb excess moisture, and keep it quiet for three days, or four, or more.
si n’i venra mie spasme, ne tremor male de cuer n’estraingnemens d’alainne;	If no spasm occurs, nor does trembling of the heart prevent it from being strained.
et quant tu vois les bones dispositions, si saiches que li plaie est sauve.	And when you see good positions, if you cut that the wound is saved.
Cure la donques de tentes et d’autres cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Treat the wounds and other treatments, until they are healed.
et s’elle ne puet saner, et oevre, adés saiches que il i a fistule;	And if it cannot heal, and work, then cut that there is a fistula;
si la cure si com on doit.	if the treatment as one should.
Et se li plaie est d’incision d’espee ou de coutel, et elle est simple, ou pis ou au dos, si la cure de ceu qui est devant;	And if the wound is of incision by sword or knife, and it is simple, or worse or at the back, then treat what is in front.
s’elle est grans, de cousture;	If it is large, of sewing;
et s’elle est petite, de poudre, et s’elle est empressee en l’os, et en a copeit pieces, si quier la plaie, et les trai fuers s’il sont desevrez;	And if it is small, of powder, and if it is pressed into the bone, and if it has chipped off pieces, if the wound requires them, and the remaining shards, if they are suitable.
et s’il ne sont desevrez, si laisse porrir la plaie, si aligera li estractions;	And if they are not suitable, leave the wound to fester, so that it aligns with the extraction.
et des autres plaies as autres membres est li jugemens si com nos avons dit.	And for other wounds on other limbs, it is up to judgment as we have said.
dou derrompement dou ventre	abdominal hernia
Li derompemens dou ventre est grans et moiens et petis;	The ruptures of the belly are large and medium and small;
de la grant plaie saut aucune fois li intestine, ou li ners des intestines, par coi li intromission d’aus;	Of the great wound, none of the intestines ever jumps out, or the nerves of the intestines, because of their insertion into them.
et li costure est plus malaisie, et aucune fois vaut pis li petite plaie que li grans, por ceu c’on remet plus a poinnes les intestines en, s’on ne les i remet de chaut en chaut;	And the sutures are more painful, and it is never worse than a small wound because if one does not put the intestines back in properly, they will not heal properly.
por ce que li intestine enflent tantost qu’il sentent le froit, si rentrent plus a poinnes, et por ceu vaut mues li moieinne plaie, por ceu c’on ramoine mues l’intestine a son leu que as autres II.	Because the intestines swell quickly when they feel the heat, and they are put back in properly, and it is better to have a minor wound because one can easily rotate the intestines back into place as with other limbs.
Et saiches que li routure dou ventre est selonc IIII manieres:	And there are four ways to treat a wound in the abdomen:
les II costures communes avienent en la costure dou ventre, et li costure des autres plaies dou cors et II autres costures propres sont communes as autres plaies;	The two common sutures are in the abdominal wound suture, and the suture of other body wounds and two other proprietary sutures are common to other wounds.
et toutevoie elles sont plus propres avec la costure dou ventre, et je dirai une chescune et declairerai.	And all ways they are cleaner with the stitching of the belly, and I will say one by one and explain.
Je di que quant li plaie est petite, et aucune chose de l’intestine ist fuer, et griés chose est dou remettre, ceu est par l’une des II manieres:	I say that when the wound is small, and nothing of the intestine is protruding, and it is a good thing to put back, this is by one of the two methods:
ou por la petitece de la plaie, si com nos avons dit, ou por ce que li intestine est enflez por le froit.	or because of the smallness of the wound, as we have said, or because the intestine is swollen by the heat.
Et quant il est frois, eschaufez lou en teil maniere:	And when it is hot, warm it in this way:
moillie une esponge ou I mol drapeil en aigue tede soulement, ou tu cuis en aigue squinant et cipre et spique, et arose l’intestine tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	soak a sponge or a piece of clean cloth in cold water only, or boil in cold water with vinegar and pepper and salt, and steam the intestine until it is swollen is softened;
et aucune fois fait ce vins restraingnans, et est muedre que awe soule por desenfler.	and never made this wine with restraining, and it is muddled that one soul for dissolution.
Et quant tu vois l’enfleure departir, si amoiste l’intestine d’aigue ou altee et malves soient cuites, car par ceu est aligie li entree a poc de chose;	And when you see the inflammation disappear, if the intestines are moist or alkaline and misaligned, for this is aligned with the entrance of the disease.
et s’il n’i puet entrer, si fent un poc la plaie a l’estrument de coi on cope les emorroydes;	and if it cannot enter, then make a little hole in the wound with the tool used to remove tumors.
et li premiere cure est muedre que li taille, que nus n’i doit taillier sens grant necessiteit n’i ait;	and the first care is to muddle that the cut, that we should not cut without great necessity.
et c’est li estrumens por le fendre:	and this is the tool for the cutting:
si trenche dedens en la corbeure et defuer non, et vez ci la forme:	if you cut into the wound and do not find it, and see its shape:
Et quant li plaie est enlargie, et li intestine saut fuer, si le remet arer selonc la forme naturel en son leu propre, se tu en as pooir, car ce vaut mues.	And when the wound is enlarged, and the intestines jump out, put them back in their natural form according to their own place, if you can, for this is good.
Quant li plaie est large, et elle est en la partie desoz lou ventre, si covient que tu faices gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et met ses jambes plus haut que son chief;	When the wound is wide and in the lower abdomen, then it is necessary to place the injured limb on its back, and raise its legs higher than its head;
et s’elle est en la partie desoz le ventre, si met le chief et le pis plus haut que les parties desoz, et ausi se li routure dou ventre est en l’une des II parties si met t’entente en ceu que li partie navree soit plus haute que li autre;	and if it is in the lower abdomen, then place the head and the foot higher than the other parts, and also if the wound breaks through the belly, place the injured side higher than the other;
et ensi covient amenistrer ceu que je dis en plaies grans et moienes.	and thus it is necessary to follow what I say in large and moderate wounds.
Es plaies petites met ceu que t’est apparilliet, puis aies entre tes mains I ministre pitous ki teigne toute la routure a sa main, et assemble les levres;	For small wounds, apply what is at hand that has been previously prepared, then put between your hands the healing ointment that covers the entire wound and brings together the lips.
