et pren warde en la restauration et en la disposition d’aposteme chaut, et secor ceu qui i vient, si com j’ai dit.	and take care in the restoration and disposition of abscesses, and treat what comes to it, as I have said.
de la cuixe brisie	of the broken rib
Li os de la cuixe est maintes fois brisiez, et bien le voit on quant elle torne devant et derrier;	The teeth of the jaw are often broken, and well seen when it turns in front and behind.
et li restauration si est c’on lie I liien desus la briseure, et I autre desoz.	and the restoration is when one side of the bone above the fracture is connected to the other side below the fracture.
Et li malaides gise sus sa faice, puis estende chescuns ministres son lien a sa part igalment;	And the broken bones are then arranged on their face, and each of the attendants stretches out their ligament to their equal part.
et c’est quant li brisure est emmi l’os.	and it is when the fracture is put back into the bone.
Et se li brisure est prochiene a la racine de la cuixe, si soit li uns des liiens devers lou poignil, et li autres liiens desoz la briseure.	And if the fracture is close to the root of the chest, then one of the lines should be towards the base of the rib, and the other lines away from the fractured rib.
Et ausi s’elle est prochiene au genoil, et adonques soit li liens delez lou genoil, et soit li extension aval;	And also if it is close to the knee, and then the ligaments above the knee are stretched out, and the extension below.
puis mette li mires l’os igal a ses II mains, tant qu’il soit selonc sa figure natureil, et puis met l’emplaustre, et lou lie, se apostemes chaz n’i vient.	then put the splint on the bone with both hands, as it is according to its natural shape, and then apply the plaster, and the bandage, if there are no abscesses.
Et s’il i a aposteme chaut, si le laisse apaisier puis revien a ton ovraige et a ta cure;	If there is an abscess, let it calm down first, then return to your work and care.
li lieure est faite en teil maniere.	The litter is made in this manner.
Il covient que tu envoloupes sus la briseure I bendeil dur doublé en II ou III, et en demoure li superfluitez, puis torne la jambe tant que li talons veigne a la racine de la naige, et boute I fil lonc entre la cuixe et la jambe, delez lou genoil desoz, et veignent li chief dou fil au desus;	It is necessary that you wrap the fractured bone with a bandage doubled in two or three layers, and let the excess hang down, then bend the leg until the toes reach the root of the heel, and tie a long thread between the thigh and the leg, below the knee joint, and bring the end of the thread upwards.
puis torne sus la jambe et sus la cuixe le bendeil, puis met sus la briseure esteles, et met une estele sus l’os de la jambe;	Then bend over the leg and the thigh, then place the splint on the fractured bone, and place a splint on the bone of the leg.
puis emple le leu vuit entre la jambe et la cuixe de drapelz souef por mettre igal l’estrignement, puis comence a liier forment III tors ou IIII sus la briseure;	then place the cloth that is soft between the leg and the thigh to equalize the pressure, then begin to bandage firmly three or four times above the fracture.
et quant plus vas en sus de la briseure, et moins l’estraint;	and as you go higher than the fracture, and less the pressure.
puis enten as II chiés dou fil que tu as bouteit entre la jambe et la cuixe, et en lie III esteles que sont desus, puis revai au desoz au chief dou fil, tant que tu veignes delez le piet;	then take two threads that you have tied between the leg and the thigh, and bind three stitches that are above, then return to the outside at the top of the thread, until you come beyond the bone.
et l’estraint, si qu’il ne se mueve de son leu, puis le laisse ensi, puis k’il n’i vient ne aposteme ne enfleure n’autre semblant.	and the pressure, so that it does not move from its place, then leave it thus, then if there is no abscess or swelling of any other kind.
Et s’il i avient, si le deslie, et adresce ceu que i vient, si com nos avons dit maintes fois;	And if there is, then release it, and direct it to where it comes, as we have said many times.
et se il i a pieces de l’os que poigne, si le covient ewer, s’om puet;	and if there are pieces of bone that can be felt, then remove them if possible.
et s’on ne puet, si covient fendre le leu, et traire fuer;	and if they cannot be removed, then cut the limb and draw out the splinters.
et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant k’il soit sanez.	and treat it as we have said, until it is healed.
Et aucune fois est brisie li cuixe ensi c’on i met esteles, si com en l’ajutoire et ou bras;	And never break the rib in such a way that these are inserted, as in the dislocation and shoulder.
toutevoie, en la restauration ensi faite ne cloche mie li malaides.	However, in this restoration, do not strike the hairs.
Et saiches que li cuixe est restoree en L jors, ou poc moins ou poc plus, selonc les diversitez des complexions.	And wash the ribs when they are restored at the appropriate times, either a little sooner or a little later, according to the diversities of the conditions.
de la ruelle dou genoil	of the road of the gentleman
Saiches que en la ruelle dou genoil avient poc brisure, mais elle ploie maintes fois.	It is said that in the road of the gentleman, there is little breakage, but it rains many times.
Et s’elle brise, si n’est mais c’une fendure, ou I pertus, et avient a tout plaie, et sens plaie, et ce sent om bien.	And if it breaks, it is not but a cut, or a puncture, and it has to all wounds, and without wound, and it feels very well.
Et li restauration si est c’on mette igal ceu qui est rons a ses dois, tant qu’il soit assemblez mues c’on puet;	And the restoration is done by putting back together what is broken until it can be put back together as much as possible.
puis met l’emplaustre, et i met une estele reonde, se tu en as mestier, et l’estraint si com il covient, puis rewarde toutes les dispositions que nos avons dit ens autres briseures, si com aposteme chaut et autre semblant;	Then apply the ointment, and if you have skill, place a round bandage, and bind it as it should be, then warm up all the positions that we have mentioned in other broken things, such as abscesses and similar.
si met a chescun accident ceu k’il li covient, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And apply what is necessary for each accident until it is healed.
de la brisure de la jambe	of the broken leg
Saiches que en la jambe ait II os, de coi li uns est apelez par droit non «mustelz», et li autres est apelez «foscile»;	It is said that in the leg there are two bones, one of which is called "canons" and the other "fibula".
et avient tout auteil briseure com il vient au bras, et por ceu est li restauracion si com celle dou bras igalment, et li ovraiges est tout i. Et se li dui os sont brisiet ensamble, si torne li jambe de toutes pars.	And it breaks everything as it comes to the arm, and for this reason, the restoration is the same as that of the arm equally, and the work is all there. And if both bones are broken together, then the leg returns from all parts.
Et se li os subtilz est brisiez, si torne devant.	And if the delicate bones are broken, it returns in front.
Et se li gros os est brisiez, si sent on grant dolor, et le voit on bien;	And if the large bone is broken, then it feels great pain, and one can see it well;
et torne desoz.	and it returns dislocated.
Adonques amenistre extension, et le met igal, et lie les esteles igalement;	Then apply extension, and make it equal, and tie the splints equally;
mais toutevoie, il covient se li brisure est laide, et il i a plusors pieces, que li extension soit menor et plus legiere;	but in any case, if the fracture is ugly, and there are many pieces, then the extension should be less and lighter;
et l’alige selonc ta vertu.	and the physician according to his skill.
Et quant tu as tout acomplit ton ovraige, si pren II faixes de fust chevees que porpreignent la jambe d’une part et d’autre, et soient dou lonc de la jambe des le genoil jusque desoz;	And when you have completed your work, take two strips of cloth that bind the leg on one side and the other, and be long from the knee to the groin.
puis envoloupe en II leus I bendeil desus et desoz, et le lie em mileu ausi, et a ceste lieure ne pora li jambe decliner a destre ne a senestre, et ensi est bien;	Then wrap the two strips of cloth above and below, and tie it in the middle as well, and at this point it should not be able to bend the leg to the right or left, and thus it is good.
et aucun i aministrent I bers dou lonc de la jambe, et s’est de fust, et i met on la jambe por warder de movement, et proprement fait on ceu en la brisure ou il a plaie;	And no one administers the long cloth of the leg, and it is from the cloth, and put the leg to prevent movement, and properly made, one puts it in the break or where it is wounded.
et remue chescun jor la jambe, por veoir s’il i a aposteme chaut n’autre accident;	and shake each leg, to see if there is an abscess or other accident.
si le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	if the patient is healthy until healed.
de la brisure des os dou piet	of the fracture of bones due to a fall
A la cheville ne vient point de brisure, mais as os dou piet vient aucune fois brisure et as dois poc, et n’i avient fuer que quassure em plusor dispositions.	At the ankle, there is no fracture, but bones due to a fall never break and are only slightly displaced, and there is no injury in most cases.
Et s’il avient as os dou piet brisure, et tu vois ces os sormonter l’un l’autre, si mette si malaides som piet sus la terre, ausi com s’il voloit aler, et puis met maintenant ton piet sus lou sien, lai ou li os sont levez, puis le presse tant k’il reveignent en lor leus;	And if he has broken bones that are slightly protruding, and you see these bones overlapping each other, if you put pressure on the bone above the ground, as if it wanted to walk, and then put your foot on the place where the bones are raised, then press until they return to their original position;
puis met l’emplaustre et estoupes sus, et met desoz lou ventre dou piet une petite tauble a II chiés plains, puis l’estraint au piet avenanment, puis que tu as envoloupez drapelz entor, et autres choses dont tu as mestier.	then apply the plaster and soak it above, and put a small cushion under the belly of the bone, then tie it to the bone evenly, then wrap it with cloths and other things you have at hand.
Et quant III jors ou IIII seront passez, si deslie lou liien, car tu troveras les os igalz, soient brisiez, soient desaluez.	And when three or four days have passed, if the joint is released, you will find the bones even, whether they are broken or dislocated.
Et s’il i a aucuns des dois brisiez, si les restoure, si com nos avons dit as dois de la main;	And if there are any of the two broken, restore them as we have said about the two bones of the hand.
puis met au doi brisiet une estele selonc la longesce dou doi, et soit un poc plus large, puis met desoz le piet celle tauble que j’ai dit, et l’estrain avenanment;	Then place the broken bone along its length, and it should be slightly wider, then put the petal of the herb I mentioned on top, and apply pressure evenly.
et s’il en i a II ou III, ou plus, brisiez, si met sus chescun doi une estele selonc sa quantiteit, envoloupee en I drapeil de lin, et estraint la tauble desoz lou piet;	And if there are two or three or more broken bones, place a splint on each according to its quantity, wrapped in a piece of linen, and apply pressure from outside the petal.
et soit estans sus lou chief de la tauble defuer lou ventre dou piet, si qu’il le teigne bien.	And it should be placed on top of the back of the petal under the belly of the wound, so that it stains well.
Et covient que tu n’oblier mie les autres choses que j’ai dit as autres briseures, des que nos avons dit;	And it is necessary that you do not forget the other things that I have said about other fractures, as we have mentioned.
et secor chescun accident si com il covient.	and treat each event as it should be.
de la brisure de l’os dou poignil	of the breaking of the bone in the thumb
Quant li os de la nature la femme est brisiez, si la fai seoir enlargie, puis l’encline a la partie dou dos, et soit tenue par derrier;	When the jaw of a woman is broken, if it has been displaced, then enlarge it, then tilt it towards the back of the neck, and hold it in place from behind.
puis emplisse li baile la nature de la malaide de couton, et en i mette ausi gros com I sto;	then fill the hollow of the jaw with cotton, and put in as much as it is full.
puis deboute la femme, et lieve lou dos poc et poc, et adonques saut li coton, tant qu’il vient a l’entree de la nature, et revient li os avec lou sto;	then raise the woman, and gradually lift her back, and then slowly remove the cotton until it reaches the entrance of the jaw, and then return the bone with the cotton.
et quant elle vuet pissier, si oste lou coton, et quant elle a pissiet, se li remette, et ensi faice VII jors ou entor:	And when she wants to urinate, remove the cotton, and when she has finished, return it, and thus do this every seven hours or so.
si sera restoree li brisure, et se tu vues, pren une vessie de berbis, et lie au pertus une cainne, et boute toute la vessie en la nature;	If she is restored, and if you see, take a birch-bark vessel, and tie a rope around it, and fill the whole vessel with urine in its natural state.
puis soffle en la cainne forment, tant que li vessie soit enflee dedens:	Then blow through the rope until the vessel is emptied inside.
la nature si revenra li brisure;	The natural state will return to the broken place.
puis soit emplie de coton, et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then it should be filled with cotton and left in this way for some time until it is healed.
Et quant li os dou poignil de l’ome est brisiez, ou de la femme, si le restoure ensi com nos avons dit en l’os de la hainche;	And when the tooth of the little finger of the hand is broken, or of a woman, if it is reset as we have said in the bone of the shoulder;
et ne sont mie occultees ces briseures prochienes a celui qui i met son estude et son us, et entent mon livre.	and these broken bones are not hidden from him who puts his study and use to this book, and listen to my book.
Car li brisure li signifie em plusors dispositions la droite voie de la restauration:	For the break means in many positions the right way of restoration:
enten le donques.	Therefore, listen then.
En la verge, quant elle est brisie, pren une gorge d’oie et i boute la verge;	In the tooth, when it is broken, take a goose beak and push the tooth;
puis envoloupe drapelz entor, et le laisse III jors ou enqui entor, et il sera sanez hastanment.	then wrap it with cloths around, and leave it three days or more, and it will heal quickly.
de brisure avec plaie	of break with wound
Il covient a celui qui a brisure avec plaie, meismement s’elle est grans, si com li os de la cuixe ou de l’ajutoire ou semblant, qu’il soit sainiez maintenant, si que les sainies que nos avons dit le tesmoignent.	It is necessary for the one who has broken with a wound, even if it is large, such as the bones of the ribs or shoulder or similar, that they be cleansed immediately, so that the cleansings that we have said bear witness.
Et se li plaie saine, si la restainche de vitriole, se tu n’as autre chose, puis rencomence a restorer la briseure en cele meisme houre, ou celui jor, se apostemes chaus n’i vient.	And if the wound is clean, if the remaining vitriol, if you have nothing else, then begin to restore the breaker in the same hour, or the next day, if pus does not come.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si laisse la restauration jusc’a nuevime jor, tant que li apostemes soit apaisiez, et n’i touchier ne au tier jor ne au quart, car tu i feroies venir malvais accident.	And if pus comes, leave the restoration until the next day, as long as the pus is calm, and do not touch it on the next day or the fourth, for you will bring about bad accidents.
Et se li os brisiez est aparans sus lou keur descovert, si covient que tu lou mettes a point legierement a tes mains, a extension petite.	And if the broken teeth appear above the gum line, then it is necessary to carefully place them gently in your hands and extend them slightly.
Et se li extensions ne t’est apareillie por mettre igal a tes mains, si le ramoine a cest estrument qui est de fer, qui a VII dois ou VIII de lonc, et li largesce est selonc la quantiteit de la plaie;	And if the extensions are not provided to make your hands even, then bend the arm with this iron instrument which is made of iron, which has seven or eight inches of length, and its width according to the size of the wound;
et por ceu est mestier au mire qu’il empreigne III ou IIII, selonc ceu qu’il en ait mestier en chescune cure de briseure;	and because it is necessary for the mirror to take three or four, according to how much it has in each case of fracture treatment;
et soit rons et un poc gros, k’il ne ploie mie a la compression sus lou membre a ton ovraige, et soit agus devant, et gros des le mileu en avant, ensi:	and it should be round and a little thick, so that it does not slip when compressing on the limb at your work, and it should be narrow behind, and wide in the middle in front, thus:
Et est apelez «palainche», por coi il covient que li chiés corbes soit mis sus lou chief de l’os apparent;	And it is called "palainche", because it should be placed on the top of the head of the apparent bone;
et le boute a une fois, tant k’il reviegne, et soit igalz l’un encontre l’autre.	and it is struck once, as much as it returns, and they should be evenly placed against each other.
Et se li brisure est subtilz, et li estrumens ne puet bien prendre l’os, si covient que tu copes lou chief de l’os, tant que li estrumens en ait possance.	And if the fracture is slight, and the instruments cannot well grasp the bone, then you must cut the head of the bone until the instruments have hold.
Et se tu ne pues ramener l’os, si com nos avons dit, si lou cope d’un estrument covenable a ceu, ou incisoire ou soieure, a ton pooir;	And if you cannot reset the bone as we have said, with the help of an appropriate instrument, such as a saw or a chisel, to your power;
puis reis ceu qui est demorez en l’os d’aspreteit et de menues escorces.	then file off what is remaining in the bone of hardness and small scratches.
Et quant li os est ramenez, et li malaides sent grant dolor aprés, saiches qu’il n’est mie en son leu natureil.	When the bone is returned, and the pain is great afterward, do not let it remain in its natural position.
Si fai tant qu’il soit en son leu, puis moille I drapeil en vin stiptique noir, et proprement se c’est en esteit;	If you do this until it is in its place, then wipe the wound with black vinegar wine, and if it is still in place;
et ne mettre mie sus la plaie cerote ne autre chose ou il ait oile, qu’il n’i faice venir porriture et corruption;	and do not place anything on the wound or apply any other thing where there is oil, so that it does not cause putrefaction and corruption.
puis aministre esteles quant tu as restoreit l’os, et laisse la plaie descoverte, et cope la coverture tout entor, selonc la quantiteit de la plaie, et te done bien en garde que li plaie ne soit estrainte avec la brisure;	then administer ointments when you have restored the bone, and leave the wound open, and cover the dressing all around, according to the size of the wound, and be careful that the wound is not squeezed with the fracture.
et maintes fois ont ce fait li fol mire, et ont fait venir sus le malaide ou mort ou corrodent aucune fois;	many times have done this foolish thing, and have caused the pain or death or corrosion of any part.
et soit li estrignemens plus molz et plus souef des autres brisures.	and let the fractures be softer and more pliable than the others.
Et se li plaie est male ou grans, et tu doutes que mavais accidens n’i veigne, si com nos avons dit, et tu trueves dolor au leu, si n’i covient mie mettre sus esteles;	If the wound is bad or large, and you doubt that no harmful event has occurred, as we have said, and if you alleviate pain to the limb, then it does not matter to put on these bandages.
mais envoloupe entor, en leu d’esteles, drapelz durs, et les lie.	But wrap it around, instead of these bandages, hard cloths, and tie them.
Et quant tu vois aprés I jor ou II enjanrer bowe a la plaie, si oste ceu que tu as mis sus a tout vin, et i met oignement sanant plaies, si com oignement tetrafarmaçon et semblans.	And when you see after one or two days that the wound is discharging pus, remove what you have placed on top of the wound, and put healing ointment on it, such as Tetraflamron and similar ointments.
Et covient que tu deslies lou membre II fois le jor, lou matin et au vespre, tant qu’il soit soudez et sanez.	And it is necessary to move the limb twice a day, in the morning and in the evening, as long as it is sound and healthy.
Et covient que li membres soit aparilliez en teil maniere que li bowe corre aval legierement.	And it is necessary that the member be aligned in such a way that the bow can move freely.
Et se maint jor trespassent, et il ne puet souder mais rent adés bowe, saiches k’il i a petites pieces d’os, por coi il covient que tu quieres la plaie avec tente, et oste toutes ces pieces desevrees que font venir celle dolor.	And if they continue to move too much, and it cannot be set back in place, but rather moves like a bow, because of small pieces of bone, then you must first clean the wound with a tent, and remove all those unwanted pieces that cause this pain.
Et se fistule vient au leu, ou autre maniere de corruption, si covient que tu le cures, selonc ceu qu’il dist en son chapistre ci devant.	And if a fistula comes to the limb, or some other form of corruption, then you must treat it according to what is written in his chapter before.
Et quant li os est brisiez, et apert sus lou membre, si com li os de la cuixe ou de l’ajutoire, et autres semblans des grans membres, si ne le traire mie, car maintes fois en vient li mors, mais le laisse tant qu’il porrisse;	And when the bone is broken, and open above the limb, as the bones of the jaw or shoulder, and other similar large limbs, do not pull it out, for many times it causes death, but leave it until it heals.
par aventure cherra par lui aprés XX jors ou XXX, puis cure la plaie, se tu pues;	Perhaps it will fall off after twenty or thirty days, then treat the wound if you can.
et se tu ne pues, si la laisse.	and if you cannot, then leave it.
des brus qui vienent sor la sodure	forcibly applying bandages
Nous vienent maintes fois aprés la santeit de la briseure, meismement quant c’est pres de la jointure, et laide chose est a veoir li figure dou membre;	We often see after the health of the fractured bone, exactly where it is near the joint, and the ugly thing is to see the shape of the limb.
et par aventure ne puet faire li membres ses ovraiges naturelz.	and by chance cannot do its natural work.
Pren warde donques se li nous est fres:	Take then, since it is fresh:
si li aministre medicines stiptiques, si com aloes, encens, et mirre, et sarcocolle, acaice, et semblans autres, ensi que tu preignes aucune de ces choses, ou toutes ensamble, et les confit avec vin stiptique ou avec abun d’uef ou avec aisil;	if you administer styptics such as aloes, incense, and myrrh, and sarcocolla, acacia, and similar things, so that you do not use any of these, or all together, and mix them with stypic wine or with abundant blood or with vinegar;
et les met sus le nout en estoupes, et l’estraint bien, et ne la desliier en mains jors;	and place them on the nostrils, hold them tightly, and do not remove them from the hands for a long time.
et puis la desloie, et rencomence une autre, tant que li nodations soit ostee;	then dislocate it again, and start another one until the headache is gone;
ou tu estrain sus une piece de plonc bien faite;	or hold tightly a piece of wet clay well-shaped;
car li proprietez dou plonc si est qu’il oste toutes les enfleures desus les membres;	because the property of clay is that it removes all swellings from the limbs;
et se li nodation est ja convertie en durteit ausi com piere, et il est besoing de l’oster, si la cope desus, et fent la superfluiteit apparent;	and if the dislocation has hardened like a stone, and it is necessary to remove it, then cut off the top layer and make the excess apparent;
ou tu la reis a aucun raseur, tant qu’ele soit ostee, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee.	or you reset it with any tool until it is healed, and treat it until it is healthy.
dou membre qui est foibles aprés la garison	a weak limb that is after the garment
Quant li brisure de l’os est restoree, et demoure aprés li membres foibles et subtilz, si avient por mout de causes:	When the fracture of the bone is healed, and it remains afterwards with weak and fine members, there are many reasons:
de coi l’une est por ceu qu’il fut liiez trop estroit, et ne fut mie liiez si com il covenoit;	because one is due to the fact that it was tied too tightly, and was not loosened as it should have been;
ou por ceu qu’il i ot trop de liiens, et ne pooit venir li norrissemens au membre;	or because there were too many bandages, and could not come to the bones of the member;
ou por multitude d’arosement;	or due to the multitude of swelling;
ou por trop grans movements, ne mie en son houre;	or because of too great movements, and not enough rest in its hour;
ou por ceu qu’il a poc de sanc en son cors, si est foibles.	or because it has little blood in its body, so it is weak.
Et li cure si est que tu faices mengier le malaide, et faire le cors tendre, tant que li sans soit multipliiez en lui;	And the cure is that you make the pain less, and make the body supple, until the swelling is not multiplied in it;
et li aministre bain, et li done joie et liesce;	and the assistant bathes, and gives joy and relief;
puis met poix sus le membre, si que li poix atraie a li grant norrissement, et l’arose sovent d’aigue tede, tant que li norrissement corre au membre;	then puts clay on the limb, so that the clay attracts to the great swelling, and the heat often from high heat, until the swelling goes down in the limb;
et reviegne a sa figure natureil.	and returns to its natural shape.
dou membre tort aprés la santeit	a deformed limb after healing
Quant li membres est tors aprés la restauration, et li os brisiez apert, et li forme dou membre est laide, toutevoie ne pert mie son ovraige natureil:	When the limb is twisted after restoration, and the bones are broken open, and the shape of the limb is deformed, it does not at all keep its natural work:
si ne croire mie les folz qui dient c’on doit brisier lou membre tout de noveil, et maint fol mire ont ce fait en nostre terre;	if one does not believe the people who say that one should break the limb all at once, and many have done this in our land;
et cist ovraiges est blamez, et en vient grans malz, et par aventure li mors;	and this work is blamed, and it often causes great harm, and perhaps death.
toutevoie, se li nodations et li torture sont fres, si covient k’il soient arosez d’aigue chaude, ou herbes mollifians soient cuites, si com foilles de vismalve, et racines, et mellilote, et semblans choses;	Nevertheless, if the dislocations and torture are fresh, it is necessary that they be treated with hot water, or mollifying herbs cooked as follows: wormwood, roots, and meadowsweet, and similar things.
et li fai I emplaustre mollificatif, si com dyaquilon bien fait, et tu pren le muscillaige de vismalve, et la confit avec graisse de geline ou oile de sisament, et fai emplaustre sus;	and the softening poultice, such as made with diluted honey, and take the mustard seed of wormwood, and cook it with chicken fat or sesame oil, and make a poultice from it.
ou tu pren figues graisses, et les broie avec fien de colon, et semblans medicines que amenuisent le soudement.	or you take figs fat, and grind them with flour of coltsfoot, and similar medicines that soothe the pain.
Et aucune fois est ostee li nodacion por froter continuelment et longement a mains moistes.	And never is it necessary to apply continuous and prolonged pressure with wet hands to the dislocation.
Et soit amenistrez movement au membre chescune houre.	And allow movement to the limb every hour.
Et se li tortuositez est enveillie et endurcie, ausi com piere, et besoins est de l’oster au fer, si la covient coper jusc’a l’os, a l’incisoire subtil legierement;	And if the twisting is awakened and hardened, like stone, and it is necessary to remove it with iron, if it is covered just above the bone, with a slight incision.
et mettre cusenson et estude en la cure.	and apply a bandage and rest in the treatment.
Ci encomence li livres des dislocations	This begins the book of dislocations
Dislocations est issue d’aucune jointe de son leu, por coi il ne se puet muevre, et est li membres mal figurez, et sent li malaides grant dolor et grant lesion.	Dislocation occurs when a joint moves out of its place, which prevents it from moving, and the limb is misaligned, causing the patient great pain and injury.
Quant dislocation vient a aucun, si le covient maintenant ramener sens targier.	When dislocation comes to none, it must now be returned towards the shoulder.
Car s’on tarde, si enfle li leus, et par aventure si le remet on a poines au leu;	For if it delays, if the joint swells, and perhaps if it is reset to the bone;
por ceu ne covient mie c’on le mueve a l’oure k’il est enflez:	because then it does not matter that it moves at the time when it swells.
maintes fois fait venir spame et autres dolors;	many times it brings pain and other aches.
toutevoie, quant ce avenra, si fai sainier lou malaide, puis le laisse, tant que li apostemes chas soit apaisiez;	However, when it happens, if you make the dislocation straight, then let it be, until the abscesses are calmed.
puis arose le membre d’aigue chaude et d’oile, puis le ramoinne legierement, et cure chescun membre si com li cure venra en son leu.	Then raise the limb with hot and oiled cloths, then gently realign it, and treat each limb as it would be treated in its proper place.
Et j’ai ordenez les chapistres des dislocations des lou chief jusc’a piez.	And I have ordered the chapters on the dislocations of the shoulder down to the feet.
des mandibules	of the jawbone
Poc avient que les mandibules soient desaluees andous, et li dislocations d’ambedous est selonc II manieres:	It often happens that the jaws are dislocated backwards, and the dislocation of both is in two ways:
ou elles sont un poc ostees de lor leus, et mollifies un poc;	or they are slightly pushed out of their place and somewhat softened.
ou elles sont desaluees entierement, et pendent vers lou pis, et cort li salive de la bouche qu’il ne la puet tenir, ne ne puet clore sa bouche, et envoloupe sa langue avec la parole.	or they are completely dislocated and hang down to the side, and the saliva from the mouth flows out that it cannot hold it, nor can it close its mouth, and its tongue is wrapped with speech.
Quant li dislocations est petite, si revient par li em plusors disposicions.	When the dislocation is small, it returns in many positions.
Et s’elle est entiere et acomplie, si covient que tu la ramoinne hastanment, et ne targier mie;	And if she is whole and complete, it is necessary that you reset her quickly, and do not delay.
et en tel maniere que li ministres teigne le chief dou malaide, et boute li mires som pochet de l’une de ses mains en la racine de la dislocation de la mandibule dedens la bouche, se li dislocations est de II pars;	And in such a way that the minister wipes the bad part of the head, and puts the mirror some close to one of her hands at the root of the dislocation of the mandible inside the mouth, if the dislocation is of two parts.
et li autre doi des mains soient defuer, por mettre igal;	and the other hand should be free, to make it even.
et comande au malaide qu’il les amollisse, ses mandibules, et les mueve de toutes pars.	and command the bad part to soften its mandibles, and move them from all sides.
Et li mires la mete igal, tant qu’elle reveigne en son leu.	And when the joint is evenly aligned, it returns to its place.
Et se li ramener est griés, meismement se ce sont les II mandibules ensamble, si les arose d’aigue chaude et d’oile, tant que les ramoinnes legierement;	And if it is difficult to reset, immediately if they are both mandibles together, then raise them with hot and oil, until they are reset lightly.
ne ne targier mie dou ramener, si com nos avons dit.	do not delay in bringing it back, as we have said.
Et quant elles sont ramenees igalment, et li bouche dou malaide clot bien sens mollifiier, si met sus drapelz moilliez en cerote fait d’oile roset et de cire, puis le lie legierement de molz liiens;	And when they are returned evenly, and the jaw of the injury is well closed to soften, then place wet cloths made of a hardened mixture of red oil and wax on it, then lightly bandage it with moist bandages;
et dorme li malaides sus son dos, et ses chiés soit estans entre II cussins, si qu’il ne lou mueve ne a destre ne a senestre, ne ne s’efforce mie de maixier, mais preigne legiere viande, tant que les dolors soient ostees, et soient noees les mandibules;	and let the injuries lie on their backs, and their heads be between two pillows, so that they do not move to the left or right, nor make any effort to speak, but take light food until the pains are removed, and the jaws are healed;
et puis menjuce ce qu’il vuet legierement, et ne se travaille mie d’ovrir la bouche au mengier et au boivre, tant que li mandibule soit bien noee et sanee.	then gently clean what he wants lightly, and do not forcefully open the mouth for eating and drinking, until the jaw is well cleaned and healed.
Et se les II mandibules ne pueent estre remises a point a une houre, et ne sont mie converties a lor leus, si en vient fievres et sode acostumees, et par aventure solution de ventre, et par aventure vomist cole pure.	If the two jaws cannot be reset to their proper position within an hour and are not converted back to their original shape, then there comes fever and sweating as usual, and perhaps diarrhea, and perhaps vomiting of pure bile.
Et quant tu verras ceu, adonc saiches que c’est perdicions;	And when you see this, then cut it off, as it is deadly;
et maintes fois muert cil cui il avient, en VIIII jors.	and often death occurs to those who have it, in seven days.
de la forcelle	of the forceps
Li forcele ne puet desaluer dou costeit dedens la continuation de li et dou pis, et est desaluee aucune fois au defuer, et bien le sent on.	The forceps cannot be removed from the side of the body without cutting into it and the surrounding tissue, and it is not reset once dislocated, and one can feel it well.
Et li restauration si est que li malaides gise sovin sor son dos, et estende ses bras;	And the restoration is that the hairs lie quietly on his back, and extends his arms;
et puis presse le leu forment a ta palme, et elle revenra;	and then press the limb gently to your palm, and it will return.
puis met sus l’emplaustre et lou bendeil, et l’estraint;	then put on the plaster and bandage, and hold it in place;
et li chiez qui est devers lou coute ne puet desaluer;	and the question of those who are next to the neck cannot evacuate;
se poc non, et se il desalue aucune fois, si le ramoinne a son leu, si com nos avons dit;	if not, and if it ever resets itself, then reset it as we have said.
puis met sus l’emplaustre et le bendeil, et l’estraint, et coumande au malaide qu’il se repose tant qu’il soit sanez;	then place the poultice and bandage on it, and hold it in place, and command the patient to rest until they are healed.
et ensi meisme est ramenez li chiés de l’espale, quant il est desevrez de son leu.	and thus the same is returned to its place when it is reset from its joint.
de la dislocation de l’espaule	of the shoulder dislocation
Saiches que li espaule n’est desaluee fuer que selonc III manieres:	There are three ways in which the shoulder is not dislocated:
de coi l’une est qu’ele desalue a la partie de l’assele au desoz;	one is that it dislocates at the part of the shoulder blade on the outside;
et li seconde est a la partie dou pis;	and the second is at the worst part;
et par aventure desalue a la partie desus, et ceu avient poc;	and by chance dislocates to the upper part, and this happens rarely;
et ne desalue mie derrier por l’espaule, et ne desalue mie dedens por les ners;	and does not dislocate much behind for the shoulder, and does not dislocate much inward for the joints;
et plusors fois desalue desoz vers l’assele, meismement a ces qui ont poc de char, car a ces saut ele fuer hastanment;	and often dislocates outwards towards the shoulder blade, especially to those who have little fat, for these it is difficult;
a ces qui ont assez char, saut ele a poines, et rentre a poines.	to those who have enough fat, it goes straight and enters straight.
Et par aventure avient a aucuns homes percussion ou casseure, et enfle li espaule d’un aposteme chaut, et cuide qu’elle est desaluee par ceu.	And sometimes happens to some people, percussion or fracture, and inflames the shoulder with an abscess, and thinks it is dislocated by the bone.
Il covient donques que tu l’esprueves, tant que tu en soies certains;	Therefore, you must first examine to be sure;
et adonques encomence la cure.	and then begin the treatment.
Et est conue li dislocations quant il est aval vers l’assele, et met difference entre l’espaule malade et la saine, et tu troveras entre lor diversiteit manifeste;	And it is known that dislocations occur when they are turned towards the shoulder, and they differ between the sick shoulder and the healthy one, and you will find their difference manifest.
et troveras au chief de l’espaule une fosse, et desoz l’assele au tochier le chief de l’espaule, ausi com se ce soit uns oes;	And you will find at the top of the shoulder a hollow, and dislocated towards the armpit, the top of the shoulder, as if it were an elbow.
et ne puet li malaides ramener sa main a son neis, ne movoir de nulz movemens;	And it cannot move its arm to its side, nor move from any movement.
et ausi, s’elle est desaluee en haut, si n’est mie occultee, car tu le trueves manifestement au tochier;	And similarly, if it is dislocated above, if it is not hidden, for you will see it clearly in the armpit.
et ceste maniere de dislocation n’est mie fors a ramener, quant elle est novele, ou se li enfes est malaides.	And this manner of dislocation is not only to be reset, when it is new, or the pain is severe.
Et li maniere est que li ministres lieve la main dou malaide en haut, puis met tes peuchas desoz l’assele, et lieve la jointure a force en haut au leu;	And the manner is that the ministrants lift the hand of the misaligned shoulder upwards, then places their fingers below the acromion process, and resets the joint upwards at the shoulder.
et li ministres lieve la main, et l’estende en haut, pues le mette desoz;	And the ministrants lift the hand, and extend it upwards, then remove it.
si venra hastanment.	If it comes quickly.
Et s’elle ne vient si com nos avons dit em mains jors aprés, si covient ke li malaides soit baigniez en aigue chaude;	And if it does not come as we have said earlier, then it is necessary that the misaligned shoulder be bathed in hot water.
et li amenistre arosement mollifiant et assouajant, si com decoction de altee et de fenugrec et de mellilote en aigue, et soit amenistree;	And the ministrants apply heat and moisture, as with a decoction of poppy, fenugreek, and melilot in hot water, and it is applied.
puis soit sovinez li malaides sus son dos, et mette on desoz l’assele un sto de lainne igal, ne trop mol ne trop dur, puis mette li mires son talon sus le sto, et lieve le chief de l’espaule vertuousement, et traie la main dou malaide;	Then ensure the misaligned parts are on their backs, and place a cloth evenly across their buttocks, not too soft or too hard, then place the patient's foot on the cloth, and gently lift the shoulder with virtue, and pull the misaligned part.
et uns autres ministres teigne lou chief dou malaide, si qu’il ne se mueve aval;	and other ministers wash the head of the misaligned part, so it does not move back.
celle espaule revient tout maintenant, et se tu vues si le ramoinne selonc ceste maniere:	The shoulder is now completely healed, and if you see that it is reset in this manner:
et est que tu faices estre present I home qui soit plus grans que li malaides;	and make sure that there is a person who is larger than the misaligned part;
et soit drois devers lou costeit, et boute s’espaule desoz l’assele dou malaide, et lieve l’assele en haut, si que li malaides pende en l’ar;	and be on the right side of the ribs, and bring the shoulder away from the misaligned part, and lift it up, so that the misaligned part hangs in the arm.
et uns autres ministres traie la main dou malaide aval devers lou ventre.	And other ministers draw the hand downwards towards the belly.
Et se li malaides est trop legiers, si pent avec lui aucune chose pesant, et li dislocation revient maintenant.	And if the pain is too light, it can be moved with anything heavy, and the dislocation now returns.
Et le ramoinne on ausi en autre maniere:	And it is also reset in another way:
et est c’on fiche I lonc tison en terre, dont li chiés soit ausi reons com I pistal, et ne soit ne trop gros ne trop graile;	And it is done by placing a long, thin stick in the ground, which the patient should hold as if it were a spear, and it should not be too thick or too sharp;
puis soit mis desoz lou malaide, mais k’il ait drapelz souef sus, et li malaides soit estans dou lonc dou fust;	then it should be placed outside the injury, but with a soft cloth above, and the hairs of the forearm should be stretched out along the length of the arm;
puis soit estendue sa main aval d’autre part forment, et li jointure revenra en son leu hastanment;	then it should be extended downwards in the other direction, and the joint will return to its place quickly.
et s’elle ne vuet revenir por toutes ces choses que nos avons dit, si fai ceste cure:	and if she does not want to return for all these things that we have said, then do this treatment:
pren I tison de II bras de grant et IIII dois de large, qui ait le chief reont por mues entrer em parfont desoz l’assele, selonc ceste forme:	take a bandage of two arms in width and four fingers in length, which has the head facing downwards to enter through the opening behind the shoulder, in this form:
puis lie sus le chief dou fust drapelz souez, que li fust ne blece lou malaide, puis le met desoz l’assele dou malaide;	then tie the head of the soft cloth, which is not the cause of the bad pain, then put it away from the shoulder with the pain;
et estende som bras sus le fust dou lonc, et lie l’ajutoire sus le fust, et lou bras au chief de la main, puis met le bras sus I eschillon d’une eschiele dou large, et soit estendue li mains aval, et soit laissiez li cors pendans d’autre part:	and extend the arm over the long cloth, and tie the dislocation over the cloth, and the arm at the top of the hand, then put the arm over one of the blades of a knife, and let it be extended with the hands down, and leave the body hanging on the other side:
li jointure reva ens maintenant.	The joint is now open.
Et quant elle est ens, en quel maniere que ce soit, si covient que tu mettes desoz l’assele une spere de laine igal, puis met l’emplaustre aparilliet de poudre dou molin, avec encens et aubun d’uef, sus toute l’espaule et entor, puis l’estrain desoz l’assele avenanment, et torne le liien sus l’emplaustre, et embraice la main a son col, et soit li mains demorans ensi.	And when it is ready, in whatever way it is, then you must place a equal woolen ball away from the pain, then apply the poultice with flour from the mill, with incense and a little honey, over the whole shoulder and around, then remove the poultice away from the pain evenly, and return the limb to the poultice, and embrace the hand at its neck, and let the hands remain thus.
Et covient qu’il menjuce poc, tant que li membres soit confortez, car il sanera plus tost;	And it is best that he move slightly, until the limb is comfortable, as it will heal faster.
et puis menjuce plus aprés V jors ou VII, et le mueve;	Then move it again after three or four days, and move it.
et s’il est fermeis et il n’est mollifiez, si est sanez.	And if it is stiff and not made soft, it is healed.
Et se li jointure est fuer de leu por moistor que i est venue, ou por autre cause, si covient que tu i aministres cauteres a III pertus, si com il est mis devant ou chapistre des cauteres.	And if the joint is strong due to moisture that has come, or for another reason, it is necessary that you administer cautery at three points, as it is placed in front or in the chapter on cautery.
Et se tu fais tout ceu, et il deslie aprés VII jors, et li jointure ne se tient, et ne puet lever som bras amont, adonc saiches que li nerf au chief de l’espaule sont copeit ou estendut ou amollis;	And if you do all this, and it dislocates again after seven days, and the joint does not stay in place, and cannot be raised above the arm, then cut or stretch or soften the nerve at the top of the shoulder.
et saiches que li jointure n’iert jamais fichie en son leu.	And cut so that the joint never again dislocates in its place.
Li dislocation qui est devers lou pis, et les mameles, ou derrier, si est faite par impulsion, et estendement de mains, et i aministre on autre lieure;	The dislocation that occurs by the side of the hip and the buttocks, or behind, is caused by an impulse and extension of the hands, and it is treated with another ointment.
et cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat until they are healed.
Et se aprés la sanation vient grietez au membre, et tardemens em movement, si use li malaides bain maintes fois, tant que celle grietez soit alegie, et reviegne a sa premiere nature.	And if after healing the limb becomes swollen and moves slowly, then frequently apply the ointment until the swelling is alleviated, and returns to its original state.
de la dislocation dou coute	of the shoulder dislocation
Saiches que li jointure dou coute est desaluee a poinnes, et a poinnes revient;	Joints that are damaged at the shoulder return to their place and return.
et s’est desaluee de toutes pars, et meismement devant et derrier, et li dislocations n’est mie reponue, car on la voit bien et sent bien;	And it is dislocated from all parts, and even in front and behind, and the dislocation is not repaired, as one can see and feel.
et desalue selonc chescune figure.	It dislocates according to each shape.
Et quant tu joins le coute malaide avec lou sain, si le pues veoir apertement.	And when you join the misaligned ear with the healthy one, let the patient see clearly.
Car li jointure est chevee, et ne puet ploier lou bras, ne touchier son espaule a tout.	For the joint is sawn off, and it cannot bend the arm, nor touch its shoulder at all.
Et covient que tu le ramoinnes ainsois que apostemes chaus i viegne, car se apostemes chaus i venoit, si seroit grief li ramener;	And it is necessary that you reset it as soon as possible, because if it comes after the joint has moved, it would be painful to reset.
et par aventure ne puet estre ramenez dou tout en tout, meismement quant ele est au derrier;	And by chance, it cannot be reset at all, even when it is in the back.
si vaut pis que les autres dislocations, et est de plus grant dolor, et par aventure i vient li mors.	It is worse than other dislocations, and causes greater pain, and may even cause death.
Et li restauration si est, quant elle est telz c’on la puet ramener, que tu li estendes sa main a tes II mains;	And the resetting, when it is possible to put it back, is that you extend your hand to your two hands;
et ses bras soit espandus, et les mains dou mire selonc le coute entor, desor et desoz, et boute la jointure a ses peuchas ensamble, ou a la racine de sa palme, tant qu’ele reviegne a son leu.	and its arms are spread wide, and the hands on either side of the wrist, in and out, and press the joint at its base together, or at the root of its palm, until it returns to its place.
Et se li dislocations est au devant, si revient quant il double sa main a sa main, et fier de la racine de la palme lou coute qui est desaluez.	If the dislocation is in front, then it returns when he doubles his hand to his hand, and holds the root of the palm of the hand which is dislocated.
Et s’il ne vuet revenir au leu, si aministre fort extension;	And if it does not return to its place, then administer strong extension;
et est que dui ministre estendent le bras, et le teignent dui ministre, si qu’il ne se mueve a l’estension;	and it is that two assistants extend the arm, and hold it with two assistants, so that it does not move during extension.
puis torne le bras de chescune part, puis que tu as envoloupeit un drapeil double lonc et large;	then turn the arm from each side, then that you have wrapped a double cloth long and wide;
et quant li mires a jointe la jointure a sa main, si l’oigne d’aucun oile por amolir la jointure, puis boute la jointure forment, tant qu’ele reviegne;	and when the patient sees the joint at his hand, if there is no oil to soften the joint, then push the joint together, as much as it returns;
et quant elle est au leu, si met sus emplaustre sec avec aubun d’uef, et l’estrain forment, et pent le bras au col dou malaide, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le deslie.	and when it is in place, put on a dry poultice with some egg, and hold it together, and let the arm against the bad side, and leave it for some time, then remove it.
Et se li jointure est ferme en son leu, si deslie lou liien, et le laisse;	And if its joint is firm in its place, release the bone and leave it.
et se tu vois que li jointure n’estrigne bien, si rencomence l’emplaustre et lou lien, et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, tant qu’il soit fermement mis;	And if you see that the joint does not hold well, restart the bandage and the bone, and leave it in this way for some time, until it is firmly placed.
puis le deslie.	Then release it.
Et se il sent grieteit aprés le ramenement de la jointe, et elle se muet, si le baigne et frote bellement, et presse tant qu’il soit assouagiez;	And if it feels gritty after the resetting of the joint, and it moves, then bathe and rub it well, and press until it is relieved.
ou tu met sus la jointure une naige de mouton grasse, puis la laisse I jor et une nuit, puis l’oste, et lou fai entrer ou bain;	Or place a thick woolen cloth on the joint, then leave it for one day and one night, then open it and put in the bath.
et quant il sue, se li frote la jointure tempreement, puis remet la naige sus, et puis entre ou bain;	And when it pursues, rub the joint immediately, then put the limb back in place, and then give a warm bath.
et ensi fai II fois ou III, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And do this twice or three times until it is healed.
et se tu vues, si met sus fien de vaiche moiste chaufeit avec burre, et l’estrain sus;	And if you see, put above the wound a piece of warm, moist cloth with butter, and press it.
si revenra a sa disposition.	Then it will return to its proper position.
li dislocation de la main	the dislocation of the hand
Li jointure de la main desalue, et li revenue est legiere, plus que les autres jointures.	The joint of the hand is easily dislocated, and its return is lighter than other joints.
Toutevoie, il la covient ramener au leu hastanment, en l’oure meisme qu’ele est desaluee, ainsois que li leus soit enflez, ou qu’il i viegne aposteme chaut.	Nevertheless, it should be returned to its place immediately, in the same moment that it is dislocated, provided that the veins are inflated, or if there is an abscess forming.
Et li ramenemens si est que tu mettes la main malaide sus une tauble, et estende li ministres la main, et li mires la mette igal, ensi que il mette sa paume sus l’aparance de la jointure, et la boute tant qu’elle reviegne.	And when bringing back the shoulder, you place your hand on the table, and extend the minister's hand, and the mirror places it evenly, so that he places his palm on the appearance of the joint, and pushes until it returns.
Toutevoie, il covient que vos regardez s’il est bien a leu;	Nevertheless, you must check if it is properly set.
adonc mette li malaides lou dos de sa main sus une tauble a l’estension et au ramenement.	Then place the hand on the table for extension and repositioning.
Et se li dislocations est au dos de la main, si mette li malaides son dos de sa main sus la tauble, et li mires mette sa main sus cele apparance de la jointure.	If the dislocation is at the back of the hand, place the patient's back of their hand on the table, and the practitioner places their hand over the appearance of the joint.
S’elle revient maintenant, c’est bien.	If it returns now, it is good.
Se ce non, si l’estrain d’emplaustres apaisans apostemes chaus, et lou laisse ensi sens rencomencier.	If not, apply analgesic plasters and let it rest before trying again.
Et s’il ne le puet soffrir, et tu ne la pues mettre au leu aprés aucuns jors, si demore li jointure torte;	And if he cannot bear it, and you cannot put it back after some time, the joint will remain twisted.
et ne nuist niant au malaide fuer que tant que li mains est amoillie, et ne puet estraindre aucune chose a tout:	and do not apply force against the pain unless the hand is washed, and cannot hold anything at all:
adonc saiches que li nerf sont copez, ou li artere;	then cut the tendons or the artery;
si n’i a autre engien fuer que d’estraindre par cautere delez le cas, et par aventure n’i vaut autre chose.	if there is no other method but to burn with cauterization through the skin, and perhaps nothing else works.
Et quant li mains est au leu, si met sus l’emplaustre que nos avons dit, puis l’estrain et le laisse V jors, puis le deslie et laisse ensi.	And when the hand is dislocated, place the poultice that we have mentioned above, then strain and leave it for three days, then remove and leave it thus.
Et s’il ne la puet bien movoir, et il i a aucune grieteit, si la moille d’aigue chaude, et le frote tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if he cannot move it well, and there is no inflammation, then use hot vinegar, and rub it until it is healthy.
de la dislocation des dois de la main	of the dislocation of the two fingers
Aucune fois sont desaluez li doi de la main a chescune part, aucune fois au dos de la palme ou au ventre;	Never reset the two fingers of the hand at each part, never at the back of the palm or the belly;
adonques estent le doi, et boute la dislocation a tes pouchés tant qu’il reviegne, puis sostien lou chief dou doi, et le pent vers la partie ou il est desjoins;	therefore let the two fingers be, and push the dislocation into your pocket as long as it returns, then support the head of the finger, and bend it to the part where it is disjointed;
et le laisse II jors, et puis le met igal celui jor;	and let him wait two days, then set it straight that day.
et de nut le lie, si com nos avons dit, et lou deslie de jor, et lou fai movoir, et le relie la nut;	and apply a bandage as we have said, and remove the splint the next day, and move it, and reapply the bandage.
et fai ce sovent, tant qu’il soit estroit, et tout ausi fai, se il est desaluez au ventre de la main, et fai si com tu as fait ci devant, tant qu’il soit sanez;	and do this often, until it is straight, and also do the same if it is dislocated in the palm of the hand, and do as you have done before, until it is healed.
et tout ausi fai, quant il est desaluez d’autre part.	and do the same when it is dislocated elsewhere.
dou desaluement de l’eschinee dou dos	back pain from a dislocation of the spine
Quant l’eschinee dou dos ou dou col est desaluee, ou il en i a plusors desaluees, si n’i a point de cure, car li mors haste le malaide.	When the spine or neck is dislocated, and there are many dislocations, there is no cure, as the patient dies from the pain.
Et li signes si est que li egestions saut fuer sens volunteit, ne ne la puet tenir, et maintes fois sont mollifiez aucun membre, ou les II cuixes ou li dui bras ou I.	And the signs are that the dislocation jumps out of its place without volition, and cannot be held, and many times the member is softened, or both shoulders or the two arms or one.
Et maintes fois se muet li eschinee a IIII pars;	And often the jaw moves at four parts;
celle qui se muet au derrier si est apelee «gilbositez»:	that which moves at the back is called "gilbositez".
li cure si est que tu rewarde se li gilbositez est venue d’enfance:	The cure is that you reward if the gilbositez comes from childhood.
si n’i ait point de cure ne de sanation dou tot.	If there is no cure or healing until then.
Et celle que vient de cheoir ou de percussions ou de semblans choses, dirent li ancien manieres de cures par grans paroles, ou il n’a mie en toutes grant profit;	And that which comes from falling or from blows or similar things, the old methods of treatment by great words, or it does not have much benefit at all.
mais je l’ai abregiet selonc mon entention, et ai formez estrumens en diverses manieres.	But I have abbreviated according to my intention, and I have formed instruments in various ways.
Je dis que en la gilbositeit que vient au pis devant, nen a engien ne santeit;	I say that in the gilbosity that comes from the worst before, there is no skill or health;
et ausi cele que vient droitement en II costez, et ne puet on curer fuers que celi proprement qui vient au dos, si com je dis;	and also that which comes straight in the second rib, and one cannot cure it except by that proper one which comes from the back, as I said;
et est que li malaides soit estendus sus sa faice en I leu igal, et ait de l’estrain desoz lui, qu’il ne se blece;	and it is that the wounds should be stretched over its face in one even leg, and have some strain away from him, so that he does not bleed.
puis fiche I tison au chief en terre forment, et I autre as piez, et lie un liien pardesoz les asseles dou malaide, et I autre as hainches, et as genous, et as chevilles;	then put one bandage at the head in a firm way, and the other at the feet, and tie a bandage outside the wounds, and the other at the hips, and the other at the knees, and the other at the ankles.
et dui ministre saichent les liiens, li uns au chief et li autres as piez, parmi les II tisons;	and two ministers seek the bonds, one at the head and the other at the feet, among the two ties.
et soient bien fermez, li tison si com nos avons dit, et li mires mette ses paumes sus l’espinee forment, tant qu’ele reviegne.	and they should be well tied, the rope as we have said, and the mirror places its palms on the spine until it returns.
Et s’elle ne revient par ceste cure, si pren une tauble de III bras de lonc, et chevé desoz la paroit, et li malaides soit en costé, et boute le chief de la tauble desoz la paroit, puis met le mileu de la tauble sus l’espinee;	And if it does not return by this cure, take a table of three long arms, and bend it away from the pain, and the hairs should be on the side, and push the head of the table away from the pain, then place the middle of the table on the spine;
et mette li mires ses piez sus l’autre chief de la tauble, et presse bien, tant qu’il reviegne au leu;	and places the mirror its feet on the other head of the table, and presses well, until it returns to the place.
et se tu vues, si le fai au tornet qui torne a la main.	and if you see, do it to the one who returns to the hand.
Et est que tu fiches II tisons au chief dou malaide d’un bras de grant, et devers les piez II autres, et ait entre chescun tison, desoure et desoz, une paume d’espaice de lonc;	And place two bandages at the head of the misaligned arm, and on the other side of the feet, and between each bandage, outwards and inwards, a length of palm.
et ait en chescun tison I pertus, ou li tornet corre, et soient li tison fermement en terre, si qu’il ne se muevent;	and have in each bandage one hole, where the twisted part corrects, and the bandages are firmly pressed against the ground, so that they do not move.
et entre chescuns II tisons ait I tison tornant, sor coi li liien tornent, et ait en II tornans II petis tisons d’une paume de lonc, por torner le tornet;	and between each two bandages, have one bandage turning, along the direction of the twisted part, and have in the two turns two small bandages of a length of palm, to straighten the twisted part.
et puis lie lou lien qui est parmi les asseles au tornet devers le chief, et l’autre liien devers les piez a l’autre tornet, et chescuns des ministres torne son tornet a tout le liien, et li maistres mette l’espinee igal si com nos avons dit.	Then tie the ligament that is among the tendons towards the neck of the shoulder, and the other ligament towards the feet at the other end, and each minister turns their tendon to all the limb, and the masters put the spine evenly as we have said.
Et quant elle est igalz, si met sus emplaustre desiccatif avec abun d’uef, et puis les estoupes, et puis l’estele d’une tablete de III dois de lonc, que porpreigne lou leu de la gilbositeit et la partie de l’espondile sainne, puis le lie d’un liien, si com nos avons dit, et use li malaides de norrissement subtil, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when it is even, put above the drying plaster with abundant sulfur, then the stoope, and then the steel of a tablet of three fingers in length, which prevents the shoulder from gangrene and the part of the spine healthy, then the ligament of a ligament, as we have said, and use the subtle remedies of traction until they are healed;
et s’aucune chose vient en la fin de la santez, si covient aministrer medicines amollissans et asouajans, avec l’estele que nos avons dit ci devant;	and if nothing comes at the end of health, then one must administer remedies that are softening and soothing, with the aforementioned steel.
et aucune fois i aministre on une piece de plonc, et aucune fois vient li apparance en la derriere spondile dou dos, et cuide on que ce soit dislocations;	and one never administers a piece of lead, and it never appears in the back spine, and one is careful that this is not dislocation.
et c’est li os qui apert, por coi on n’i doit mie avoir presumption:	and it is the bones that open, which is why one should not have any presumption.
par aventure feroit venir la mort.	by chance it would bring death.
des dislocations de la hainche	of hip dislocations
Saiches que as jointures de la hainche et as jointures de l’espaule ne vient fuers que dislocacions soulement, ne n’i vient mie si com as autres jointures;	It is known that the joints of the waist and the joints of the shoulder come only from dislocations alone, not like other joints.
et li jointure de la hainche est desaluee selonc IIII parties:	and the joint of the waist is dislocated according to FOUR parts:
dedens et defuer ,et devant et derrier;	downward and backward, and front and back.
et plus dedens c’aillors, et poc desalue devant et derrier.	and more downward than before, and slightly dislocated in the front and back.
Et li conoissance de sa dislocations dedens si est que quant on joint la jambe malaide avec la sainne, si est plus longe, et apert plus li malaides genous que li sains, et ne puet li malaides doubler son genoil au feu;	And the knowledge of its dislocation downward is such that when the crooked leg is joined with the healthy one, it is longer and more open than the healthy ones, and cannot bend the knee at the fire.
et est li leus qui est delez enflez d’aposteme chaut, por ceu que li chiés de la cuixe vient lai.	and is the one that is on top inflamed with abscess, because the one who has the back comes down.
Et li signe de celui cui il vient au defuer, si est que cist accident sont contraire a ces devant.	And the sign of the one who comes after is that this accident is opposite to those before.
Et li signes de celui cui avient au devant, si est qu’il estent bien sa jambe selonc l’acomplissement;	And the signs of the one who has in front are that he is well aligned with the completion;
toutevoie, ne double mie le genoil sens dolor, et s’on le vuet faire aler, si ne puet avant, et retient son urine, et enfle li angre, et quant il vait, si passe sus le talon.	always, do not double the genu sens dolor, and if one wants to make it move, if it cannot go forward, and retains its urine, and swells the pain, and when it goes, it passes over the heel.
Et li signes de celui cui il avient derrier, si est qu’il ne puet espandre son genoil, ne doubler, et est celle jambe plus torte de l’autre, et li angre est mollifié, et est li chiés de la cuixe au leu desoz les costes.	And the signs of the one who comes after are that he cannot spread his groin, nor double over, and the other leg is more twisted than the other, and the anger is softened, and the head is dislocated from the neck outside the ribs.
Li ramenemens de ceste semblance de dislocation si est que tu rewarde se li dislocations est anciainne, et elle demore selonc sa disposition, si n’i a nule cure;	The return of this similar dislocation is that you wait for the dislocation to settle in its place, and it lasts according to its nature, if there is no treatment.
et n’i covient mie qu’il ait presumption.	and it does not matter if it has pride.
Et en celi dont li dislocation est fresche, et c’est des IIII manieres de dislocation, si te haste que tu tornes la jointe, et l’esten dedens et defuer, et la muef a destre et senestre;	And in this case where the dislocation is fresh, and it is of four kinds of dislocation, you must hurry to return the joint, and extend it inside and outside, and move it to the right and left.
par aventure si revenra, et n’a mestier d’autre cure.	If by chance it returns, and there is no need for other treatment.
Et s’il ne revient en ceste maniere, si covient que tu apareilles I ministre fort, et esten la jambe fort a II mains, ou a I liien que soit liiez sus lou genoil;	And if it does not return in this manner, then you must apply strong ministration, and strongly extend the leg at two joints, or at one joint that is connected to the thigh.
et uns autres ministres estende sa main desus en teil maniere qu’il boute ses mains desoz ses asseles, puis l’estrigne d’un souef liien sus la cuixe;	And other ministrations extend its hand above in a similar manner that it bites its hands from its shoulders, then strangle it with a soft rope connected to the neck.
et uns autres tigne lou chief dou liien;	And other ministrations tie the head of the limb.
et estendent amont et aval tuit a une fois, tant que li malaide soit levez de terre a une fois, et demoure pendans.	And extend above and below all at once, until the pain is lifted from the ground once and for all, and remains suspended.
Ceste maniere d’estension si est commune as IIII semblances, et se li dislocation est revenue, si com nos avons dit, c’est bien.	This method of extension is common for four similar cases, and if the dislocation has returned as we have said, it is good.
Se ceu non, si covient mettre cure a sa semblance.	If not, then you must put care to its appearance.
Quant li dislocations est au pardedens, si covient que tu sovines le malaide sus son costeit sain, puis met le liien sus la racine de la cuixe, et le leu qui est desoz l’angre, puis estent le liien en haut devers l’angre, et devers la forcele;	When the dislocation is in the shoulder, then you must support the misaligned part on its chest, then put the arm over the root of the armpit, and the arm that is out of the socket, then extend the arm upwards towards the shoulder, and towards the neck;
puis preigne uns autres ministres ses bras, et embraice le gros leu de la cuixe malaide, et l’estende au defuer forment:	then take other assistants to hold his arms, and grasp the large arm of the misaligned shoulder, and extend it behind in a proper form:
si revenra a son leu maintenant;	if it returns to its place now.
et ceste maniere de dislocation est plus legiere des autres.	and this method of dislocation is less severe than others.
Et se tu ne la pues serrer en ceste maniere que nos avons dit, si covient que tu lies les II piés dou malaide ensamble d’un fort liien souef sus les II talons, et sus les II genous, et soit li jambe malaide estendue II dois plus que li autres;	And if you cannot hold it in this manner as we have said, then it is necessary to tie the two affected feet together with a strong rope above the two heels, and above the two ankles, and let the affected leg be stretched out two fingers more than the other.
puis soit pendus sus le chief d’un fust, et soit en sus de terre II bras de lonc;	Then it should be hung from the top of a stick, and let the two arms hang down two feet long.
puis comande a I ministre qu’il embraice le chief de la cuixe, et soit uns autres ministres pendans avec le malaide, qui embraice forment la cuixe, car li jointure revient maintenant hastanment.	Then command the assistant to grasp the neck of the chicken, and let another assistants hang with the affected one, who grasps the neck firmly, for the joint is now beginning to heal.
Et quant li dislocations est au defuer, si gise li malaides, si com nos avons dit en celui qui a gilbositeit, et estraigne I liien sus la jambe malaide proprement, et sus le peis ausi;	When the dislocation is present, prick the hairs, as we have said in the case of gout, and stretch the joint properly above the affected leg, and also on the foot.
puis met II tisons, I au chief et I autre as piez, puis fiche I tison entre les cuixes au malaide emmi la forme;	Then put two bandages, one at the head and the other at the foot, then fold the bandage between the thighs over the affected area in shape.
et ait plantei de drapelz moistes entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide, puis estende chescuns ministre devers lui, et li mires mette igal a sa main la dislocation.	And place wet cloths around it, so that it does not dry out, then stretch each bandage towards him, and the hand puts the dislocation evenly in his hand.
S’elle revient, c’est boin.	If it returns, it is good.
Se ce non, met sus .ie. table, et le presse ensi com nos avons dit en la gilbositeit, et gise li malaides sus le sain costeit.	If not, place it on the flat surface, and press it as we have described in the previous chapter, and cut off the hairs on the healthy side.
Et quant li dislocations est devant, si covient estendre la jambe malaide hastanment, et selonc ce que j’ai dit;	And when the dislocation is in front, it is necessary to stretch the affected leg firmly, as I have said.
et mette li mires sa paine d’estre sus l’angre malaide, puis presse a l’autre main, et l’estent aval devers lou genoil.	and places the fingers in pain above the bad joint, then presses with the other hand, and stretches it down towards the chin.
Et se li dislocations est au defuer, si ne covient pas estendre le malaide aval, ne lever sus la terre, ains covient qu’il soit ausi com se li hainche estoit desaluee au defuer, si com nos avons dit dou couchement sus les II hainches;	And if the dislocation is in the shoulder, it does not need to be stretched downwards, nor lifted up towards the ground, but should be as it was when it was reset incorrectly before, as we have said about the position of the two shoulders;
et soit sus sa faice, et li lien estendut si com nos avons dit ci devant, et doit om presser sus la jointure a la table;	and should be above its face, and the arm stretched as we have said before, and one must press on the joint at the table;
et sera a point quant li malaides estendra ses jambes, et elles seront igalz;	and will be straight when the shoulders are stretched, and they will be even;
adonques ajoste les cuixes, et met l’emplaustre, et l’estrain d’un bendeil, si que li hainche ne se mueve;	Then, apply compresses to the elbows, and put on the ointment, and bind it with a bandage, so that it does not move.
et se repose III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie, et met l’emplaustre sus;	And rest it for three days or four, then reset it, and put on the ointment.
et se tu vois qu’elles soient igalz, si l’estrain, si com devant, et le laisse III jors;	And if you see that they are even, then bind it again as before, and leave it for three days.
puis le deslie, et lou fai aler belement, tant que li membres soit confortez.	Then reset it, and make the limb move well, until the limb is comfortable.
de la dislocation dou genoil	of the shoulder dislocation
Li genous est desaluez selonc III manieres:	The knees are dislocated in three ways:
c’est a savoir, dedens et defuer, et derrier;	That is to say, from the inside and outside, and behind.
et ne desalue point devant.	and do not dislocate again before.
Et li signes si est que tu comande au malaide qu’il plie sa jambe a sa cuixe, et s’ele ne s’aert a sa cuixe, saiches qu’il est desaluez;	And the sign is that you command the patient to bend their leg at the knee, and if they cannot do so at the knee, then it is dislocated.
et li restauration de toutes si est que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et estende sa jambe s’il puet, et li met ton dos sus sa faice, et met son piet sus tes piez;	And the restoration of all is that you make the patient sit upright, and extend their leg if they can, and put your back against their face, and put their foot on your feet.
puis pren son genoil a tes paumes, et retrai entre tes dois, puis plie les II costez dou genoil forment;	Then take their thigh in your palms, and pull it between your fingers, then bend the two sides of the thigh well.
et uns autres ministres estende son piet, tant que li genous reviegne a son leu, et li signes est qu’il aert bien sa jambe a sa cuixe legierement;	And other assistants extend their foot, until the knee returns to its place, and the sign is that they can lightly bend their knee.
et met l’emplastre sus, et fai aerdre la jambe a la cuixe, et les loie ensamble fort III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie;	and apply the plaster on top, and heat the leg at the thigh for three or four hours, then release it.
et ne se travaille mie li malaides d’aler, tant que li membres soit confortez.	and do not work with the painful parts until the limb is comfortable.
Et se li membres n’est a point, si aministre estendement fort, si com nos avons dit en la cure de la hainche, tant qu’il soit sanez	If the limb is not properly aligned, administer strong extension, as we have said in the treatment of the back, until it is healed.
de la dislocation dou talon	of the ankle dislocation
Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.	The ankles are never sprained and never fully dislocated, inside and outside.
Et li signes si est que li cheville est enflee, et tent avant a la partie ou elle est desaluee:	And the signs are that the joint is dislocated, and test first at the part where it is displaced:
li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.	the return is slight, and one should gently extend it to its hands when it is only slightly warmed.
Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne I ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville;	And when it is displaced quickly, one should then make the joint straight, and hold it with one hand above the leg, above the knee;
puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre II fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut;	Then grab the bone with your right hand, and then with your left hand twice, then extend it upwards, and strongly hit the bone upwards.
et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet;	Do this twice, as we have said, by pushing and pulling the bone;
s’elle revient, c’est bien;	If it returns, it is good.
se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient;	If not, start the work again, for it will return.
et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche I passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide;	And if it cannot return thus, lay the limb on its back on the ground, and firmly fix one needle between its thighs, and wrap bandages around it, so that it does not bleed.
puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a I liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet;	then the surgeons tie the wrist, and other surgeons extend the arm to its length or to the elbow, that they tie above the wrist.
puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent;	then each surgeon extends equally, and the splints are placed between the fingers to hold the dislocated finger when extending it.
puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	then the surgeons place the splints evenly on the dislocated joint, and other surgeons tie the sound leg at the ankle, and the dislocation will return quickly.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois;	And when it has not returned, apply the plaster and pour water over it, and let the bandage form, and tie the wrist to the leg, and hold the nerves that are above the ankle behind, so that the ligaments are not too tight.
puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain;	then leave it for two or three days, and if its joints are not healed, strain it.
puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors;	then reset it on the third or fourth day, and let it heal for four days.
et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	and if it goes before that time, then it is not certain that it will not dislocate again.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if an abscess comes, it is necessary to treat it as we have said elsewhere, until it is healed.
des dois	For the fire cautery, instruct
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	When the shoulders are dislocated, if they need to be extended, it is a simple matter.
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne;	And if the dislocation is in any part of the body, it is necessary that you make the patient sit with the injured limb straight out or on a table, and put your hand on what opens up from these joints, then press firmly on your hand until it returns;
et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie;	and when it is even and there is nothing open, put the back of your hand on a table at two fingers' breadth, then reset it firmly, and leave it for three days, then reset it.
et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and let him rest until he is healthy.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	of wounds and dislocations together
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert:	When a wound comes with the dislocation, and one wants to restore it, often times the pain kills:
si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis;	if not very presumptuous in the cure, if you are not wise in the art and have not used it for a long time, and if you are not merciful and slow, do not be harsh:
et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit;	and at the beginning of things, use calming methods for abscesses, and leave the pain in God's hands, if you do not see hope of health:
et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne;	and when you see hope, then reset the member to its place, as soon as the abscesses are gone:
et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis;	When the limb is set, administer things that soothe abscesses and cleanse the wound, as it should be, with dry dressings.
et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples;	And if the dislocation is fractured, and small bones are crushed, then remove the bones, and do as we have said in simple diseases.
et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	And guard against entering the path of fear, as I have said, for it is better for you according to your Creator, and for the knowledge of your armor and your body.
